### [1] [The dark fate of ultra-faint dwarfs: gravothermal collapse in action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04508)
*Moritz S. Fischer,Hai-Bo Yu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Ultra-faint dwarf (UFD) galaxies around the Milky Way exhibit diverse dark matter (DM) density profiles consistent with self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) models undergoing gravothermal collapse. High-resolution SIDM N-body simulations show that most UFDs have likely passed core expansion and are in the collapse phase, with their diversity explained by varying degrees of gravothermal evolution accelerated by tidal stripping. Large cross-sections of $σ/m_χ \approx 80\ \text{cm}^2\ \text{g}^{-1}$ at $v \approx 20\ \text{km s}^{-1}$ remain viable.
\n\n
银河系周围的超微弱矮星系（UFD）展现出多样的暗物质（DM）密度轮廓，这与经历引力热坍缩的自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型一致。高分辨率SIDM N-body模拟表明，大多数UFD已过核心膨胀阶段，正处于坍缩相，其多样性可由不同程度的引力热演化解释，而潮汐剥离加速了这一过程。在速度$v \approx 20\ \text{km s}^{-1}$下，大截面$σ/m_χ \approx 80\ \text{cm}^2\ \text{g}^{-1}$仍为合理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ultra-faint dwarf galaxies are the most DM-dominated systems known, making them ideal laboratories to test non-gravitational DM physics such as self-interactions. Observations of stellar kinematics in Milky Way UFDs reveal a diversity in inferred DM density profiles that cannot be easily explained by collisionless cold dark matter (CDM). The paper aims to assess whether self-interacting dark matter (SIDM), through gravothermal evolution of halos, can account for this observed diversity and determine the evolutionary stage of these halos.
\n\n
超微弱矮星系是目前已知暗物质占比最高的系统，因此是检验暗物质非引力物理（如自相互作用）的理想实验室。银河系UFD中恒星运动学观测揭示了推断出的暗物质密度轮廓具有多样性，这难以用无碰撞冷暗物质（CDM）模型解释。本文旨在评估自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）是否能通过晕的引力热演化解释这种多样性，并确定这些晕所处的演化阶段。

Method: The authors perform idealized high-resolution N-body simulations of self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) in a Milky Way-like host potential. These simulations model satellite halos undergoing gravothermal evolution, including effects of tidal stripping. They compare the resulting central DM densities and structural properties of simulated satellites with observational data from Milky Way ultra-faint dwarfs to infer the evolutionary stage (core expansion vs. gravothermal collapse) of each system.
\n\n
作者在类银河系宿主势场中进行了理想化的高分辨率自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）N-body模拟。这些模拟刻画了卫星晕经历的引力热演化，包括潮汐剥离效应。他们将模拟卫星的中心暗物质密度和结构特性与银河系超微弱矮星系的观测数据进行比较，以推断每个系统的演化阶段（核心膨胀 vs. 引力热坍缩）。

Result: The simulations show that SIDM halos evolve through core expansion followed by gravothermal collapse, producing a wide range of central DM densities. Most observed Milky Way UFDs align with halos in the collapse phase, implying their central densities are increasing over time. The degree of collapse varies significantly among satellites, and those with smaller pericentre distances (stronger tidal effects) tend to be more evolved. This supports large SIDM cross-sections of $σ/m_χ \approx 80\ \text{cm}^2\ \text{g}^{-1}$ at $v \approx 20\ \text{km s}^{-1}$ as consistent with observations.
\n\n
模拟显示，SIDM晕先经历核心膨胀，随后进入引力热坍缩，产生广泛的中心暗物质密度分布。大多数观测到的银河系UFD与处于坍缩相的晕相符，表明其中心密度随时间增加。不同卫星的坍缩程度差异显著，近心距较小（潮汐效应更强）的系统通常演化得更深入。这支持在$v \approx 20\ \text{km s}^{-1}$时，大截面$σ/m_χ \approx 80\ \text{cm}^2\ \text{g}^{-1}$与观测一致。

Conclusion: Self-interacting dark matter with a large cross-section can explain the observed diversity in dark matter densities of Milky Way ultra-faint dwarfs through gravothermal evolution. Most UFDs are likely in the post-core-collapse phase, with tidal interactions accelerating their evolution. This provides strong support for SIDM models and suggests that UFDs serve as powerful probes of dark matter microphysics.
\n\n
具有大截面的自相互作用暗物质可通过引力热演化解释银河系超微弱矮星系中观测到的暗物质密度多样性。大多数UFD可能处于核心坍缩之后的阶段，而潮汐相互作用加速了其演化。这为SIDM模型提供了有力支持，并表明UFD是探测暗物质微观物理的强大探针。

Abstract: Ultra-faint dwarf (UFD) galaxies are a promising probe for dark matter (DM) physics as they are the most DM-dominated systems known. The Milky Way (MW) hosts many UFDs for which the properties of their DM distribution have been inferred from measurements of their stellar kinematics. If DM has self-interactions beyond gravity, the UFD halos may undergo a gravothermal evolution, giving rise to a population of galaxies with more diverse DM density profiles. We investigate DM densities of MW UFDs in self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) models, with an aim of determining the stage of gravothermal evolution for their halos. Therefore, we employ idealised high-resolution SIDM N-body simulations targeted to a MW-like system and compare the properties of simulated satellites to those of the observed UFDs. We find that the gravothermal evolution of SIDM halos produces diverse DM distributions, aligning with observations of the MW UFDs. Most of the UFDs have high DM densities, indicating that their halos have passed the period of maximum core expansion and entered the collapse phase, i.e., their central density may increase with time. The depth to which they have evolved into the gravothermal collapse may vary strongly across the satellites. This allows SIDM to account for the diversity in their DM densities. Moreover, the acceleration of the gravothermal evolution by tidal stripping goes hand-in-hand with explaining the diversity of the UFDs, as the ones with smaller pericentre distances require having evolved further into the gravothermal catastrophe. Large SIDM cross-sections of $σ/ m_χ\approx$ 80 cm$^2$ g$^{-1}$ at a velocity of $v \approx$ 20 km s$^{-1}$ are plausible, as the halo densities of MW UFDs are consistent with the gravothermal evolution predicted in SIDM, with most of them being in the collapse phase.

</details>


### [2] [Beyond21: A Global Framework for Cosmic Dawn and Reionization Within and Beyond the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04542)
*Omer Zvi Katz*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Beyond21 is a fast, open-source Python package that self-consistently models Pop II/III star formation, radiation backgrounds, and their effects on the intergalactic medium to predict observables like the global 21-cm signal, UVLFs, ionization history, and CXB. It enables rapid parameter exploration and supports modular extensions, such as millicharged dark matter scenarios.
\n\n
Beyond21 是一个快速、开源的 Python 软件包，通过自洽地建模 Pop II/III 恒星形成、辐射背景及其对星系际介质（intergalactic medium）的影响，预测全局 21-cm 信号、UV 光度函数（UVLFs）、电离历史和宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）等可观测量。它支持快速参数探索，并具有模块化架构，可方便地扩展新物理，例如 millicharged dark matter 场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: With improving observations of the Cosmic Dawn (CD) and Epoch of Reionization (EoR), there is a growing need for unified theoretical frameworks that can consistently interpret multiple observational probes—such as the 21-cm signal, UV luminosity functions, and the cosmic X-ray background—within a single physical model. Existing tools often lack speed, modularity, or self-consistency across these diverse observables.
\n\n
随着对 Cosmic Dawn（CD）和 Epoch of Reionization（EoR）观测的不断改进，亟需统一的理论框架，能够在单一物理模型内自洽地解释多种观测探针——如 21-cm 信号、UV 光度函数（UVLFs）和宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）。现有工具往往在速度、模块化或跨多种可观测量的自洽性方面存在不足。

Method: Beyond21 implements a modular, physically motivated framework in Python that couples prescriptions for Pop II and Pop III star formation with radiative transfer and thermal evolution of the intergalactic medium. It computes the global 21-cm signal via the spin temperature evolution, derives UVLFs from galaxy formation models, tracks reionization through ionization fractions, and calculates contributions to the CXB from X-ray sources. The code is optimized for speed (∼0.1 s per run on one CPU core) and designed for easy modification of astrophysical assumptions. As a demonstration, the authors incorporate a millicharged dark matter component that cools baryons via elastic scattering.
\n\n
Beyond21 在 Python 中实现了一个模块化且物理动机明确的框架，将 Pop II 和 Pop III 恒星形成的模型与星系际介质的辐射转移和热演化相耦合。它通过自旋温度（spin temperature）演化计算全局 21-cm 信号，从星系形成模型导出 UV 光度函数（UVLFs），通过电离分数追踪再电离过程，并计算 X 射线源对宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）的贡献。该代码经过速度优化（单 CPU 核心上每次运行约 0.1 秒），并设计为便于修改天体物理假设。作为示例，作者引入了 millicharged dark matter 成分，其通过弹性散射冷却重子（baryons）。

Result: The Beyond21 pipeline successfully reproduces key observables—including the global 21-cm signal, UVLFs at high redshift, ionization history consistent with Planck constraints, and CXB contributions—within a single, self-consistent computation. It achieves this with exceptional computational efficiency (∼0.1 s per full run), enabling large-scale Bayesian inference or parameter scans. The inclusion of millicharged dark matter demonstrates the framework’s flexibility, showing how exotic physics can alter the 21-cm absorption trough via enhanced baryon cooling.
\n\n
Beyond21 流程在单一自洽计算中成功复现了关键可观测量——包括全局 21-cm 信号、高红移 UV 光度函数（UVLFs）、符合 Planck 约束的电离历史以及对宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）的贡献。其计算效率极高（每次完整运行约 0.1 秒），可支持大规模贝叶斯推断或参数扫描。通过引入 millicharged dark matter，展示了该框架的灵活性：这种新物理可通过增强重子冷却改变 21-cm 吸收谷的形态。

Conclusion: Beyond21 provides a fast, open, and modular platform for interpreting multi-messenger observations of the early universe. Its ability to jointly model diverse observables within a unified framework makes it a powerful tool for constraining both standard astrophysics and exotic physics—such as millicharged dark matter—using upcoming data from CD and EoR experiments.
\n\n
Beyond21 提供了一个快速、开源且模块化的平台，用于解释早期宇宙的多信使观测。其在统一框架内联合建模多种可观测量的能力，使其成为利用即将开展的 Cosmic Dawn（CD）和 Epoch of Reionization（EoR）实验数据约束标准天体物理和新物理（如 millicharged dark matter）的强大工具。

Abstract: Observations of the Cosmic Dawn (CD) and Epoch of Reionization (EoR) are steadily improving, opening new opportunities to study early galaxies through complementary probes. To enable consistent interpretation of these observations, we present Beyond21, a fully open-source Python package that implements flexible prescriptions for Pop II and Pop III star formation and computes the resulting radiation backgrounds and their impact on the intergalactic medium. From this coupled evolution, Beyond21 predicts the global 21-cm signal, UV luminosity functions (UVLFs), the ionization history, and the contribution to the observed cosmic X-ray background (CXB) within a single, self-consistent pipeline. A full global evolution run executes in $\sim0.1 \ {\rm s}$ on a single CPU core, enabling broad, high-resolution parameter exploration. The modular architecture facilitates straightforward modification of astrophysical prescriptions and the incorporation of new physics. As an illustrative example, we implement a scenario in which a small fraction of dark matter is millicharged, leading to baryon cooling through elastic interactions.

</details>


### [3] [Probing Dark Energy on the Moon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04841)
*Alfredo Gurrola,Robert J. Scherrer,Oem Trivedi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that a lunar laser interferometer can probe horizon-scale metric fluctuations to directly constrain the kinetic sector of the Effective Field Theory (EFT) of dark energy—specifically the operator coefficient $M_2^4$ and dark energy sound speed $c_s^2$—providing a new observational window beyond background expansion measurements.
\n\n
本文表明，月基激光干涉仪可通过探测视界尺度度规涨落，直接约束暗能量有效场论（EFT of dark energy）的动能部分——特别是算符系数 $M_2^4$ 和暗能量声速 $c_s^2$——从而提供超越背景膨胀历史的新观测窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current cosmological observations primarily constrain the background expansion history of the universe, leaving many operators in the EFT of cosmic acceleration—especially those governing scalar perturbations—poorly constrained. A new observational method is needed to test the microphysical consistency of dark energy and modified gravity models beyond the homogeneous background.
\n\n
当前宇宙学观测主要限制宇宙的背景膨胀历史，导致宇宙加速的有效场论（EFT of cosmic acceleration）中许多算符——尤其是控制标量扰动的那些——约束很弱。需要一种新的观测方法来检验暗能量和修改引力模型在均匀背景之外的微观物理自洽性。

Method: The authors propose using a lunar laser interferometer to measure horizon-scale metric fluctuations. These fluctuations encode information about the kinetic sector of the EFT of dark energy, particularly through the time evolution of scalar perturbations. The method links observable metric perturbations to the EFT operators $M_2^4$ and the associated sound speed $c_s^2 = \\frac{\\Omega}{M_2^4}$ (where $\\Omega$ is another EFT function), enabling direct constraints on these parameters.
\n\n
作者提出利用月基激光干涉仪测量视界尺度的度规涨落。这些涨落编码了暗能量有效场论（EFT of dark energy）动能部分的信息，特别是通过标量扰动的时间演化。该方法将可观测的度规扰动与EFT算符 $M_2^4$ 及其关联的声速 $c_s^2 = \\frac{\\Omega}{M_2^4}$（其中 $\\Omega$ 是另一个EFT函数）联系起来，从而对这些参数施加直接限制。

Result: The analysis shows that a lunar laser interferometer can achieve sensitivity to the EFT kinetic coefficient $M_2^4$ and the dark energy sound speed $c_s^2$, thereby probing previously inaccessible regions of the EFT parameter space. This provides a qualitatively new observational handle on the dynamics of scalar perturbations in dark energy models.
\n\n
分析表明，月基激光干涉仪可对EFT动能系数 $M_2^4$ 和暗能量声速 $c_s^2$ 达到灵敏度，从而探测此前无法触及的EFT参数空间区域。这为暗能量模型中标量扰动的动力学提供了质上全新的观测手段。

Conclusion: Lunar laser interferometry offers a novel and powerful probe of the microphysical structure of cosmic acceleration by directly accessing the kinetic operators in the EFT of dark energy. This approach complements traditional cosmological surveys and opens a new frontier in testing the theoretical consistency of late-time acceleration scenarios.
\n\n
月基激光干涉测量通过直接探测暗能量有效场论（EFT of dark energy）中的动能算符，为宇宙加速的微观物理结构提供了新颖而强大的探针。该方法补充了传统宇宙学巡天，并开启了检验晚期加速场景理论自洽性的新前沿。

Abstract: The effective field theory (EFT) of cosmic acceleration provides a model-independent framework for describing dark energy and modified gravity, yet many of its defining operators remain weakly constrained by existing observations. We show that measurements of horizon-scale metric fluctuations with a lunar laser interferometer can directly probe the kinetic sector of the EFT of dark energy, enabling constraints on operators governing scalar perturbation dynamics rather than only the background expansion history. In particular, we demonstrate sensitivity to the EFT kinetic coefficient $M_2^4$ and the associated sound speed of dark energy, $c_s^2$. This establishes a qualitatively new observational handle on the microphysical consistency conditions of late-time acceleration models, allowing broad regions of EFT parameter space to be probed, constrained, or potentially discovered.

</details>


### [4] [STOchastic LAttice Simulation of hybrid inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04850)
*Tomoaki Murata,Yuichiro Tada*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper studies the spatial profile of curvature perturbations in multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models using lattice simulations with the STOLAS code. It examines how the number of waterfall fields $n$ and inflaton potential shapes (Quadratic vs. Cubic) affect the probability distribution function (PDF), power spectra, and topological defect formation. The Cubic case shows a PDF upper bound that suppresses primordial black hole (PBH) formation. Using the Euler characteristic, the authors find that topological defects (domain walls, cosmic strings, monopoles) are fragmented into sub-Hubble structures during inflation due to stochastic noise, and only the $n=1$ case shows global features in the curvature perturbation.
\n\n
本文利用基于随机暴胀形式的格点模拟代码STOLAS，研究了多瀑布场混合暴胀模型中曲率扰动的空间分布。通过改变瀑布场数量$n$和暴胀子势的形式（“二次”与“三次”情形），分析了概率分布函数（PDF）、功率谱及拓扑缺陷的形成。三次势情形显示出PDF的上限特征，抑制了原初黑洞（PBH）的形成。作者采用欧拉示性数作为拓扑诊断工具，发现拓扑缺陷（如畴壁、宇宙弦、磁单极子）在暴胀期间被随机噪声碎裂为远小于哈勃尺度的精细结构；仅在$n=1$情形下，曲率扰动呈现出全局结构，这可能为早期宇宙物理提供新探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the rich phenomenology of multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models, which can generate diverse topological defects and non-Gaussian curvature perturbations relevant for primordial black hole (PBH) and large-scale structure formation. Understanding how stochastic dynamics during the waterfall phase transition shape the statistics and topology of these perturbations is crucial for connecting early-universe physics to observable signatures. Previous work hinted at a PDF cutoff in the Cubic potential that suppresses PBHs, warranting deeper investigation across different model parameters and topological configurations.
\n\n
动机源于多瀑布场混合暴胀模型丰富的现象学：该类模型可产生多种拓扑缺陷及非高斯曲率扰动，对原初黑洞（PBH）和大尺度结构形成具有重要意义。理解瀑布相变期间随机动力学如何塑造这些扰动的统计性质与拓扑结构，对于将早期宇宙物理与可观测信号联系起来至关重要。此前工作已指出三次势情形中PDF存在截断效应从而抑制PBH形成，因此有必要在不同模型参数和拓扑构型下进行更深入的研究。

Method: The authors employ the lattice simulation code STOLAS, which implements the stochastic formalism of inflation to evolve the coupled inflaton and waterfall fields on a 3D grid. They simulate six scenarios: combinations of $n = 1, 2, 3$ waterfall fields and two inflaton potentials (Quadratic: $V(\\phi) \\propto \\phi^2$; Cubic: $V(\\phi) \\propto \\phi^3$). Statistical properties—PDFs and power spectra—are computed and compared against predictions from the stochastic-$δN$ formalism. Additionally, the Euler characteristic is used as a topological diagnostic to quantify the geometry and connectivity of both the waterfall field configurations and the resulting curvature perturbation $\\zeta$.
\n\n
作者采用格点模拟代码STOLAS，该代码基于暴胀的随机形式，在三维网格上演化耦合的暴胀子场与瀑布场。他们模拟了六种情形：瀑布场数量$n = 1, 2, 3$与两种暴胀子势（二次势：$V(\\phi) \\propto \\phi^2$；三次势：$V(\\phi) \\propto \\phi^3$）的组合。计算了概率分布函数（PDF）和功率谱，并与随机-$δN$算法的预测进行对比。此外，使用欧拉示性数作为拓扑诊断工具，量化瀑布场构型及由此产生的曲率扰动$\\zeta$的几何与连通性。

Result: The simulations confirm that the PDFs and power spectra align with the stochastic-$δN$ prediction across all cases. The Cubic potential exhibits a sharp upper bound in the PDF, consistent with prior findings, which limits large-amplitude fluctuations and thus suppresses PBH formation. Topological analysis via the Euler characteristic reveals that domain walls ($n=1$), cosmic strings ($n=2$), and monopoles ($n=3$) do not persist as coherent super-Hubble structures; instead, stochastic noise fragments them into sub-Hubble scales during inflation. Only for $n=1$ does the curvature perturbation show global topological features, though their direct link to domain walls remains inconclusive since $n=2,3$ cases lack such signatures.
\n\n
模拟结果证实，所有情形下的PDF和功率谱均与随机-$δN$预测一致。三次势情形中PDF存在明显的上限，与先前结果一致，限制了大振幅涨落，从而抑制原初黑洞（PBH）形成。通过欧拉示性数的拓扑分析表明，畴壁（$n=1$）、宇宙弦（$n=2$）和磁单极子（$n=3$）并未以相干的超哈勃结构存留；相反，随机噪声在暴胀期间将其碎裂为亚哈勃尺度。仅在$n=1$情形下，曲率扰动呈现出全局拓扑特征，但由于$n=2,3$情形缺乏此类信号，尚无法确定该特征是否直接源于畴壁。

Conclusion: Multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models produce curvature perturbations whose statistical and topological properties are governed by stochastic dynamics during the waterfall transition. While the stochastic-$δN$ formalism successfully captures the one-point statistics, the Euler characteristic reveals unexpected sub-Hubble fragmentation of topological defects—contrary to standard expectations—and hints at global structures in $\\zeta$ for $n=1$. These findings suggest that the spatial morphology of primordial perturbations encodes information about the underlying field content and symmetry breaking pattern, offering a new observational window into early-universe physics beyond the power spectrum.
\n\n
多瀑布场混合暴胀模型所产生的曲率扰动，其统计与拓扑性质由瀑布相变期间的随机动力学主导。尽管随机-$δN$形式能成功描述单点统计量，但欧拉示性数揭示了拓扑缺陷出人意料地碎裂为亚哈勃结构（与标准预期相反），并在$n=1$情形下暗示了曲率扰动$\\zeta$的全局结构。这些结果表明，原初扰动的空间形态编码了底层场内容与对称性破缺模式的信息，为超越功率谱的早期宇宙物理提供了新的观测窗口。

Abstract: We investigate the spatial profile of the curvature perturbation generated in multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models, which are known to produce various topological defects. Using the lattice simulation code \acl{STOLAS}, based on the stochastic formalism of inflation, we analyse six cases by varying the number of waterfall fields $n$ and the functional form of the inflaton potential (``Quadratic'' and ``Cubic'' cases). Our statistical analysis shows that the \acp{PDF} and power spectra are broadly consistent with the so-called stochastic-$δN$ algorithm. The ``Cubic'' case also exhibits a characteristic upper bound in the \ac{PDF}, as discovered in our previous work, that suppresses \acl{PBH} formation while potentially affecting halo formation. Furthermore, we employ the Euler characteristic as a topological diagnostic tool to identify the structures of the waterfall fields as well as the curvature perturbation. We find that the topological defects, such as domain walls ($n=1$), cosmic strings ($n=2$), and monopoles ($n=3$), are reconnected during inflation into finer structures by the stochastic noise, making their correlation lengths much smaller than the Hubble scale at the critical point of the waterfall phase transition counterintuitively. The Euler characteristic also implies global structures of the curvature perturbation for $n=1$, though we do not conclude if they are due to the domain wall, because neither the strings ($n=2$) nor monopoles ($n=3$) leave such structures. The global structures of the curvature perturbation will provide a novel probe for the physics of the early universe.

</details>


### [5] [Sound Mode and Scale-Dependent Growth in Two-Fluid Dynamical Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05049)
*Frans van Die,Vincent Desjacques*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper studies dynamical dark energy (DDE) using a two-fluid model that permits the equation of state to cross the phantom divide, consistent with DESI observations. The DDE perturbations behave as sound waves, inducing scale-dependent effects in matter growth and halo bias. These effects are comparable in magnitude to those from massless neutrinos in $Λ$CDM for cluster-sized halos. A Fisher forecast shows that bispectrum data is crucial for detecting this scale dependence, especially for dark energy sound speeds $c_s^2 \sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$ in a survey volume of $V \sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$ at $z=0.5-1$. Very low sound speeds ($c_s^2 \sim 10^{-5}$) induce a gravitational drag on halos, biasing growth rate measurements by ~10%, while higher sound speeds ($c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$) may be accessible via optimal weighting to suppress shot noise.
\n\n
本文研究了使用双流体模型的dynamical dark energy (DDE)，该模型允许状态方程平滑穿越phantom divide，与DESI观测一致。DDE扰动表现为声波，在物质增长和halo bias中引入尺度依赖效应，其幅度与$Λ$CDM中无质量neutrinos对星系团尺度halos的影响相当。Fisher forecast表明，bispectrum信息对于探测这种尺度依赖至关重要，尤其当dark energy声速$c_s^2 \sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$、在体积为$V \sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$、红移$z=0.5-1$的巡天中。极低声速（$c_s^2 \sim 10^{-5}$）会在halos上产生gravitational drag，使growth rate测量偏移约10%；而较高声速（$c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$）可通过optimal weighting方案抑制shot noise来探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent observational results from DESI suggest that the dark energy equation of state may cross the phantom divide ($w = -1$), which cannot be described by a simple cosmological constant. This motivates the use of dynamical dark energy (DDE) models that allow for time-varying $w(z)$ and support perturbations. Understanding how such DDE perturbations affect cosmic structure formation—particularly through their sound-speed-dependent behavior—is essential for interpreting upcoming large-scale structure (LSS) surveys and distinguishing DDE from $Λ$CDM or other alternatives.
\n\n
近期DESI观测结果表明dark energy的状态方程可能穿越phantom divide（$w = -1$），这无法用简单的cosmological constant描述。这促使人们采用dynamical dark energy (DDE)模型，其允许状态方程$w(z)$随时间变化并支持扰动。理解此类DDE扰动如何通过其依赖于sound speed的行为影响宇宙结构形成，对于解读即将到来的large-scale structure (LSS)巡天数据、区分DDE与$Λ$CDM或其他替代理论至关重要。

Method: The authors employ a two-fluid effective description of dynamical dark energy, where each fluid has its own sound speed $c_s^2$, enabling the total equation of state to cross $w = -1$. They compute the impact of DDE perturbations—modeled as propagating sound waves—on the growth of matter density fluctuations and on halo bias. Using linear perturbation theory and a peak-background split approach, they derive the scale-dependent correction to halo bias induced by DDE sound modes. They then perform a Fisher matrix forecast for a multi-tracer analysis combining the galaxy power spectrum (P) and bispectrum (B) in a survey volume $V \sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$ at redshift $z = 0.5 - 1$, assessing detectability of the scale-dependent signal as a function of $c_s^2$.
\n\n
作者采用dynamical dark energy的双流体有效描述，其中每种流体具有各自的sound speed $c_s^2$，使总状态方程可穿越$w = -1$。他们计算了被建模为传播声波的DDE扰动对物质密度涨落增长和halo bias的影响。利用线性微扰理论和peak-background split方法，推导出由DDE声模引起的halo bias的尺度依赖修正。随后，他们在体积为$V \sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$、红移$z = 0.5 - 1$的巡天中，对多示踪（multi-tracer）分析结合galaxy power spectrum (P)和bispectrum (B)进行Fisher矩阵预测，评估尺度依赖信号对不同$c_s^2$值的可探测性。

Result: The scale-dependent halo bias induced by DDE sound modes is comparable in amplitude to that from massless neutrinos in $Λ$CDM for cluster-sized halos. A P-only analysis is insufficient to detect this effect; inclusion of the bispectrum (B) is essential. For $c_s^2 \sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$, a two-tracer P+B analysis can detect the scale dependence. At very low sound speeds ($c_s^2 \sim 10^{-5}$), DDE excitations exert a gravitational drag on halos, biasing inferred growth rates by ~10%. For higher sound speeds ($c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$), optimal weighting schemes that reduce shot noise and enhance effective bias could improve detectability.
\n\n
由DDE声模引起的尺度依赖halo bias在星系团尺度halos上的幅度与$Λ$CDM中无质量neutrinos产生的效应相当。仅使用power spectrum (P)的分析不足以探测该效应；必须包含bispectrum (B)。当$c_s^2 \sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$时，双示踪P+B分析可探测该尺度依赖性。在极低声速（$c_s^2 \sim 10^{-5}$）下，DDE激发对halos施加gravitational drag，使推断的growth rate偏移约10%。对于较高声速（$c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$），可通过optimal weighting方案降低shot noise并增强effective bias以提高可探测性。

Conclusion: Dynamical dark energy with non-negligible sound speed leaves distinct imprints on large-scale structure through scale-dependent modifications to halo bias and matter growth. These signatures are potentially detectable in next-generation LSS surveys using multi-tracer P+B analyses, especially when $c_s^2 \gtrsim 10^{-4}$. The work demonstrates that DDE is not only constrained by background expansion but also by its clustering properties, and that ignoring these effects could lead to biased estimates of cosmological parameters like the growth rate $f\sigma_8$.
\n\n
具有不可忽略sound speed的dynamical dark energy通过halo bias和物质增长的尺度依赖修正，在large-scale structure上留下独特印记。这些信号在下一代LSS巡天中，特别是当$c_s^2 \gtrsim 10^{-4}$时，有望通过多示踪P+B分析被探测到。本工作表明，DDE不仅受背景膨胀约束，也受其clustering性质约束；忽略这些效应可能导致对growth rate $f\sigma_8$等宇宙学参数的估计出现偏差。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of dynamical dark energy (DDE) on the growth of cosmic structure using a two-fluid model. This framework allows the dark energy equation of state to smoothly cross the phantom divide, in agreement with recent DESI results. In this effective description, DDE supports propagating perturbations that behave like sound waves. These perturbations induce a scale dependence in the growth of matter fluctuations and in halo bias, which can be exploited to test the dynamical nature of dark energy at the level of its fluctuations. For cluster-sized halos, the amplitude of the scale-dependent halo bias is comparable to that produced by massless neutrinos in $Λ$CDM. Using a Fisher forecast for a multi-tracer analysis of the power spectrum (P) and bispectrum (B) of galaxy number counts, we find that bispectrum information is essential to detect the scale dependence induced by the DDE sound mode. For a survey of volume $V\sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$ at redshift $z=0.5 - 1$, a two-tracer P+B analysis could detect this scale dependence if the sound speeds of the dark energy fluids are in the range $c_s^2\sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$. Lower sound speeds cause halos to experience a gravitational drag force through the excitations of sound waves. This effect impacts measurements of the growth rate inferred from cluster-sized halos at the 10\% level if one of the fluids has a very low sound speed $c_s^2\sim 10^{-5}$. Larger sound speeds $c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$ could be probed with optimal weighting schemes that reduce shot noise and increase the effective bias.

</details>


### [6] [Reassessing the SIGW Interpretation of PTA Signal: The Role of Third-Order Gravitational Waves and Implications for the PBH Overproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05191)
*Zhi-Chao Zhao,Sai Wang,Qing-Hua Zhu,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper proposes that including third-order scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) can enhance the SIGW spectrum enough to explain recent pulsar timing array (PTA) signals without overproducing primordial black holes (PBHs), thereby resolving a key theoretical tension. Constraints from CMB, BAO, and PTA data support this scenario, and the interpretation remains robust even when including astrophysical gravitational wave backgrounds from supermassive black hole binaries.
\n\n
本文提出，包含三阶标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）可显著增强SIGW谱，从而在不导致原初黑洞（PBHs）过量产生的前提下解释近期脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）信号，缓解关键理论张力。来自宇宙微波背景（CMB）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和PTA数据的联合约束支持该方案，且即使加入超大质量黑洞双星产生的天体物理引力波背景，该SIGW解释依然稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent interpretations of PTA signals as second-order scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) from early-universe curvature perturbations lead to excessive production of primordial black holes (PBHs), creating a theoretical inconsistency. The authors aim to resolve this tension by exploring higher-order (third-order) contributions to the SIGW spectrum, which could amplify the gravitational wave signal without requiring large scalar perturbations that overproduce PBHs.
\n\n
近期将脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）信号解释为早期宇宙曲率扰动产生的二阶标量诱导引力波（SIGWs），会导致原初黑洞（PBHs）过量产生，造成理论不自洽。作者旨在通过探索更高阶（三阶）对SIGW谱的贡献来缓解这一张力，因为高阶项可在不依赖过大标量扰动（从而避免PBH过产）的情况下放大引力波信号。

Method: The authors extend the standard second-order SIGW formalism to include third-order gravitational wave contributions. They compute the resulting enhancement in the spectral amplitude of the stochastic gravitational wave background. Using observational data from the cosmic microwave background (CMB) and baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), they place constraints on the energy density fraction $\\Omega_{\\rm GW}$ of cosmological gravitational waves. They then incorporate PTA data to constrain the peak frequency and amplitude of the SIGW spectrum. Additionally, they test the robustness of their interpretation by including a component from supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs) in the total gravitational wave background.
\n\n
作者将标准的二阶SIGW形式扩展至包含三阶引力波贡献，计算由此产生的随机引力波背景谱幅增强。利用宇宙微波背景（CMB）和重子声学振荡（BAO）观测数据，对宇宙学引力波的能量密度分数 $\\Omega_{\\rm GW}$ 施加限制；再结合PTA数据，约束SIGW谱的峰值频率与振幅。此外，他们通过在总引力波背景中加入超大质量黑洞双星（SMBHBs）成分，检验其解释的稳健性。

Result: The inclusion of third-order SIGWs significantly enhances the spectral amplitude, allowing the model to fit the PTA signal while evading stringent PBH overproduction constraints. Joint analysis of CMB, BAO, and PTA data identifies a viable parameter region where the SIGW interpretation is consistent with observations and alleviates the PBH problem. The conclusion remains valid even when an astrophysical foreground from SMBHBs is included, demonstrating the robustness of the cosmological SIGW explanation.
\n\n
引入三阶SIGWs显著增强了谱幅，使模型在拟合PTA信号的同时规避了严格的PBH过产限制。CMB、BAO与PTA数据的联合分析识别出一个可行参数区域，在该区域内SIGW解释与观测一致，并缓解了PBH问题。即使加入来自超大质量黑洞双星（SMBHBs）的天体物理前景成分，结论依然成立，表明宇宙学SIGW解释具有稳健性。

Conclusion: Third-order scalar-induced gravitational waves provide a theoretically consistent mechanism to explain the PTA signal without overproducing primordial black holes. This framework reconciles early-universe cosmology with current gravitational wave observations and is testable with future high-precision experiments.
\n\n
三阶标量诱导引力波提供了一种理论自洽的机制，可在不导致原初黑洞过量产生的前提下解释PTA信号。该框架调和了早期宇宙学与当前引力波观测之间的矛盾，并可通过未来高精度实验进行检验。

Abstract: In light of recent interpretations attributing pulsar timing array (PTA) signal to second-order gravitational waves induced by linear cosmological curvature perturbations in the early universe, the overproduction of primordial black holes (PBHs) poses a theoretical tension. In this work, we address this issue through extending such a scalar-induced gravitational wave (SIGW) framework to include third-order gravitational waves, which allow for a substantial enhancement in the spectral amplitude of SIGWs. Analyzing a combined dataset from cosmic microwave background and baryon acoustic oscillations, we derive cosmological constraints on the physical energy-density fraction of cosmological gravitational waves. Further incorporating PTA data, we obtain constraints on the spectral amplitude and peak frequency of SIGWs. Our results indicate that the parameter region favored by the data combination can to some extent alleviate the PBH overproduction problem, thereby supporting the theoretical consistency of our model. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our SIGW interpretation for the PTA signal by extending the analysis to include a gravitational wave background from supermassive black hole binaries. These findings are poised for further scrutiny with future high-precision observations.

### [7] [The Bayesian view of DESI DR2: Evidence and tension in a combined analysis with CMB and supernovae across cosmological models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05472)
*Dily Duan Yi Ong,David Yallup,Will Handley*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper reanalyzes DESI DR2 data within a fully Bayesian framework using nested sampling, comparing $Λ$CDM against seven extended cosmological models. It finds that Bayesian model selection (via evidence ratios and Ockham's razor) generally disfavors extensions, especially dynamical dark energy ($w_0w_a$CDM), unless the uncorrected DES-SN5YR supernova calibration is used—highlighting how hidden tensions in datasets can drive apparent evidence for new physics.
\n\n
本文在完全贝叶斯框架下利用嵌套采样重新分析DESI DR2数据，将$Λ$CDM与七个扩展宇宙学模型进行比较。研究发现，贝叶斯模型选择（通过证据比和奥卡姆剃刀）通常不支持扩展模型，尤其是动力学暗能量（$w_0w_a$CDM），除非使用未经修正的DES-SN5YR超新星定标——这突显了数据集中的隐藏张力如何驱动对新物理的表观证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to reassess claims of evidence for dynamical dark energy from the DESI collaboration using a rigorous Bayesian approach that accounts for model complexity via the Ockham penalty, which frequentist $Δχ^2$ methods neglect. The authors aim to determine whether apparent tensions or preferences for extended models are robust or artifacts of dataset inconsistencies or statistical methodology.
\n\n
动机在于使用严格的贝叶斯方法重新评估DESI合作组关于动力学暗能量的证据主张，该方法通过奥卡姆惩罚项考虑模型复杂性，而这是频率主义的$Δχ^2$方法所忽略的。作者旨在判断对扩展模型的明显偏好或张力是否稳健，抑或只是数据集不一致或统计方法的人为产物。

Method: The authors employ a fully Bayesian reanalysis using nested sampling (via PolyChord) to compute Bayesian evidences for $Λ$CDM and seven extended models. They combine DESI DR1/DR2 BAO data with Planck CMB, multiple supernova samples (including Pantheon+, Union3, DES-SN5YR, and the corrected DES-Dovekie), and DES-Y1 weak lensing. Model comparison is performed via Bayes factors ($\ln B$), and internal tensions are quantified using Bayesian tension metrics.
\n\n
作者采用完全贝叶斯重分析方法，利用嵌套采样（通过PolyChord）计算$Λ$CDM与七个扩展模型的贝叶斯证据。他们将DESI DR1/DR2 BAO数据与Planck CMB、多个超新星样本（包括Pantheon+、Union3、DES-SN5YR和已修正的DES-Dovekie）以及DES-Y1弱引力透镜数据相结合。模型比较通过贝叶斯因子（$\ln B$）进行，并使用贝叶斯张力度量量化内部张力。

Result: When using DESI DR2 BAO + Planck, the Bayesian evidence modestly favors $Λ$CDM over $w_0w_a$CDM ($\ln B = -0.57 \pm 0.26$), contradicting the DESI collaboration’s $3.1σ$ frequentist preference. Including the corrected DES-Dovekie SN data maintains this concordance ($\ln B = -0.01 \pm 0.27$). However, using the original DES-SN5YR calibration yields strong Bayesian support for $w_0w_a$CDM ($\ln B = +3.32 \pm 0.27$, equivalent to $3.07σ$), driven by a $2.95σ$ tension between DES-SN5YR and DESI DR2 within $Λ$CDM. This tension drops to $1.96σ$ after calibration correction, eliminating the evidence for dynamical dark energy.
\n\n
当使用DESI DR2 BAO + Planck时，贝叶斯证据略微支持$Λ$CDM而非$w_0w_a$CDM（$\ln B = -0.57 \pm 0.26$），与DESI合作组的$3.1σ$频率主义偏好相矛盾。加入修正后的DES-Dovekie超新星数据后，这一一致性得以维持（$\ln B = -0.01 \pm 0.27$）。然而，若使用原始DES-SN5YR定标，则贝叶斯证据强烈支持$w_0w_a$CDM（$\ln B = +3.32 \pm 0.27$，相当于$3.07σ$），其根源是DES-SN5YR与DESI DR2在$Λ$CDM内存在$2.95σ$张力。该张力在定标修正后降至$1.96σ$，从而消除了对动力学暗能量的证据。

Conclusion: The apparent evidence for dynamical dark energy in DESI analyses is not robust under Bayesian model selection and is highly sensitive to supernova calibration choices. The study underscores that unaccounted-for tensions between datasets—rather than genuine new physics—can drive spurious preferences for extended cosmological models. Correcting the DES-SN5YR calibration removes both the tension and the Bayesian evidence for $w_0w_a$CDM, reinforcing $Λ$CDM as the preferred model.
\n\n
DESI分析中动力学暗能量的表观证据在贝叶斯模型选择下并不稳健，且高度依赖于超新星定标的选择。本研究强调，数据集之间未被识别的张力（而非真实的新物理）可能驱动对扩展宇宙学模型的虚假偏好。修正DES-SN5YR定标后，张力与对$w_0w_a$CDM的贝叶斯证据同时消失，进一步巩固了$Λ$CDM作为优选模型的地位。

Abstract: We apply the unimpeded framework to perform a fully Bayesian reanalysis of the DESI DR2 data, using nested sampling with PolyChord to compute evidences for $Λ$CDM and seven extensions across combinations of DESI DR1/DR2, Planck CMB, supernovae (Pantheon+, Union3, DES-SN5YR, DES-Dovekie), and DES-Y1 weak lensing. The Bayesian Ockham's razor penalises extended models, yielding weaker or opposite preferences compared to $Δχ^2$-based analyses. For DESI DR2 BAO combined with Planck CMB alone, the DESI collaboration's $3.1σ$ frequentist preference for $w_0w_a$CDM is eliminated entirely: we obtain ${\ln B = -0.57{\scriptstyle\pm0.26}}$, modestly favouring $Λ$CDM. Adding the corrected DES-Dovekie supernova calibration maintains this concordance (${\ln B = -0.01{\scriptstyle\pm0.27}}$). However, when the original DES-SN5YR calibration is included instead, the DESI collaboration's $4.2σ$ result survives the Bayesian Ockham penalty as a $3.07{\scriptstyle\pm0.10}\,σ$ preference (${\ln B = +3.32{\scriptstyle\pm0.27}}$). That this signal persists despite the Ockham penalty makes the role of tension quantification essential: our analysis traced the preference to the DES-SN5YR calibration error, which introduced a $2.95{\scriptstyle\pm 0.04}\,σ$ conflict with DESI DR2 within $Λ$CDM -- a tension that stands out from the grid -- reduced to $1.96{\scriptstyle\pm 0.04}\,σ$ once the calibration was corrected. With the calibration corrected, the Bayesian evidence for dynamical dark energy vanishes.

</details>


### [8] [Crunching, Bouncing, and Cyclical Cosmologies from Dark Sector Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02332)
*Marcel van der Westhuizen,Amare Abebe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that strong non-gravitational interactions between dark matter and dark energy in flat FLRW cosmologies can lead to exotic background dynamics—specifically, a future Big Crunch or a past non-singular bounce—by allowing one dark-sector density to become negative, thereby violating standard energy conditions. Analytic conditions and closed-form expressions for the turnaround scale factors are derived, and a cyclic solution is shown possible in a closed universe.
\n\n
本文展示了在平坦FLRW宇宙学中，暗物质与暗能量之间的强非引力相互作用可通过使某一暗区域能量密度变为负值，从而违反标准能量条件，导致奇异的背景动力学行为——具体表现为未来的大挤压（Big Crunch）或过去的非奇异反弹（bounce）。作者推导了这些转向行为的解析条件，并给出了相应的最大或最小尺度因子的闭式表达式，同时指出在闭合宇宙中该模型可调谐为循环宇宙场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard cosmological models assume weak or negligible interactions between dark matter and dark energy, preserving positivity of energy densities and satisfying classical energy conditions. However, the full parameter space of interacting dark energy (IDE) models remains underexplored, especially regimes where energy transfer is strong enough to drive one component’s density negative. The authors aim to investigate whether such extreme but theoretically allowed IDE scenarios can produce non-standard global spacetime structures—like bounces or recollapses—in flat universes within general relativity, without invoking modified gravity or exotic matter fields.
\n\n
标准宇宙学模型通常假设暗物质与暗能量之间相互作用微弱或可忽略，从而保持能量密度为正并满足经典能量条件。然而，相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型的完整参数空间尚未被充分探索，特别是当能量转移足够强以致某一组分密度变为负值的情形。作者旨在研究此类极端但理论上允许的IDE情形是否能在广义相对论框架内、不引入修改引力或奇异物质场的前提下，在平坦宇宙中产生非标准的整体时空结构（如反弹或再坍缩）。

Method: The authors consider phenomenological IDE models with an interaction kernel $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$, where $Q$ quantifies the energy transfer rate from dark energy to dark matter. They analyze the Friedmann and continuity equations for a flat FLRW metric, allowing $ρ_{\rm dm}$ or $ρ_{\rm de}$ to become negative when the interaction persists through zero-density crossings. By examining the sign and magnitude of the total effective energy density and pressure, they derive conditions under which the Hubble parameter $H$ vanishes at finite scale factor $a$, signaling a turnaround (bounce or crunch). Closed-form solutions for the extremal scale factor $a_{\rm ext}$ are obtained by solving $H(a_{\rm ext}) = 0$. The analysis is extended to $k=+1$ (closed) universes to construct a cyclic model.
\n\n
作者考虑具有相互作用核 $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$ 的唯象IDE模型，其中 $Q$ 表征从暗能量到暗物质的能量转移速率。他们分析平坦FLRW度规下的Friedmann方程和连续性方程，允许在相互作用持续存在的情况下，$ρ_{\rm dm}$ 或 $ρ_{\rm de}$ 在穿越零密度时变为负值。通过考察总有效能量密度和压强的符号与大小，推导出Hubble参数 $H$ 在有限尺度因子 $a$ 处为零的条件，这标志着转向点（反弹或大挤压）。通过求解 $H(a_{\rm ext}) = 0$ 得到极值尺度因子 $a_{\rm ext}$ 的闭式解。该分析进一步推广至 $k=+1$（闭合）宇宙以构建循环模型。

Result: The study finds that in the strong interaction regime—where $δ_{\rm de} > 0$ and energy flows persistently from DE to DM—even in a spatially flat universe ($k=0$), the total energy density can become negative after one dark component crosses zero, violating the strong and null energy conditions. This enables: (i) a future Big Crunch if $H \to 0^+$ at some $a_{\rm max}$ followed by $H < 0$, or (ii) a past non-singular bounce if $H \to 0^-$ at some $a_{\rm min} > 0$ followed by expansion. Explicit analytic expressions for $a_{\rm max}$ and $a_{\rm min}$ are derived. In a closed universe ($k=+1$), tuning parameters yields a cyclic cosmology with alternating expansion and contraction phases.
\n\n
研究发现，在强相互作用区域（$δ_{\rm de} > 0$ 且能量持续从DE流向DM），即使在空间平坦宇宙（$k=0$）中，当某一暗组分密度穿越零后，总能量密度可变为负值，从而违反强能量条件和零能量条件。这使得：(i) 若在某 $a_{\rm max}$ 处 $H \to 0^+$ 随后 $H < 0$，则发生未来大挤压；(ii) 若在某 $a_{\rm min} > 0$ 处 $H \to 0^-$ 随后转为膨胀，则发生过去非奇异反弹。文中给出了 $a_{\rm max}$ 和 $a_{\rm min}$ 的显式解析表达式。在闭合宇宙（$k=+1$）中，通过参数调谐可实现交替膨胀与收缩的循环宇宙学。

Conclusion: While observationally disfavored due to conflicts with late-time cosmic acceleration and structure formation, these strong-interaction IDE scenarios demonstrate that exotic global spacetime geometries—such as bounces and crunches—can emerge naturally within general relativity using only standard dark sector components with non-gravitational couplings. This highlights the richness of the IDE parameter space and cautions against assuming energy density positivity without physical justification. The results also suggest that energy condition violations in dark sector interactions could serve as a mechanism for avoiding singularities or enabling cyclic cosmologies.
\n\n
尽管由于与晚期宇宙加速膨胀及结构形成观测相冲突而不太可能描述真实宇宙，但这些强相互作用IDE情形表明：仅通过标准暗区组分之间的非引力耦合，在广义相对论框架内即可自然产生奇异的整体时空几何（如反弹与大挤压）。这凸显了IDE参数空间的丰富性，并警示人们不应在缺乏物理依据的情况下默认能量密度为正。结果还表明，暗区相互作用中的能量条件破坏可作为避免奇点或实现循环宇宙学的一种机制。

Abstract: We present new mechanisms that produce either a future Big Crunch turnaround or a past non-singular bounce in flat FLRW cosmologies within general relativity at the background level, driven solely by non-gravitational interactions between dark matter (DM) and dark energy (DE). We study phenomenological interacting dark energy (IDE) models based on linear kernels of the form $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$, focusing on parameter regimes with strong energy transfer from dark energy to dark matter. In this strong interacting regime, the interaction does not vanish when one component crosses zero density, allowing one of the dark-sector densities to become negative. The resulting sign changes can violate the energy conditions required for cosmological turnarounds in a flat universe, thereby enabling either (i) a maximum scale factor followed by recollapse into a big crunch, or (ii) a minimum non-zero scale factor corresponding to a bounce. We derive analytic conditions for these turnarounds and obtain closed-form expressions for the associated maximum or minimum scale factor. We also show that, in a closed universe, a special case of the same IDE framework can be tuned to yield a cyclic scenario. Although these strong interaction scenarios are unlikely to describe the observed Universe, they provide a concrete demonstration that exotic cosmological behaviour can arise naturally in underexplored regions of the parameter space of familiar IDE models.

</details>

### [9] [Covariant canonical-spinor amplitudes for partial wave analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04487)
*Hong Huang,Yi-Ning Wang,Jiang-Hao Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper introduces a covariant orbital-spin ($LS$) decomposed amplitude using the massive spinor-helicity formalism, enabling Lorentz-covariant partial wave analysis without frame-dependent rotations. It validates this canonical-spinor method by reproducing consistent results with traditional approaches in the decay $Λ_c^+ \to Λπ^+π^0$.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于大质量旋量-螺旋度形式（massive spinor-helicity formalism）的协变轨道-自旋（$LS$）分解振幅，用于实现洛伦兹协变的部分波分析，无需依赖参考系的旋转。通过在衰变过程 $Λ_c^+ \to Λπ^+π^0$ 中验证，该规范旋量（canonical-spinor）方法与传统方法结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional partial wave analysis methods—such as the little group $LS$ decomposition and Zemach tensor approach—lack manifest Lorentz covariance or require cumbersome frame-dependent rotations, especially in cascade decays. The authors aim to construct a fully Lorentz-covariant $LS$-decomposed amplitude that intrinsically separates orbital and spin degrees of freedom while preserving $\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$ symmetry.
\n\n
传统的部分波分析方法（如小群 $LS$ 分解和Zemach张量方法）缺乏显式的洛伦兹协变性，或在级联衰变中需要繁琐的参考系相关旋转。作者旨在构建一个完全洛伦兹协变的 $LS$ 分解振幅，在保持 $\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$ 对称性的同时，内在地分离轨道角动量与自旋自由度。

Method: The authors employ the massive canonical-spinor variables within the spinor-helicity formalism to construct three-point amplitudes. By projecting all external particle little group indices onto a single little group space, they achieve an intrinsic $LS$ decomposition. The resulting amplitude is manifestly Lorentz covariant due to the spinor representation, enabling direct evaluation in any frame without additional alignment rotations. The method is implemented in the TF-PWA framework for practical amplitude analysis.
\n\n
作者采用旋量-螺旋度形式中的大质量规范旋量变量（massive canonical-spinor variables）来构造三点振幅。通过将所有外粒子的小群指标投影到单一小群空间，实现了内蕴的 $LS$ 分解。由于旋量表示天然具有洛伦兹协变性，所得振幅可在任意参考系中直接计算，无需额外对齐旋转。该方法已在TF-PWA框架中实现用于实际振幅分析。

Result: When applied to the decay $Λ_c^+ \to Λπ^+π^0$, the canonical-spinor amplitude yields fit results consistent with both the helicity formalism and the traditional $LS$ method. This demonstrates that the new covariant approach reproduces established physics while offering computational and conceptual advantages in multi-step decays.
\n\n
在衰变过程 $Λ_c^+ \to Λπ^+π^0$ 中应用该规范旋量振幅，其拟合结果与螺旋度形式和传统 $LS$ 方法一致。这表明新协变方法在保留已有物理结果的同时，在多步衰变中提供了计算和概念上的优势。

Conclusion: The canonical-spinor amplitude provides a practical, manifestly Lorentz-covariant framework for partial wave analysis in complex decay chains. It eliminates the need for frame-specific rotations and streamlines the treatment of cascade decays, making it a robust tool for modern amplitude analyses in high-energy physics.
\n\n
规范旋量振幅为复杂衰变链中的部分波分析提供了一个实用且显式洛伦兹协变的框架。它消除了对特定参考系旋转的需求，并简化了级联衰变的处理，成为高能物理中现代振幅分析的有力工具。

Abstract: We propose a covariant orbital-spin ($LS$) decomposed amplitude for the partial wave analysis using the massive spinor-helicity formalism. First we review the traditional-$LS$ method in the little group space and the Zemach tensor method in the double cover of the $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ space. To recover the $\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$ Lorentz covariance, several Lorentz covariant $LS$ tensors have been constructed in several different methods: covariant tensor, covariant projection tensor in pure-spin and general-spin schemes, but performing a intrinsic separation between $LS$ coupling while maintaining covariance is not obvious. We utilize the massive canonical-spinor variables to determine general three-point amplitudes, in which the spin-orbital decomposition is realized in single little group space by projecting little group indices of each particles into one, while the Lorentz covariance is ensured by the spinor form naturally. This covariant spinor method allows direct evaluation in any frame and a streamlined treatment of cascade decays within a single frame without additional alignment rotations in non-covariant treatment. As a benchmark, we implement the method in TF-PWA and analyze $Λ_c^+\toΛπ^+π^0$, finding consistent fit results across the helicity, traditional-$LS$, and canonical-spinor amplitudes. This validates the canonical-spinor amplitude as a practical tool for modern partial wave analyses of complex decay chains.

</details>


### [10] [Domain Walls from $Σ(36 \times 3)$, $Δ(54)$ and $Δ(27)$ potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04496)
*Gonçalo Barreto,Ivo de Medeiros Varzielas,Ye-Ling Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies degenerate vacua in scalar potentials invariant under the discrete flavor symmetry groups $Σ(36\times 3)$, $Δ(54)$, and $Δ(27)$ (with or without CP), for a triplet field representation. It classifies distinct Domain Walls connecting these vacua and computes their tensions.
\n\n
本文研究了在离散味对称群 $Σ(36\times 3)$、$Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$（含或不含 CP 对称性）下不变的标量势中出现的简并真空，考虑的是这些对称群的三重态表示。文章对连接这些简并真空的不同 Domain Walls 进行了分类，并计算了相应的张力（tension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the vacuum structure of scalar potentials with non-Abelian discrete flavor symmetries is crucial for model building in particle physics, especially in contexts where spontaneous symmetry breaking leads to topological defects like Domain Walls. The symmetries $Σ(36\times 3)$, $Δ(54)$, and $Δ(27)$ are known to yield predictive flavor structures; however, their vacuum manifolds can possess multiple degenerate minima, potentially giving rise to cosmologically problematic Domain Walls. Classifying these walls and computing their tensions helps assess their physical viability and implications.
\n\n
理解具有非阿贝尔离散味对称性的标量势的真空结构对于粒子物理中的模型构建至关重要，尤其是在自发对称性破缺导致拓扑缺陷（如 Domain Walls）的情形下。对称群 $Σ(36\times 3)$、$Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$ 能够产生具有预言能力的味结构；然而，其真空流形可能存在多个简并极小值，从而可能产生宇宙学上有问题的 Domain Walls。对这些墙进行分类并计算其张力有助于评估其物理可行性和相关影响。

Method: The authors analyze the scalar potential for a complex triplet field $\\phi = (\\phi_1, \\phi_2, \\phi_3)^T$ invariant under $Σ(36\\times 3)$ or its subgroups $Δ(54)$ and $Δ(27)$. They identify all degenerate global minima by solving the minimization conditions of the potential. Using group-theoretical arguments and explicit parameter scans, they determine the set of physically distinct vacua. Domain Walls are then constructed as static, planar solutions interpolating between pairs of such minima. The wall tension $\\sigma$ is computed via the standard formula $\\sigma = \\int_{-\\infty}^{\\infty} dz \\left[ \\frac{1}{2} \\left( \\frac{d\\phi}{dz} \\right)^2 + V(\\phi) - V_{\\text{min}} \\right]$, where $z$ is the coordinate perpendicular to the wall.
\n\n
作者分析了一个复三重态场 $\\phi = (\\phi_1, \\phi_2, \\phi_3)^T$ 的标量势，该势在 $Σ(36\\times 3)$ 或其子群 $Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$ 下不变。他们通过求解势的极小化条件，找出所有简并的全局极小值。利用群论论证和显式的参数扫描，确定了一组物理上不同的真空。随后，Domain Walls 被构造为在这样一对真空之间插值的静态平面解。墙张力 $\\sigma$ 通过标准公式 $\\sigma = \\int_{-\\infty}^{\\infty} dz \\left[ \\frac{1}{2} \\left( \\frac{d\\phi}{dz} \\right)^2 + V(\\phi) - V_{\\text{min}} \\right]$ 计算，其中 $z$ 是垂直于墙的坐标。

Result: The paper identifies all distinct sets of degenerate minima for each symmetry case (with and without CP). It finds that the number and nature of Domain Walls depend sensitively on the imposed symmetry and whether CP is conserved. Explicit expressions for the tensions of all physically inequivalent Domain Walls are derived, revealing hierarchies among them based on the underlying group structure and potential parameters.
\n\n
本文识别出每种对称情形（含或不含 CP）下所有不同的简并极小值集合。研究发现，Domain Walls 的数量和性质强烈依赖于所施加的对称性以及 CP 是否守恒。作者推导出了所有物理上不等价的 Domain Walls 张力的显式表达式，并揭示了这些张力根据底层群结构和势参数所呈现的层级结构。

Conclusion: The classification and tension calculation of Domain Walls in models based on $Σ(36\\times 3)$, $Δ(54)$, and $Δ(27)$ provide essential input for assessing their cosmological stability and compatibility with observations. The results indicate that certain symmetry-breaking patterns may lead to long-lived or stable Domain Walls, which could be cosmologically dangerous unless additional mechanisms (e.g., bias terms or inflationary dilution) are invoked.
\n\n
基于 $Σ(36\\times 3)$、$Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$ 的模型中 Domain Walls 的分类及其张力计算，为评估其宇宙学稳定性及与观测的兼容性提供了关键输入。结果表明，某些对称性破缺模式可能导致长寿命甚至稳定的 Domain Walls，除非引入额外机制（例如偏置项或暴胀稀释），否则可能带来宇宙学危险。

Abstract: We consider the degenerate minima arising from scalar potentials invariant under $Σ(36\times 3)$, or under its subgroups $Δ(54)$ and $Δ(27)$ (with or without imposed CP symmetries), for a triplet of those symmetries. In this framework, we classify the distinct Domain Walls between the degenerate minima and calculate the respective tensions.

</details>


### [11] [Momentum fraction and hard scale dependence of double parton scattering in heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04510)
*Joao Vitor C. Lovato,Edgar Huayra,Emmanuel G. de Oliveira*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper extends previous studies of Double Parton Scattering (DPS) from proton--proton to heavy--ion ($pA$ and $AA$) collisions, incorporating nuclear effects like shadowing and antishadowing. It proposes a model for the transverse parton distribution in nuclei, hypothesizes that partons in bound nucleons are more spatially separated than in free protons, computes the effective cross section for $p$Pb data with reasonable agreement, and predicts that DPS in heavy--ion collisions can probe both nucleon and nuclear transverse structure.
\n\n
本文将此前关于双部分子散射（Double Parton Scattering, DPS）在质子-质子碰撞中的研究扩展至重离子（$pA$ 和 $AA$）碰撞，纳入了相关运动学区域内的核效应（如遮蔽效应和反遮蔽效应）。文章提出了一个原子核横向部分子分布的简单模型，并假设束缚核子内部的部分子比自由质子中的部分子空间分离更广。作者计算了 $p$Pb 数据的有效截面，结果与实验数据合理吻合，并预测重离子碰撞中的 DPS 可用于探测自由质子与束缚核子的横向结构（主要在 $pA$ 碰撞中），以及原子核的横向结构（主要在 $AA$ 碰撞中）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand how nuclear modifications—specifically shadowing and antishadowing—affect Double Parton Scattering observables in heavy--ion collisions. Since DPS is sensitive to both longitudinal and transverse parton correlations, extending prior proton--proton analyses to nuclear environments offers a novel probe of nucleon and nuclear structure, particularly their transverse spatial profiles, which are not easily accessible through other processes.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于需要理解核修正效应（特别是遮蔽效应和反遮蔽效应）如何影响重离子碰撞中的双部分子散射（DPS）观测量。由于 DPS 对纵向和横向部分子关联均敏感，将此前在质子-质子碰撞中的分析推广到核环境中，为探测核子与原子核的横向空间结构（这些结构难以通过其他过程获得）提供了一种新手段。

Method: The authors extend their earlier framework for DPS in $pp$ collisions to $pA$ and $AA$ collisions by incorporating nuclear-modified parton distribution functions (nPDFs) that account for shadowing and antishadowing. They introduce a simple model for the transverse parton distribution in nuclei, assuming that partons within a bound nucleon have a broader spatial separation than in a free proton. The effective cross section $\sigma_{\\text{eff}}$ is computed using these modified distributions and compared with existing $p$Pb LHC data; predictions are made for future measurements.
\n\n
作者通过引入考虑遮蔽和反遮蔽效应的核修正部分子分布函数（nPDFs），将其先前用于 $pp$ 碰撞的 DPS 框架推广至 $pA$ 和 $AA$ 碰撞。他们提出了一个原子核中横向部分子分布的简单模型，假设束缚核子内的部分子比自由质子中的具有更广的空间分离。利用这些修正后的分布计算有效截面 $\sigma_{\\text{eff}}$，并与现有的 $p$Pb LHC 数据进行比较，并对未来测量做出预测。

Result: The computed effective cross section for $p$Pb collisions shows reasonable agreement with available LHC data. The predictions exhibit a clear dependence on final--state kinematics, indicating sensitivity to the transverse partonic structure. In $pA$ collisions, DPS primarily probes the transverse profile of the free proton versus the bound nucleon, while in $AA$ collisions it is more sensitive to the overall transverse nuclear geometry.
\n\n
所计算的 $p$Pb 碰撞有效截面与现有 LHC 数据表现出合理的一致性。预测结果显示出对末态运动学的明显依赖性，表明其对横向部分子结构具有敏感性。在 $pA$ 碰撞中，DPS 主要用于探测自由质子与束缚核子的横向轮廓；而在 $AA$ 碰撞中，则更敏感于原子核整体的横向几何结构。

Conclusion: DPS in heavy--ion collisions serves as a promising tool to investigate the transverse spatial structure of both individual nucleons (free vs. bound) and entire nuclei. The observed agreement with $p$Pb data validates the proposed modeling of nuclear effects and transverse parton distributions, supporting the use of DPS as a structural probe in future high--energy nuclear collision experiments at the LHC.
\n\n
重离子碰撞中的双部分子散射（DPS）是研究单个核子（自由态与束缚态）及整个原子核横向空间结构的一种有力工具。与 $p$Pb 数据的合理吻合验证了所提出的核效应和横向部分子分布模型，支持在未来 LHC 高能核碰撞实验中将 DPS 用作结构探针。

Abstract: In a previous work, we studied the momentum fraction and hard--scale dependence of double parton scattering (DPS) in proton--proton collisions and the resulting dependence of the effective cross section on the final--state observables. In this paper, we extend those results to heavy--ion ($pA$ and $AA$) collisions, accounting for nuclear effects in the relevant kinematic region, namely shadowing and antishadowing. In addition to modifying the longitudinal parton distributions, these effects also alter the transverse parton distribution of the nucleus, for which we propose a simple model. We further hypothesize that partons inside a bound nucleon are more widely separated than in a free proton. We compute the effective cross section for the available $p$Pb data, obtaining reasonable agreement, and provide predictions for future measurements at the LHC. The observed dependence of our predictions on the final state indicates that DPS in heavy--ion collisions can be used to probe the transverse profile of the free proton and the bound nucleon, primarily in $pA$ collisions, as well as the transverse structure of the nucleus, mainly in $AA$ collisions.

</details>


### [12] [Improved supernova bounds on CP-even scalars: cooling and decay constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04513)
*Melissa Joseph,Samuel Liebersbach,Anirudhan A. Madathil,Gustavo Marques-Tavares*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper significantly tightens constraints on MeV-scale CP-even scalars that mix with the Higgs boson by combining updated supernova cooling arguments with new decay-based astrophysical bounds from the 511 keV galactic positron line and energy deposition in Type II-P supernovae, reaching mixing angles as small as $\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$—surpassing collider limits by over five orders of magnitude. The analysis is extended to hadrophilic scalar models, constraining nucleon Yukawa couplings down to $y_N \sim 10^{-10}$. Together, astrophysical and collider probes now cover more than nine orders of magnitude in coupling for such light scalar models.
\n\n
本文通过结合更新的超新星冷却论证与来自银河系511 keV正电子谱线和II-P型超新星低能能量沉积的新衰变型天体物理约束，显著收紧了对MeV质量尺度下与Higgs玻色子混合的CP偶标量的限制，达到混合角小至$\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$，比现有对撞机限制强五个数量级以上。分析还扩展到hadrophilic标量模型，将核子Yukawa耦合限制到$y_N \sim 10^{-10}$。天体物理与对撞机探针共同覆盖了此类轻标量模型超过九个数量级的耦合参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Laboratory experiments lose sensitivity to weakly-coupled new particles in the MeV mass range, creating a gap in experimental coverage. Supernovae, due to their high temperatures and densities, serve as powerful natural laboratories for probing such particles. The motivation is to exploit astrophysical phenomena—particularly supernova dynamics and associated emissions—to constrain light scalar particles that could be relevant for dark matter or other beyond-Standard Model physics, especially where terrestrial experiments cannot reach.
\n\n
实验室实验在MeV质量范围内对弱耦合新粒子的灵敏度下降，导致探测空白。超新星因其高温高密环境，可作为探测此类粒子的强大天然实验室。本文旨在利用天体物理现象——特别是超新星动力学及相关辐射——来约束可能与暗物质或其他超出标准模型（BSM）物理相关的轻标量粒子，尤其是在地面实验无法触及的参数区域。

Method: The authors combine three complementary methods: (1) an improved calculation of scalar production via nucleon bremsstrahlung in supernova cores, leading to a refined cooling argument; (2) a decay-based constraint from the observed galactic 511 keV positron flux, assuming scalars decay into $e^+e^-$ pairs; and (3) limits from energy deposition in low-energy Type II-P supernovae, where late-time scalar decays would inject extra energy and alter light curves. They also generalize the analysis to a hadrophilic scalar model where the scalar couples preferentially to nucleons via Yukawa interactions, using similar astrophysical channels to constrain $y_N$.
\n\n
作者结合三种互补方法：(1) 改进超新星核心中通过核子轫致辐射产生标量粒子的计算，从而优化冷却约束；(2) 利用观测到的银河系511 keV正电子流量，假设标量粒子衰变为$e^+e^-$对，建立基于衰变的限制；(3) 利用低光度II-P型超新星的光变曲线，其中晚期标量衰变注入额外能量会改变光变行为，从而设限。作者还将分析推广到hadrophilic标量模型，其中标量通过Yukawa相互作用优先耦合到核子，并使用类似天体物理通道约束$y_N$。

Result: The combined constraints exclude CP-even Higgs-mixed scalars with masses in the MeV range for mixing angles as small as $\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$, improving previous supernova cooling bounds by over an order of magnitude and surpassing collider limits by more than five orders of magnitude. For hadrophilic scalars, nucleon Yukawa couplings are constrained down to $y_N \sim 10^{-10}$. These results cover a vast region of parameter space that is theoretically motivated by dark matter models involving light mediators.
\n\n
综合约束排除了MeV质量范围内的CP偶Higgs混合标量，其混合角小至$\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$，比此前超新星冷却限制提升一个数量级以上，并比对撞机限制强五个数量级以上。对于hadrophilic标量，核子Yukawa耦合被限制到$y_N \sim 10^{-10}$。这些结果覆盖了由涉及轻媒介子的暗物质模型所理论驱动的大片参数空间。

Conclusion: Astrophysical probes—particularly from supernovae and galactic positron observations—provide unparalleled sensitivity to very weakly coupled MeV-scale scalars, far exceeding the reach of current colliders. When combined with laboratory experiments, they enable comprehensive coverage over more than nine orders of magnitude in coupling strength. This synergy underscores the critical role of multi-messenger astrophysics in testing well-motivated extensions of the Standard Model, especially in regimes inaccessible to terrestrial experiments.
\n\n
天体物理探针——尤其是来自超新星和银河系正电子观测的数据——对极弱耦合的MeV尺度标量粒子提供了无与伦比的灵敏度，远超当前对撞机的探测能力。与实验室实验结合后，可在耦合强度上实现超过九个数量级的全面覆盖。这种协同效应凸显了多信使天体物理在检验标准模型合理扩展中的关键作用，特别是在地面实验无法触及的参数区域。

Abstract: Supernovae provide among the most powerful probes of weakly-coupled new particles in the MeV mass range, where laboratory experiments lose sensitivity. In this work, we derive improved supernova constraints on CP-even scalars mixing with the Higgs boson, combining an updated production rate calculation, which improves the cooling bound by more than an order of magnitude, with new decay-based constraints from the galactic 511~keV positron flux and energy deposition in low-energy Type~II-P supernovae. Together, these constraints probe mixing angles as small as $\sinθ\sim 10^{-9}$, more than five orders of magnitude below existing collider bounds. We also extend our analysis to a hadrophilic scalar model, constraining Yukawa couplings down to $y_N \sim 10^{-10}$. Our results demonstrate that the combination of astrophysical and collider probes covers over nine orders of magnitude in coupling for these classes of models, probing a large region of parameter space motivated by dark matter considerations.

</details>


### [13] [50 Years of SUSY and SUGRA, circa 1974-2024, and Future Prospects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04664)
*Pran Nath*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This article reviews the historical development and interdisciplinary impact of supersymmetry (SUSY), supergravity (SUGRA), and their connection to superstring theory from circa 1974 to 2024, emphasizing their roles in particle physics unification, cosmology, and experimental searches.
\n\n
本文回顾了自约1974年至2024年间supersymmetry（SUSY）、supergravity（SUGRA）及其与superstring理论联系的历史发展和跨学科影响，强调它们在粒子物理统一、宇宙学及实验搜寻中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to synthesize five decades of theoretical and experimental progress stemming from SUSY and SUGRA, highlighting how these frameworks have unified particle physics with cosmology and string theory, and motivated extensive experimental efforts to test their predictions.
\n\n
动机在于综合SUSY和SUGRA所引发的五十年理论与实验进展，突出这些框架如何将粒子物理与宇宙学及string theory统一起来，并推动了对其预言的大规模实验检验。

Method: The paper adopts a historical and conceptual review methodology, tracing key theoretical milestones—such as the emergence of SUSY, gauge supersymmetry, supergravity, gravity-mediated SUSY breaking, and supergravity grand unification—and their implications for inflation, dark matter, dark energy, and experimental physics.
\n\n
本文采用历史与概念综述的方法，追溯关键理论里程碑——如SUSY的提出、gauge supersymmetry、supergravity、gravity-mediated SUSY breaking以及supergravity grand unification——并分析它们对inflation、dark matter、dark energy和实验物理的影响。

Result: The review demonstrates that SUSY and SUGRA have profoundly shaped modern theoretical physics by bridging high-energy particle physics, early-universe cosmology, and string theory, while also driving decades of experimental searches across colliders, precision tests, and astrophysical observations—even in the absence of direct discovery.
\n\n
综述表明，SUSY和SUGRA通过连接高能粒子物理、早期宇宙cosmology和string theory，深刻塑造了现代理论物理，并推动了数十年来在对撞机、精密实验和天体物理观测中的搜寻工作——即便尚未有直接发现。

Conclusion: Although SUSY and SUGRA remain experimentally unconfirmed, their theoretical elegance and capacity to address fundamental problems (e.g., hierarchy problem, dark matter, unification) have cemented their role as pivotal frameworks linking particle physics, cosmology, and quantum gravity via superstrings.
\n\n
尽管SUSY和SUGRA尚未被实验证实，但其理论优雅性及解决基本问题（如hierarchy problem、dark matter、unification）的能力，已使其成为通过superstrings连接粒子物理、宇宙学和量子引力的关键框架。

Abstract: The development in the early seventies of supersymmetry, in the mid-seventies of gauge supersymmetry and supergravity, and in the early eighties of gravity mediated breaking of supersymmetry and of supergravity grand unification have led to remarkable progress in the pursuit of unification of fundamental interactions of particle physics. They have also led to the intertwining of particle physics, cosmology, and strings. Since supersymmetry and supergravity are manifest in the low energy limit of superstring below the Planck scale, experimental test of them are of interest regarding the validity of the superstring itself. For that reason, over the past decades, after the advent of supersymmetry and SUGRA models, there have been sustained experimental searches for supersymmetry at colliders, in precision experiments, and in astrophysical and cosmological data. The SUSY and SUGRA models have also had deep impact on theories related to inflation, dark matter, and dark energy. The purpose of this article is to provide a view from the bridge of these developments over the past fifty years circa 1974-2024.
