### [14] [The effect of charm quark on the QCD chiral phase diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04728)
*Fei Gao,Yuepeng Guan,Shinya Matsuzaki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This work investigates how the inclusion of dynamical charm quarks affects the chiral phase structure of QCD, particularly the location of the critical endpoint (CEP), using the miniDSE approach to Dyson-Schwinger equations. It finds a 2–3% shift of the CEP to lower chemical potential, indicating non-negligible heavy-flavor effects.
\n\n
本文利用 Dyson-Schwinger 方程的 miniDSE 方法，研究了动力学 charm 夸克对 QCD 手征相结构（特别是临界端点 CEP 位置）的影响。结果表明 CEP 向较低化学势方向移动约 2–3%，说明重味动力学效应不可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the QCD phase diagram, especially the location and existence of the critical endpoint (CEP), is a central goal in strong-interaction physics. Most prior studies have focused on light ($u$, $d$) and strange ($s$) quarks, often neglecting heavier flavors like charm. However, as lattice QCD and effective models improve, it becomes necessary to assess whether heavy-flavor dynamics—despite their large mass—can subtly influence chiral symmetry restoration and the CEP. This motivates a systematic study of $2+1+1$ flavor QCD versus $2+1$ flavor QCD using a nonperturbative framework.
\n\n
理解 QCD 相图，尤其是临界端点（CEP）的位置和存在性，是强相互作用物理的核心目标。以往研究多集中于轻夸克（$u$, $d$）和奇异夸克（$s$），常忽略 charm 等重味夸克。然而，随着格点 QCD 和有效模型的发展，有必要评估重味动力学——尽管其质量较大——是否对手征对称性恢复和 CEP 产生微妙影响。这促使作者在非微扰框架下系统比较 $2+1+1$ 味 QCD 与 $2+1$ 味 QCD。

Method: The authors employ the miniDSE (minimal Dyson-Schwinger equation) scheme, a recently developed approximation to the full Dyson-Schwinger equations (DSEs) that retains key nonperturbative features while being computationally tractable. They compute the quark propagator for both $2+1$ (up, down, strange) and $2+1+1$ (adding charm) flavor QCD across finite temperature and chemical potential. The chiral condensate and its susceptibility are extracted to locate the pseudo-critical temperature and the CEP. The charm quark is treated as a fully dynamical degree of freedom, not integrated out, allowing its back-reaction on the gluon and light-quark sectors to be captured.
\n\n
作者采用 miniDSE（minimal Dyson-Schwinger equation）方案——一种新近发展的 Dyson-Schwinger 方程（DSEs）近似方法，在保持关键非微扰特征的同时具备计算可行性。他们计算了 $2+1$ 味（上、下、奇异夸克）和 $2+1+1$ 味（加入 charm 夸克）QCD 在有限温度和化学势下的夸克传播子。通过提取手征凝聚及其 susceptibilities 来确定赝临界温度和 CEP。charm 夸克被作为完全动力学自由度处理（而非被积分掉），从而捕捉其对胶子和轻夸克扇区的反作用。

Result: Including the charm quark as a dynamical flavor shifts the critical endpoint to lower baryon chemical potential by approximately 2–3%, while leaving the overall topology of the phase diagram qualitatively unchanged. This demonstrates that even heavy quarks with masses well above the QCD scale ($m_c \\gg \\Lambda_{\\text{QCD}}$) can exert a measurable influence on chiral phase transitions through quantum fluctuations and screening effects.
\n\n
将 charm 夸克作为动力学味包含进来，会使临界端点向更低的重子化学势方向移动约 2–3%，而相图的整体拓扑结构在定性上保持不变。这表明，即使质量远高于 QCD 能标（$m_c \\gg \\Lambda_{\\text{QCD}}$）的重夸克，也能通过量子涨落和屏蔽效应对手征相变产生可测量的影响。

Conclusion: Heavy-flavor contributions, though small, are non-negligible in precision studies of the QCD phase diagram, particularly near the critical endpoint. Future theoretical efforts aiming to locate the CEP—whether via DSEs, functional renormalization group, or lattice QCD—should incorporate dynamical charm quarks to avoid systematic biases. The miniDSE framework proves effective for such multi-flavor explorations.
\n\n
重味贡献虽小，但在 QCD 相图（尤其是临界端点附近）的精密研究中不可忽略。未来旨在定位 CEP 的理论工作——无论是通过 DSEs、泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）还是格点 QCD——都应包含动力学 charm 夸克以避免系统性偏差。miniDSE 框架在此类多味探索中被证明是有效的。

Abstract: We study the influence of charm quark dynamics on the chiral phase structure of Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) using the recently developed miniDSE scheme of the Dyson-Schwinger equations. By calculating the quark propagator in $2+1$ and $2+1+1$ flavor QCD, we quantify the impact of including the charm quark as a dynamical degree of freedom on the QCD phase diagram. Our results show that the charm quark induces a moderate but noticeable shift to lower chemical potential in the location of the critical endpoint (CEP) by approximately 2-3%. The result in this work indicates that the heavy-flavor dynamics can subtly influence the QCD phase structure and should be taken into account in particular for searching the CEP of QCD.

</details>


### [15] [Exploring Nucleon Structure and the Proton Mass Problem through Holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04794)
*Jiali Deng,Defu Hou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a unified parameterization framework based on Light-Front Holographic QCD (LFHQCD) to simultaneously extract quark and gluon generalized parton distributions (GPDs), from which parton distribution functions (PDFs) and gravitational form factors (GFFs) are derived. It further uses gauge/string duality to analyze near-threshold $J/ψ$ production and quantifies the trace anomaly’s contribution to the proton mass as $\sim 23\%$, consistent with experimental and lattice QCD data.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于光前全息QCD（Light-Front Holographic QCD, LFHQCD）的统一参数化框架，用于同时提取夸克和胶子的广义部分子分布（GPDs），并由此导出部分子分布函数（PDFs）和引力形状因子（GFFs）。进一步利用规范/弦对偶分析近阈值$J/ψ$产生过程，量化了迹反常对质子质量的贡献约为$\sim 23\%$，结果与实验和格点QCD数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the absence of a unified theoretical framework that consistently connects quark and gluon generalized parton distributions (GPDs) with parton distribution functions (PDFs), gravitational form factors (GFFs), and the proton mass decomposition—particularly the role of the QCD trace anomaly. Existing approaches often treat these quantities separately, limiting a coherent understanding of proton structure within quantum chromodynamics (QCD).
\n\n
该研究的动机源于缺乏一个统一的理论框架，能够一致地关联夸克和胶子的广义部分子分布（GPDs）与部分子分布函数（PDFs）、引力形状因子（GFFs）以及质子质量分解——特别是QCD迹反常的作用。现有方法通常将这些量分开处理，限制了对量子色动力学（QCD）中质子结构的连贯理解。

Method: The authors employ a parameterization method grounded in Light-Front Holographic QCD (LFHQCD) to model quark GPDs using electromagnetic form factor constraints. From these GPDs, they extract both quark PDFs and gravitational form factors (GFFs). The approach is extended to gluon GPDs by imposing consistency with soft Pomeron behavior. Additionally, they use gauge/string duality (AdS/QCD correspondence) to compute near-threshold $J/ψ$ photoproduction cross-sections as a probe of the trace anomaly, linking the $t$-dependence of the cross-section to the gluonic energy-momentum tensor form factor.
\n\n
作者采用基于光前全息QCD（LFHQCD）的参数化方法，利用电磁形状因子约束构建夸克GPDs，并从中提取夸克PDFs和引力形状因子（GFFs）。该方法通过要求与软Pomeron行为一致，推广至胶子GPDs。此外，他们利用规范/弦对偶（AdS/QCD对应）计算近阈值$J/ψ$光致产生截面，以此作为迹反常的探针，将截面的$t$依赖性与胶子能量-动量张量形状因子联系起来。

Result: The extracted quark and gluon GPDs yield PDFs and GFFs consistent with experimental data and lattice QCD. The gluon GPD model reproduces the expected soft Pomeron behavior. The analysis of near-threshold $J/ψ$ production yields a trace anomaly contribution to the proton mass of approximately $23\%$, with the predicted $t$-dependence of the differential cross-section matching experimental measurements from GlueX and other collaborations.
\n\n
所提取的夸克和胶子GPDs导出的PDFs和GFFs与实验数据及格点QCD一致。胶子GPD模型成功复现了预期的软Pomeron行为。对近阈值$J/ψ$产生的分析表明，迹反常对质子质量的贡献约为$23\%$，且微分截面的$t$依赖性预测与GlueX等实验组的测量结果相符。

Conclusion: This work establishes a coherent framework unifying quark and gluon GPDs, PDFs, and GFFs within Light-Front Holographic QCD, and provides direct phenomenological evidence for the significant role of the QCD trace anomaly in generating proton mass. It bridges non-perturbative QCD modeling with experimental observables, advancing our understanding of proton structure and mass decomposition.
\n\n
本工作在光前全息QCD框架内建立了统一描述夸克和胶子GPDs、PDFs与GFFs的自洽框架，并为QCD迹反常在质子质量生成中的重要作用提供了直接的唯象学证据。该研究连接了非微扰QCD建模与实验可观测量，深化了我们对质子结构及其质量起源的理解。

Abstract: Understanding the internal structure of the proton-including the distributions of quarks and gluons and their contributions to proton properties such as mass-remains a central challenge in quantum chromodynamics (QCD). While quark generalized parton distributions (GPDs) have been studied extensively, a unified approach that simultaneously extracts quark parton distribution functions (PDFs), gravitational form factors (GFFs), and gluon GPDs from experimental constraints is still lacking. Moreover, the role of gluons in proton mass generation, particularly through the trace anomaly mechanism, requires deeper theoretical and phenomenological exploration. In this study, we first extract quark GPDs in protons using parameterization method based on the electromagnetic form factors provided by Light-Front Holographic QCD (LFHQCD) from which we derive both quark PDFs and their GFFs. We then extend this approach to model gluon GPDs. Our calculations show consistency with experimental data and lattice QCD results and successfully reproduce soft Pomeron behavior. Furthermore, we investigate near-threshold $J/ψ$ production using gauge/string duality to quantify the contribution of the trace anomaly to the proton mass. Our results demonstrate that the parameterization method provides a consistent framework for describing both quark and gluon structure, bridging GPDs, PDFs, and GFFs. The analysis of $J/ψ$ production confirms that the trace anomaly contributes significantly ($\sim 23\%$) to the proton mass, with the calculated cross-section dependence on momentum transfer $t$ in agreement with experimental observations. This work advances the understanding of proton structure by integrating quark and gluon degrees of freedom and elucidating the origin of proton mass within QCD.

</details>


### [16] [Magnetic moments of strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks and the role of spin flavor correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04911)
*Pallavi Gupta,vikas kumar Garg*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute magnetic moments of strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks ($qqqbb$) in three structural models—baryon-meson molecule, diquark-diquark-antiquark, and diquark-triquark—and find that magnetic moments are nearly identical across compact configurations, governed by global spin-flavor symmetry rather than internal clustering. Moments are suppressed with increasing strangeness and dominated by light strange quark spin correlations due to the heavy bottom quark mass.
\n\n
本文计算了含奇异夸克的隐底五夸克态（$qqqbb$）在三种结构模型（重子-介子分子态、双夸克-双夸克-反夸克态、双夸克-三夸克态）下的磁矩，发现紧致构型中的磁矩几乎相同，由整体自旋-味对称性而非内部团簇细节主导。随着奇异性的增加，磁矩系统性压低，并且主要由轻奇异夸克的自旋关联决定，因为底夸克质量很大，其贡献被强烈抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the internal structure of exotic hadrons like pentaquarks requires observables sensitive to their configuration. Magnetic moments serve as such probes, distinguishing between molecular versus compact multiquark arrangements. The hidden-bottom sector offers a theoretically clean environment due to the heavy $b$-quark mass, which simplifies dynamics via heavy-quark symmetry and suppresses its magnetic contribution, thereby highlighting the role of light (strange) quarks.
\n\n
理解五夸克等奇特强子的内部结构需要对构型敏感的可观测量。磁矩正是这类探针，可用于区分分子态与紧致多夸克构型。隐底强子体系因底夸克（$b$-quark）质量大而提供了一个理论干净的环境：重夸克对称性简化了动力学，且其磁矩贡献被强烈抑制，从而凸显轻（奇异）夸克的作用。

Method: The authors employ the constituent quark model to compute magnetic moments for negative-parity strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks ($S = -1, -2, -3$) with quark content $qqqbb$. Three structural ansätze are considered: (i) baryon-meson molecular state $[bq_1][\bar{b}q_2q_3]$, (ii) diquark-diquark-antiquark $[bq_1q_2][\bar{b}q_3]$, and (iii) diquark-triquark $[bq_1][\bar{b}q_2q_3]$. Spin-flavor wavefunctions are constructed for maximally aligned spin configurations, and magnetic moments are evaluated using $\mu = \sum_i \\frac{e_i}{2m_i} \\sigma_i$, where $e_i$, $m_i$, and $\\sigma_i$ are the charge, constituent mass, and spin projection of quark $i$.
\n\n
作者采用组分夸克模型计算具有负宇称、含奇异夸克的隐底五夸克态（$S = -1, -2, -3$，夸克组分 $qqqbb$）的磁矩。考虑了三种结构假设：(i) 重子-介子分子态 $[bq_1][\\bar{b}q_2q_3]$，(ii) 双夸克-双夸克-反夸克态 $[bq_1q_2][\\bar{b}q_3]$，(iii) 双夸克-三夸克态 $[bq_1][\\bar{b}q_2q_3]$。针对最大自旋排列构型构建自旋-味波函数，并使用公式 $\mu = \sum_i \\frac{e_i}{2m_i} \\sigma_i$ 计算磁矩，其中 $e_i$、$m_i$ 和 $\\sigma_i$ 分别为第 $i$ 个夸克的电荷、组分质量和自旋投影。

Result: For dominant spin couplings and maximally aligned states, the diquark-diquark-antiquark and diquark-triquark compact configurations yield nearly identical magnetic moments, indicating insensitivity to internal clustering. All configurations exhibit systematic suppression of magnetic moments with increasing strangeness ($|S|$) and a clear hierarchy based on total spin. The heavy $b$-quark contributions are negligible due to $m_b \gg m_{u,d,s}$, rendering the magnetic moments primarily dependent on spin correlations among light strange quarks.
\n\n
在主导自旋耦合和最大自旋排列态下，双夸克-双夸克-反夸克与双夸克-三夸克这两种紧致构型给出几乎相同的磁矩，表明其对内部团簇结构不敏感。所有构型均表现出随奇异量子数（$|S|$）增大而系统性压低的磁矩，以及清晰的总自旋层级结构。由于 $m_b \gg m_{u,d,s}$，重底夸克贡献可忽略，磁矩主要依赖于轻奇异夸克之间的自旋关联。

Conclusion: The magnetic moments of strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks are robustly determined by global spin-flavor symmetries rather than specific spatial clustering, especially in compact configurations. This universality, combined with strong suppression from strangeness and dominance of light-quark spin dynamics, provides clear theoretical predictions for future experimental identification of exotic multiquark states in the hidden-bottom sector.
\n\n
含奇异夸克的隐底五夸克态的磁矩由整体自旋-味对称性稳健决定，而非特定的空间团簇结构，尤其在紧致构型中如此。这种普适性，结合奇异性的强压低效应和轻夸克自旋动力学的主导作用，为未来实验在隐底区域识别奇特多夸克态提供了清晰的理论预言。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic moments of strange hidden bottom pentaquark states within the constituent quark model considering molecular and compact configurations. The system with quark content qqqbb is analyzed in three scenarios a baryon meson molecular configuration bq1bq2q3 a diquark diquark antiquark configuration bq1q2q3b and a diquark triquark configuration bq1bq2q3. The negative parity states with are studied for strangeness. We find that for the dominant spin couplings and maximally aligned configurations the diquark diquark antiquark qqqbb and diquark triquark bqqqb descriptions yield identical or numerically very close magnetic moments indicating that in the hidden bottom sector the magnetic properties are governed primarily by the global spin flavor structure rather than clustering details. A systematic suppression with increasing strangeness and a clear spin hierarchy are observed in all configurations. Due to the large bottom quark mass, heavy quark contributions are strongly suppressed, making the magnetic moments primarily sensitive to light strange spin correlations. These results provide theoretical benchmarks for future experimental studies of exotic multiquark states.

</details>


### [17] [Critical fluctuation patterns and anisotropic correlations driven by temperature gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04923)
*Lijia Jiang,Tao Yang,Jun-Hui Zheng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how spatial temperature gradients in heavy-ion collision fireballs affect QCD phase transition signals, revealing that singular fluctuation modes exhibit strong anisotropy—long-ranged along isotherms but suppressed radially—and that angular momentum modes contribute comparably to correlations, offering new azimuthally sensitive observables for detecting the QCD critical point.
\n\n
本文研究了重离子碰撞火球中空间温度梯度对QCD相变信号的影响，揭示奇异涨落模式表现出强烈各向异性——沿等温线长程关联但径向受抑制——且角动量模式对关联的贡献相当，从而提出新的方位角敏感观测量以探测QCD临界点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional studies of QCD phase transition signals assume spatially uniform temperature, neglecting realistic thermal inhomogeneities in heavy-ion collision fireballs. The authors aim to explore how temperature gradients near the phase interface modify critical fluctuations and whether these modifications yield new experimental signatures.
\n\n
传统QCD相变信号研究假设空间温度均匀，忽略了重离子碰撞火球中真实的热不均匀性。作者旨在探索相界面附近温度梯度如何改变临界涨落，以及这些改变是否产生新的实验信号。

Method: The authors employ an Ising-like effective potential to model locally equilibrated systems with spatial temperature gradients in a 2D disk geometry. They decompose low-energy fluctuations into radial and angular momentum modes, analyze the nonlocal correlation structure of singular eigenmodes, and connect dominant angular momentum modes to anisotropic flow observables.
\n\n
作者采用Ising-like有效势，在二维圆盘几何中建模具有空间温度梯度的局域平衡系统。他们将低能涨落分解为径向和角动量模式，分析奇异本征模式的非局域关联结构，并将主导的角动量模式与各向异性流观测量联系起来。

Result: The singular eigenmodes exhibit strong anisotropy: correlations are long-ranged along isotherms (angular direction) but suppressed in the radial direction due to thermal geometry. Unlike homogeneous systems dominated by the zero-momentum mode, here multiple angular momentum modes (including non-zero) contribute comparably to correlations. These modes are linked to azimuthally sensitive observables such as anisotropic flow.
\n\n
奇异本征模式表现出强烈各向异性：关联沿等温线（角向）长程，但因热几何而在径向受抑制。与由零动量模式主导的均匀系统不同，此处多个角动量模式（包括非零）对关联的贡献相当。这些模式与各向异性流等方位角敏感观测量相关联。

Conclusion: Spatial temperature gradients fundamentally alter the nature of critical fluctuations near the QCD phase transition, inducing anisotropic correlation patterns that can be probed via azimuthally differential measurements. This provides a novel experimental strategy to detect the QCD critical point through anisotropic flow and related observables.
\n\n
空间温度梯度从根本上改变了QCD相变附近临界涨落的性质，诱导出可通过方位角微分测量探测的各向异性关联模式。这为通过各向异性流及相关观测量探测QCD临界点提供了新实验策略。

Abstract: Studies of QCD phase transition signals are often conducted under spatially uniform temperature conditions. However, the influence of spatial temperature gradients on the signals emerging at the phase interface in the fireball generated by heavy-ion collisions has not yet been fully explored. Based on an Ising-like effective potential, we study the locally equilibrated systems with temperature gradients. In a 2D disk geometry, the low-energy fluctuation spectrum is explicitly resolved into radial and angular momentum modes. The nonlocal correaltions of singular eigen-mode exhibits strong anisotropy, which are long-ranged along isotherms but suppressed radially due to the thermal geometry of the system. Unlike homogeneous systems where the zero-momentum mode dominates, correlations in such inhomogeneous system result from the superposition of a series of zero and non-zero angular momentum modes with comparable contributions. We extract the singular angular momentum modes and establish their connection to experimentally observable anisotropic flow. We find azimuthally sensitive observables may offer a previously unexplored avenue for detecting the QCD phase transition.

</details>


### [18] [On the robustness of the indirect determination of the width of the detected Higgs boson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05020)
*Panagiotis Stylianou,Georg Weiglein*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates whether the LHC's indirect Higgs width bounds remain robust when relaxing the assumption of equal on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers. It finds that in realistic BSM scenarios (e.g., scalar extensions), the bound weakens by at most a factor of ~2, except for light new states.
\n\n
本文研究了在放宽“壳上（on-shell）与壳外（off-shell）耦合修正因子相等”这一假设后，LHC对希格斯玻色子总宽度的间接限制是否仍然稳健。结果表明，在现实的超出标准模型（BSM）情形（如标量扩展）中，该限制最多仅被削弱约2倍，除非存在较轻的新粒子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The LHC collaborations infer the Higgs boson total width indirectly under the assumption that coupling modifiers $\\kappa$ are identical for on-shell and off-shell production. However, BSM physics could modify these regions differently, potentially allowing a larger physical width than currently quoted. The authors aim to assess how much this assumption affects the derived upper limits on the Higgs width in well-motivated BSM frameworks.
\n\n
LHC合作组在推断希格斯玻色子总宽度时，依赖于壳上与壳外耦合修正因子 $\\kappa$ 相同的假设。然而，超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理可能对这两个区域产生不同影响，从而允许实际宽度大于当前实验所给出的上限。作者旨在评估在有理论动机的BSM框架下，该假设对希格斯宽度上限的影响程度。

Method: The authors consider explicit BSM scenarios—specifically scalar extensions of the Standard Model featuring an additional scalar state that contributes either as a resonance or via loop corrections. They compute the effective on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers induced by these new states, compare them against existing experimental constraints (from Higgs signal strengths, direct searches, etc.) and theoretical requirements (unitarity, perturbativity). They then re-evaluate the indirect Higgs width bound without assuming equality between on- and off-shell modifiers.
\n\n
作者考虑了具体的超出标准模型（BSM）情形——特别是包含额外标量态的标准模型标量扩展，该标量态可作为共振态或通过圈图修正贡献。他们计算了这些新粒子诱导的有效壳上与壳外耦合修正因子，并与现有实验约束（如希格斯信号强度、直接新粒子搜索等）及理论要求（幺正性、微扰性）进行比较。随后，他们在不假设壳上与壳外修正因子相等的前提下，重新评估希格斯总宽度的间接上限。

Result: In most of the parameter space of the considered scalar extensions, the indirect Higgs width bounds from ATLAS and CMS remain valid. Only when the additional scalar is relatively light (close to the electroweak scale) can the on-shell and off-shell modifiers differ significantly, leading to a relaxation of the width bound. Even in these cases, the total width $\\Gamma_H$ is constrained to be less than about twice the Standard Model prediction ($\\Gamma_H^{\\rm SM}$), i.e., $\\Gamma_H \\lesssim 2\\, \\Gamma_H^{\\rm SM}$, consistent with current data.
\n\n
在所考虑的标量扩展模型的大部分参数空间中，ATLAS和CMS给出的希格斯宽度间接限制仍然有效。仅当额外标量粒子质量较轻（接近电弱能标）时，壳上与壳外耦合修正因子才可能出现显著差异，从而导致宽度限制被放松。即便如此，总宽度 $\\Gamma_H$ 仍被限制在标准模型预测值 $\\Gamma_H^{\\rm SM}$ 的约两倍以内，即 $\\Gamma_H \\lesssim 2\\, \\Gamma_H^{\\rm SM}$，与当前实验数据一致。

Conclusion: Relaxing the assumption of equal on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers only mildly weakens the indirect upper bound on the Higgs total width in realistic BSM scenarios. The current LHC limit remains robust, with the maximal allowed width increasing by at most a factor of two. Future direct searches for light scalars will further test the remaining viable parameter space where the bound could be relaxed.
\n\n
在现实的超出标准模型（BSM）情形中，放宽壳上与壳外耦合修正因子相等的假设仅会轻微削弱对希格斯总宽度的间接上限。当前LHC限制依然稳健，最大允许宽度最多增加约两倍。未来对轻标量粒子的直接搜索将进一步检验那些可能导致限制放松的剩余参数空间。

Abstract: The indirect determination of the total width of the detected Higgs boson that is carried out by the experimental collaborations at the LHC relies on the assumption that the coupling modifiers for the on-shell and off-shell couplings are the same. However, physics beyond the Standard Model affecting the on-shell and off-shell regions differently could invalidate this assumption, so that the actual width of the detected Higgs boson could be larger than the bounds obtained under this assumption. Relaxing the assumption and investigating different types of extensions of the Standard Model, we analyse under which conditions a larger total width of the detected Higgs boson is compatible with all experimental and theoretical constraints. For the considered scenarios of scalar extensions with an additional state contributing as a resonance or at the loop level, we find that the indirect bounds obtained by ATLAS and CMS remain valid over large parts of the parameter space, with the exception of parameter regions where the additional particles have relatively small masses. We discuss the potential of experimental searches for new particles to further constrain such scenarios. Based on the existing experimental and theoretical constraints we conclude that relaxing the assumption of equal on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers that is used in the experimental analyses at the LHC yields an upper bound on the total width of the detected Higgs boson in realistic extensions of the Standard Model that is only weakened by up to a factor of about two compared to the case where this assumption is valid.

</details>


### [19] [Renormalisation of Chiral Gauge Theories with Non-Anticommuting $γ_5$ at the Multi-Loop Level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05059)
*Matthias Weißwange*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This thesis achieves the first complete 4-loop renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory and the full 1-loop renormalisation of the Standard Model using the Breitenlohner-Maison/’t Hooft-Veltman (BMHV) scheme in dimensional regularisation, resolving γ₅-related symmetry-breaking issues via a systematic, algorithmic restoration procedure based on the quantum action principle.
\n\n
该论文首次在Breitenlohner-Maison/’t Hooft-Veltman（BMHV）方案下完成了阿贝尔手征规范理论的完整四圈重整化和标准模型（Standard Model）的完整一圈重整化，通过基于量子作用原理的系统性、算法化程序解决了γ₅引起的对称性破缺问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Chiral gauge theories, such as the Standard Model, pose significant challenges in dimensional regularisation due to the ill-defined nature of $\\gamma_5$ in $D \\neq 4$ dimensions. The widely used BMHV scheme introduces a non-anticommuting $\\gamma_5$, which breaks gauge and BRST symmetry at the quantum level, obstructing consistent multi-loop calculations. A robust, systematic method to restore these symmetries is essential for high-precision predictions in electroweak physics.
\n\n
手征规范理论（如标准模型）在维度正规化（dimensional regularisation）中因$D \\neq 4$维下$\\gamma_5$定义不明确而面临重大挑战。广泛使用的BMHV方案引入非反对易的$\\gamma_5$，在量子层面破坏规范对称性和BRST对称性，阻碍了自洽的多圈计算。为电弱物理中的高精度预言，亟需一种稳健且系统性的方法来恢复这些对称性。

Method: The work employs the BMHV scheme with a non-anticommuting $\\gamma_5$, where symmetry breaking is treated as a local insertion in the effective action. Using the quantum action principle, the authors develop a fully algorithmic procedure to restore gauge and BRST invariance by introducing finite counterterms order-by-order in perturbation theory. This is implemented within a high-performance automated computational framework optimized for multi-loop Feynman diagram evaluation, handling evanescent operators and $D$-dimensional fermion algebra efficiently.
\n\n
该工作采用具有非反对易$\\gamma_5$的BMHV方案，将对称性破缺视为有效作用量中的局域插入项。作者基于量子作用原理，发展了一套完全算法化的程序，通过在微扰论中逐阶引入有限抵消项（finite counterterms）来恢复规范与BRST不变性。该方法在一个高性能自动化计算框架中实现，该框架针对多圈费曼图计算进行了优化，能高效处理蒸发算符（evanescent operators）和$D$维费米子代数。

Result: The thesis reports the complete 4-loop renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory—the highest loop order achieved with the BMHV scheme—and the complete 1-loop renormalisation of the full Standard Model. It demonstrates that consistent treatment of $\\gamma_5$ is feasible at high orders, resolves ambiguities related to different $D$-dimensional implementations, and provides practical prescriptions for fermion and gauge sectors. The results confirm the viability of the BMHV scheme for precision SM calculations.
\n\n
论文报告了阿贝尔手征规范理论的完整四圈重整化（BMHV方案迄今最高圈数）以及完整标准模型的一圈重整化。结果表明，即使在高圈阶，$\\gamma_5$仍可被一致处理；解决了不同$D$维实现方案引起的模糊性，并为费米子与规范相互作用提供了实用处方。这些成果验证了BMHV方案用于标准模型高精度计算的可行性。

Conclusion: This work establishes a solid, self-consistent foundation for multi-loop renormalisation of chiral gauge theories in dimensional regularisation using the BMHV scheme. The algorithmic symmetry-restoration procedure and efficient computational tools pave the way for future high-order calculations in the Standard Model, enabling rigorous high-precision electroweak phenomenology beyond leading order.
\n\n
本工作为在维度正规化中使用BMHV方案进行手征规范理论的多圈重整化建立了坚实且自洽的基础。所发展的算法化对称性恢复程序与高效计算工具，为标准模型中的高阶计算铺平了道路，使超越领头阶的严格高精度电弱唯象学成为可能。

Abstract: This thesis presents a comprehensive study of the renormalisation of chiral gauge theories in dimensional regularisation (DReg) at the multi-loop level. We employ the mathematically consistent Breitenlohner-Maison/`t~Hooft-Veltman (BMHV) scheme with non-anticommuting $γ_5$, whose modified algebraic relations induce a spurious violation of gauge and BRST invariance. A central focus is the systematic restoration of the broken symmetry, for which we provide a transparent and fully algorithmic procedure based on the quantum action principle. A major achievement of this work is the complete 4-loop renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory -- the highest-order application of the BMHV scheme to date. This calculation is made possible by an automated, high-performance computational framework incorporating several optimised algorithms. Our results demonstrate that a rigorous, self-consistent treatment of $γ_5$ is feasible even at very high loop orders. We further analyse dimensional ambiguities and evanescent details corresponding to different implementations of the regularisation, and identify practically efficient prescriptions for $D$-dimensional fermions and gauge interactions. Building on these insights, we present the complete 1-loop renormalisation of the full Standard Model (SM) in the BMHV scheme, providing a first step towards a fully self-consistent multi-loop renormalisation of the SM and establishing a solid foundation for future high-precision electroweak phenomenology.

</details>


### [20] [Muon collider experiments as electron/positron beam sources: case studies of new light-particle searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05086)
*Yasuhito Sakaki,Daiki Ueda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the feasibility of extracting high-energy electrons and positrons from muon decays in two future muon collider designs—IMCC and μTRISTAN—and proposes their use for novel particle physics searches, including dark matter via missing energy/momentum at μTRISTAN and axion-like particles/light scalars via visible decays at IMCC.
\n\n
本文研究了从两种未来缪子对撞机设计（IMCC 和 $\\mu$TRISTAN）中提取高能电子和正电子的可行性，并提出利用这些粒子开展新物理搜索：在 $\\mu$TRISTAN 上通过丢失能量/动量寻找暗物质，在 IMCC 上通过可见衰变寻找类轴子粒子和轻标量粒子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon colliders naturally generate intense beams of decay electrons and positrons with high energies, high repetition rates, and small intrinsic uncertainties—features not accessible at current accelerators. The authors aim to assess whether these secondary beams can be practically extracted and repurposed for precision or intensity-frontier experiments beyond the collider’s primary program.
\n\n
缪子对撞机天然产生具有高能量、高重复频率和小本征不确定性的强电子/正电子束流，这些特性在现有加速器设施中无法实现。作者旨在评估这些次级束流是否可以被实际提取并用于主对撞程序之外的精度或强度前沿实验。

Method: The authors perform Monte Carlo simulations using the design parameters of two muon collider concepts: IMCC and μTRISTAN. They analyze the spatial, angular, and energy distributions of decay electrons/positrons in the curved sections of the ring. They evaluate deflection angles (0.1–10 mrad) achievable with bending magnets acting as pre-septum elements for beam extraction. Based on the distinct beam characteristics of each collider, they formulate complementary experimental strategies.
\n\n
作者使用两种缪子对撞机方案（IMCC 和 $\\mu$TRISTAN）的设计参数进行蒙特卡洛模拟，分析环形弯曲段中衰变电子/正电子的空间、角度和能量分布。他们评估了利用弯转磁铁（作为预偏转磁铁）可实现的偏转角（0.1–10 mrad），并据此提出基于各对撞机束流特性的互补实验策略。

Result: The simulations show that even high-energy electrons carrying 60–100% of the muon beam energy can be deflected by 0.1–10 mrad using existing ring bending magnets, enabling practical extraction. This facilitates two new search channels: (1) missing energy/momentum searches for dark matter at μTRISTAN, and (2) visible-decay searches for axion-like particles and light scalars at IMCC, both probing unexplored parameter space beyond current experimental sensitivities.
\n\n
模拟表明，即使携带缪子束流能量 60–100% 的高能电子也能通过现有环形弯转磁铁实现 0.1–10 mrad 的偏转，从而支持实际束流提取。这催生两种新搜索通道：(1) 在 $\\mu$TRISTAN 上通过丢失能量/动量寻找暗物质；(2) 在 IMCC 上通过可见衰变寻找类轴子粒子和轻标量粒子，二者均可探测当前实验灵敏度之外的新参数空间。

Conclusion: Decay electrons and positrons from muon colliders represent a valuable, underutilized resource. With modest modifications, existing collider infrastructure can enable novel fixed-target or beam-dump experiments. The proposed extraction scheme is feasible, and the resulting beams open unique opportunities for probing dark sectors, complementing the main collider physics program.
\n\n
缪子对撞机产生的衰变电子和正电子是一种宝贵但未被充分利用的资源。通过适度改造现有对撞机基础设施，即可支持新型固定靶或束流打靶实验。所提出的提取方案切实可行，所产生的束流为探索暗区物理提供了独特机遇，可有效补充主对撞机物理计划。

Abstract: At muon colliders, muon decays naturally produce intense electrons and positrons with unique features, namely high energies, high repetition rates, and small intrinsic uncertainties, that are unavailable at existing accelerator facilities. We quantitatively study the feasibility of extracting such particles in two representative future muon collider designs, IMCC and $μ$TRISTAN. Using Monte Carlo simulations with the corresponding design parameters, we study the spatial, angular, and energy distributions of decay electrons and positrons in the curved sections of the collider ring. We find that typical deflections of $0.1-10~\mathrm{mrad}$ can be achieved even for high-energy electrons carrying large energy fractions ($\simeq 0.6 - 1.0$) of the muon beam energy, with the ring bending magnets (or magnets providing an equivalent field) effectively serving as a pre-septum magnet, that partially deflects the beam before the main septum magnet, suggesting that the extraction scheme could be practically feasible. Exploiting the distinct beam properties of IMCC and $μ$TRISTAN, we propose complementary search strategies, missing energy and momentum searches for dark matter at $μ$TRISTAN and visible-decay searches for axion-like particles and light scalars at IMCC, which probe parameter space beyond the reach of current and other proposed experiments.

### [21] [Flavor Democracy Calls for Vector Like Leptons and Quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05104)
*Burak Dagli,Saleh Sultansoy,Ismail Toy*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper argues that Flavor Democracy in the Standard Model is challenged by the large top quark mass, and proposes Vector-Like Leptons (VLLs) and Vector-Like Quarks (VLQs) as a viable solution. It criticizes current LHC searches for VLLs for relying on an overly restrictive model and calls for broader experimental analyses covering all decay channels.
\n\n
本文指出，标准模型中的Flavor Democracy假设因顶夸克质量远大于其他费米子而面临挑战，并提出引入Vector-Like Leptons（VLLs）和Vector-Like Quarks（VLQs）作为自然解决方案。文章批评当前LHC对VLLs的搜寻依赖于一个高度受限的模型，并呼吁开展涵盖所有可行衰变道的更全面实验分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the tension between the Flavor Democracy hypothesis—which posits nearly equal treatment of all fermion generations at high scales—and the observed large hierarchy in fermion masses, particularly $m_t \\gg m_b, m_\\tau$. The exclusion of a fourth SM generation by Higgs data removes a previously plausible resolution, necessitating alternative mechanisms like VLLs/VLQs that preserve Flavor Democracy while generating realistic mass spectra.
\n\n
动机源于Flavor Democracy假设（即在高能标下所有费米子代近乎平权）与观测到的费米子质量层级（尤其是$m_t \\gg m_b, m_\\tau$）之间的张力。由于希格斯数据已基本排除第四代标准模型，必须寻找替代机制；VLLs/VLQs可在保持Flavor Democracy的同时生成符合现实的质量谱。

Method: The paper advocates a theoretical framework where VLLs and VLQs are introduced to restore Flavor Democracy through their mixing with SM fermions. It critiques the current experimental approach—specifically the “Restricted Model” used by ATLAS/CMS—which assumes degenerate VLL doublet masses and no right-handed neutrinos. The authors call for phenomenological re-analysis incorporating general VLL mass splittings and full decay topologies.
\n\n
本文采用的理论方法是引入VLLs和VLQs，通过它们与标准模型费米子的混合来恢复Flavor Democracy。作者批判了ATLAS/CMS目前采用的“Restricted Model”——该模型假设VLL双重态内带电与中性分量质量简并且不含右手中微子。文章呼吁开展包含一般VLL质量分裂和完整衰变拓扑的唯象学再分析。

Result: The key result is the identification of a significant gap between current experimental searches and theoretically motivated VLL scenarios. The Restricted Model fails to capture realistic parameter space, implying that existing null results do not rule out VLLs that could naturally explain fermion mass hierarchies under Flavor Democracy.
\n\n
核心结果是指出当前实验搜寻与理论驱动的VLL场景之间存在显著差距。“Restricted Model”无法覆盖真实参数空间，意味着现有零结果并不能排除那些在Flavor Democracy框架下自然解释费米子质量层级的VLLs。

Conclusion: To test the Flavor Democracy hypothesis via VLLs/VLQs, collider experiments must move beyond the Restricted Model and perform comprehensive searches across all kinematically allowed decay channels. Only such generalized analyses can meaningfully probe the viability of this elegant solution to the flavor puzzle.
\n\n
为通过VLLs/VLQs检验Flavor Democracy假设，对撞机实验必须超越“Restricted Model”，在所有运动学允许的衰变道中开展全面搜寻。唯有此类广义分析才能有效检验这一解决味物理难题的优雅方案的可行性。

Abstract: There are strong arguments favoring the Flavor Democracy hypothesis (or the Democratic Mass Matrix approach) within the Standard Model framework. However, the large mass of the top quark ($m_t >> m_b, m_τ$) poses an obstacle to the functioning of Flavor Democracy in the three SM family scenario. While a fourth Standard Model generation could have provided a natural resolution, this possibility is now almost entirely excluded by precision data on Higgs boson production and decay rates. The Flavor Democracy hypothesis can be elegantly resurrected through the introduction of Vector-Like Leptons (VLLs) and Vector-Like Quarks (VLQs), which naturally accommodate the observed fermion mass hierarchies while remaining consistent with current experimental constraints. Currently, experimental searches for VLLs conducted by the ATLAS and CMS collaborations rely on a highly constrained Restricted Model. This model imposes a mass degeneracy between charged and neutral VLLs within a doublet and assumes the absence of right-handed neutrinos. Consequently, current results are valid only for the restricted model and do not cover a more realistic, general scenario. Therefore, to accurately reflect the physical reality, it is imperative to conduct a comprehensive re-evaluation that incorporates all viable decay channels.

### [22] [TeV-scale unification of light dark matter and neutrino mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05200)
*Cheng-Wei Chiang,Shu-Yu Ho,Van Que Tran*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes a unified framework where TeV-scale heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) generate neutrino masses via the inverse seesaw mechanism and simultaneously produce and mediate the decay of a light pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson dark matter (DM) candidate. The model predicts correlated observables: sub-GeV DM with a lifetime consistent with current bounds, and detectable neutrino signals from DM decay in next-generation experiments.
\n\n
本文提出一个统一框架：TeV能标的重惰性中微子（HNLs）通过逆跷跷板机制（inverse seesaw）产生中微子质量，同时生成并介导一种轻的赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子暗物质（DM）候选者的衰变。该模型预言了相互关联的可观测量：亚GeV暗物质，其寿命符合当前实验限制，并且其衰变产生的中微子信号可在下一代探测器（如Hyper-Kamiokande、DUNE和JUNO）中被观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to unify the origin of neutrino masses and dark matter within a minimal, testable extension of the Standard Model. By linking both phenomena to TeV-scale HNLs and spontaneous lepton number violation, the model addresses the nature of DM while explaining small neutrino masses, and offers concrete predictions for upcoming neutrino experiments and colliders.
\n\n
动机在于在一个极小且可检验的标准模型扩展中统一中微子质量和暗物质的起源。通过将这两种现象与TeV能标的重惰性中微子（HNLs）及轻子数自发破缺联系起来，该模型在解释微小中微子质量的同时阐明了暗物质的本质，并为即将开展的中微子实验和对撞机提供了明确的预言。

Method: The authors employ an inverse-seesaw extension of the Standard Model that includes TeV-scale HNLs and a spontaneously broken global $U(1)_L$ lepton number symmetry. The explicit breaking of this symmetry generates a small mass for the resulting pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson, which is identified as the DM candidate. The DM is produced via the freeze-in mechanism through interactions with the HNLs, and its decay into neutrinos is also mediated by these same HNLs. The relic abundance and decay rate are calculated self-consistently using the same parameters that determine the light neutrino masses.
\n\n
作者采用标准模型的一种逆跷跷板扩展，其中包含TeV能标的重惰性中微子（HNLs）和一个自发破缺的全局$U(1)_L$轻子数对称性。该对称性的显式破缺为所产生的赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子赋予一个小质量，后者被认定为暗物质候选者。暗物质通过与HNLs的相互作用以freeze-in机制产生，其衰变为中微子的过程也由相同的HNLs介导。作者利用决定轻中微子质量的同一组参数，自洽地计算了暗物质的剩余丰度和衰变率。

Result: The model establishes a tight correlation between the light neutrino mass scale, the DM relic density, and the DM lifetime. For HNLs at the TeV scale accessible to colliders, satisfying the observed relic density ($\\Omega_{\\rm DM} h^2 \\approx 0.12$) and current lifetime constraints requires the DM mass to be in the sub-GeV range. This leads to a predicted flux of decay-produced neutrinos that is within reach of next-generation detectors like Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, and JUNO.
\n\n
该模型在轻中微子质量标度、暗物质剩余丰度和暗物质寿命之间建立了紧密关联。对于对撞机可探测的TeV能标HNLs，若要同时满足观测到的剩余丰度（$\\Omega_{\\rm DM} h^2 \\approx 0.12$）和当前寿命限制，暗物质质量必须处于亚GeV范围。这导致由暗物质衰变产生的中微子通量可被下一代探测器（如Hyper-Kamiokande、DUNE和JUNO）探测到。

Conclusion: This work presents a predictive and experimentally falsifiable framework that unifies neutrino mass generation and dark matter. The use of TeV-scale HNLs in an inverse-seesaw setup not only explains small neutrino masses but also provides a complete dark matter scenario—from production via freeze-in to decay into neutrinos—with observable consequences in both collider and neutrino experiments.
\n\n
本工作提出了一个具有预言能力且可被实验证伪的框架，统一了中微子质量生成与暗物质。在逆跷跷板机制中引入TeV能标的重惰性中微子（HNLs），不仅解释了微小的中微子质量，还构建了一个完整的暗物质图像——从freeze-in机制产生到衰变为中微子——并在对撞机和中微子实验中具有可观测效应。

Abstract: We demonstrate that TeV-scale heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) responsible for inverse-seesaw neutrino mass generation can simultaneously fix the cosmological abundance and decay properties of dark matter (DM). The spontaneous breaking of lepton number gives rise to a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson that serves as a light DM candidate, whose mass originates from a small explicit breaking term. The same HNLs that generate neutrino masses produce the DM via freeze-in and mediate its decay into neutrinos, leading to a tight correlation among neutrino masses, DM relic abundance, and DM lifetime. For collider-accessible TeV-scale HNLs, the observed relic density and lifetime constraints point to sub-GeV DM, yielding observable neutrino signals at next-generation detectors such as Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, and JUNO. This framework establishes a predictive and experimentally testable link between neutrino mass generation and dark matter.

</details>


### [23] [Effective vertexes in magnetized quark-gluon plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05248)
*V. Skalozub*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates one-loop quark contributions to the effective potential in high-temperature QGP, deriving new effective vertices coupling magnetic fields ($b^3, b^8, b$) and the $A_0$ Polyakov loop condensate, which may produce observable signatures in heavy-ion collisions.
\n\n
本文研究了高温夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中单圈夸克对有效势的贡献，推导出耦合色磁場（$b^3, b^8$）、普通磁场（$b$）与Polyakov圈相关的$A_0$凝聚的新有效顶点，这些顶点可能在重离子碰撞实验中产生可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous work established a two-loop effective potential in SU(2) gluodynamics and full QCD that incorporates magnetic backgrounds and explains spontaneous generation of color and electromagnetic magnetic fields along with the $A_0$ condensate. However, the role of dynamical quarks at one-loop level—particularly their contribution to interactions between magnetic fields and the $A_0$ condensate—remained unexplored. This paper aims to fill that gap to identify novel experimental signatures of QGP formation.
\n\n
先前的工作已在SU(2)胶子动力学和完整量子色动力学（QCD）中建立了包含磁背景的双圈有效势，解释了色磁場、普通磁场及$A_0$凝聚的自发产生。然而，动力学夸克在单圈水平上的作用——特别是其对磁场与$A_0$凝聚之间相互作用的贡献——尚未被研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，以识别QGP形成的新型实验信号。

Method: The authors compute one-loop quark contributions to the finite-temperature effective potential $W(T, b^3, b^8, b, A_0)$ using thermal field theory in the presence of constant background fields: color magnetic fields $b^3, b^8$, electromagnetic field $b$, and the temporal gauge field $A_0$ (related to the Polyakov loop). They derive effective vertices by taking functional derivatives of the one-loop quark determinant with respect to these background fields, leveraging the proper-time formalism or heat kernel expansion adapted to non-Abelian backgrounds at high $T$.
\n\n
作者在恒定背景场（包括色磁場$b^3, b^8$、电磁场$b$以及与Polyakov圈相关的时序规范场$A_0$）存在下，利用有限温度场论计算单圈夸克对有效势$W(T, b^3, b^8, b, A_0)$的贡献。他们通过对单圈夸克行列式关于这些背景场进行泛函导数，推导出有效顶点，采用适用于高温非阿贝尔背景的固有时方法（proper-time formalism）或热核展开（heat kernel expansion）。

Result: The paper derives explicit expressions for effective vertices coupling quarks to combinations of $A_0$ and magnetic fields ($b^3, b^8, b$). These vertices generate new interaction terms in the effective action, leading to temperature-dependent couplings that could manifest as anomalous charge separation, chiral magnetic effects, or modified dilepton production in heavy-ion collisions—distinct signals of QGP formation beyond standard hydrodynamic predictions.
\n\n
本文推导出了夸克与$A_0$及磁場（$b^3, b^8, b$）组合耦合的有效顶点的显式表达式。这些顶点在有效作用量中生成新的相互作用项，导致温度依赖的耦合，可能在重离子碰撞中表现为反常电荷分离、手征磁效应或修正的双轻子产额——这些是超出标准流体力学预言的QGP形成特征信号。

Conclusion: Including one-loop quark effects completes the picture of spontaneous magnetization and $A_0$ condensation in hot QCD. The newly derived effective vertices provide a microscopic mechanism linking the Polyakov loop dynamics with electromagnetic and color magnetic responses, offering concrete phenomenological channels to probe QGP properties in experiments via magnetic-field-induced observables.
\n\n
包含单圈夸克效应完善了高温QCD中自发磁化与$A_0$凝聚的图像。新推导的有效顶点提供了Polyakov圈动力学与电磁及色磁响应之间联系的微观机制，为通过磁场诱导观测量在实验中探测QGP性质提供了具体的唯象通道。

Abstract: In quark-gluon plasma (QGP), at high temperatures $T$ the spontaneous generation of color magnetic fields, $b^3(T), b^8(T) \not = 0$ (3, 8 are color indexes), and usual magnetic field $b(T) \not = 0$ happens. Also, the Polyakov loop and related to it the $A_0(T)$ condensate, which is solution to Yang-Mills imaginary time equations, create.
  Recently, with the new type two-loop effective potential, which generalizes the known integral representation for the Bernoulli polynomials and takes into consideration the magnetic background, these effects were derived.
  The corresponding effective potential $W(T, b^3, b^8, b, A_0 )$ was calculated either in SU(2) gluodynamics or full quantum chromodynamics (QCD). The values of magnetic field strengths at different temperatures were calculated and the mechanism for stabilizing the background due to $A_0(T)$ was also discovered.
  In present paper, we concentrate on the one-loop quark contributions. In particular, we derive the effective vertexes, which couple magnetic fields and $A_0$. The vertexes result in new specific effects signalling the creation of QGP in heavy ion collision experiments.
  Key words: spontaneous magnetization, high temperature, asymptotic freedom, effective potential, $A_0$ condensate, effective vertexes.

### [24] [Axial-vector neutral-current measurements in coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05281)
*D. Aristizabal Sierra,Pablo M. Candela,Valentina De Romeri,Dimitrios K. Papoulias,Laura Trincado S*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the feasibility of measuring axial-current contributions to Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering (CE$\\nu$NS) using fluorine-based targets, particularly octafluoropropane ($\\text{C}_3\\text{F}_8$), and shows that such measurements could indirectly determine the axial coupling at the $\\sim 10\\%$ level while offering sensitivity to spin-dependent new physics.
\n\n
本文探讨了利用氟基靶材（特别是八氟丙烷（$\\text{C}_3\\text{F}_8$））测量Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering (CE$\\nu$NS) 中轴矢流贡献的可行性，表明此类测量可间接以约 $\\sim 10\\%$ 的精度确定轴矢耦合，并对自旋依赖的新物理场景具有探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While CE$\\nu$NS is primarily driven by vector neutral-current interactions, the axial-current component—though subleading—carries unique information about nuclear spin structure and potential spin-dependent beyond-Standard-Model physics. However, due to experimental challenges, this axial contribution has been largely neglected. The authors aim to identify viable target materials that enhance the axial signal relative to the dominant vector background, enabling its extraction and use as a probe for new physics.
\n\n
尽管CE$\\nu$NS主要由矢量中性流相互作用主导，但轴矢流分量（尽管是次主导的）携带了关于核自旋结构和潜在的自旋依赖超出标准模型（BSM）物理的独特信息。然而，由于实验上的挑战，这一轴矢贡献在很大程度上被忽视。作者旨在识别能够增强轴矢信号相对于主导矢量背景的可行靶材，从而实现其提取并用作新物理的探针。

Method: The authors compare the relative magnitudes of vector and axial contributions to the CE$\\nu$NS cross section across various target nuclei used in neutrino and dark matter experiments. They focus on nuclei with non-zero ground-state spin, especially fluorine, and evaluate the expected event rates for both pion decay-at-rest and reactor neutrino sources. Using realistic detector thresholds and flux uncertainties, they estimate the precision with which the axial coupling can be inferred from CE$\\nu$NS data.
\n\n
作者比较了在各类用于中微子和暗物质实验的靶核中，CE$\\nu$NS截面中矢量与轴矢贡献的相对大小。他们聚焦于具有非零基态自旋的原子核，特别是氟，并评估了来自π介子静止衰变和反应堆中微子源的预期事例率。结合现实的探测器阈值和通量不确定性，他们估算了从中微子核散射数据中推断轴矢耦合的精度。

Result: Fluorine-based compounds, especially $\\text{C}_3\\text{F}_8$, are identified as optimal targets due to their high axial-to-vector response ratio. With current and upcoming CE$\\nu$NS experiments using such targets and exposed to pion decay-at-rest or reactor neutrino fluxes, the axial coupling can be constrained at the $\\sim 10\\%$ level. This sensitivity also opens a pathway to test spin-dependent new physics scenarios via CE$\\nu$NS.
\n\n
氟基化合物（尤其是 $\\text{C}_3\\text{F}_8$）因其高的轴矢-矢量响应比而被确定为最优靶材。利用当前及未来的CE$\\nu$NS实验，配合π介子静止衰变或反应堆中微子通量，轴矢耦合可被限制在约 $\\sim 10\\%$ 的水平。这一灵敏度还为通过CE$\\nu$NS检验自旋依赖的新物理场景开辟了途径。

Conclusion: Measuring the axial-current contribution in CE$\\nu$NS is experimentally challenging but feasible with fluorine-rich targets like $\\text{C}_3\\text{F}_8$. Such measurements not only provide a novel way to determine the axial coupling of neutrons but also serve as a unique probe of spin-dependent interactions beyond the Standard Model, complementing direct dark matter searches.
\n\n
在CE$\\nu$NS中测量轴矢流贡献虽然具有实验挑战性，但使用如 $\\text{C}_3\\text{F}_8$ 等富氟靶材是可行的。这类测量不仅为确定中子的轴矢耦合提供了新方法，还可作为探测标准模型之外自旋依赖相互作用的独特手段，与直接暗物质搜寻形成互补。

Abstract: Coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) is predominantly governed by vector neutral-current interactions, with subleading contributions arising from the axial current in nuclei with non-zero ground-state spin. Experimentally, the extraction of axial-current contributions has been so far of little interest, mainly because of the challenges its measurement entail. In this work, we investigate the relative size of the vector and axial components for target materials currently employed by the neutrino and dark matter experimental communities. We identify fluorine-based compounds as the most promising targets for probing the axial-current event rate. Among them, octafluoropropane ($\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$) emerges as a particularly suitable candidate, given its widespread use in spin-dependent dark matter searches and its relevance for upcoming dedicated CE$ν$NS experiments. Considering both pion decay-at-rest and reactor neutrino fluxes, we show that such measurements can allow an indirect determination of the axial coupling at the $\sim 10\%$ level, depending on flux uncertainties and detector thresholds. We further emphasize that measurements of the axial current will allow to probe spin-dependent new physics scenarios through CE$ν$NS.

### [25] [The eV-Scale Sterile Neutrino and Neutrinoless Double Beta Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05304)
*Priya,Simran Arora,B. C. Chauhan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates short-baseline neutrino anomalies (e.g., LSND, MiniBooNE) using sterile neutrino models (3+1, 1+3, 2+2) and constrains the eV-scale sterile neutrino mass via neutrinoless double beta decay data under both normal and inverted mass hierarchies. The 3+1 model is favored, with sterile neutrino mass limited to ~4.75 eV (NH) and ~4.72 eV (IH) at 3σ, and total neutrino mass sum bounded at ~4.8 eV.
\n\n
本文研究了短基线中微子反常（如LSND、MiniBooNE）问题，采用惰性中微子模型（3+1、1+3、2+2），并利用无中微子双贝塔衰变数据在正常和倒转质量序下对eV量级的惰性中微子质量进行限制。3+1模型最受支持，在3σ置信度下，惰性中微子质量被限制为~4.75 eV（NH）和~4.72 eV（IH），四代中微子总质量之和上限约为4.8 eV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the persistent electron neutrino excess observed in short-baseline experiments like LSND and MiniBooNE, which cannot be explained within the standard three-neutrino oscillation framework. This anomaly suggests the possible existence of one or more eV-scale sterile neutrinos that mix with active neutrinos. The paper aims to explore how such extensions—specifically the 3+1, 1+3, and 2+2 neutrino mixing schemes—affect predictions for neutrinoless double beta decay ($0\\nu\\beta\\beta$), thereby providing constraints on sterile neutrino properties using current and future experimental sensitivities.
\n\n
动机源于LSND和MiniBooNE等短基线实验中持续观测到的电子中微子超出，该现象无法用标准三味中微子振荡框架解释。这一反常暗示可能存在一个或多个与活性中微子混合的eV量级惰性中微子。本文旨在探讨此类扩展模型（特别是3+1、1+3和2+2中微子混合方案）如何影响无中微子双贝塔衰变（$0\\nu\\beta\\beta$）的预言，从而利用当前及未来实验灵敏度对惰性中微子性质施加限制。

Method: The authors perform a global analysis incorporating updated experimental data and global fits to evaluate three sterile neutrino mixing schemes: 3+1 (three active + one sterile), 1+3 (one active + three sterile), and 2+2 (two active + two sterile). They compute the effective Majorana mass $m_{\\beta\\beta}$ relevant for neutrinoless double beta decay, considering both normal hierarchy (NH) and inverted hierarchy (IH) of the active neutrino masses. Using constraints from current and projected $0\\nu\\beta\\beta$ experiments, they derive upper limits on the sterile neutrino mass $m_s$ as a function of the lightest active neutrino mass $m_{\\text{lightest}}$, and also constrain the total sum of all four neutrino masses $\\sum m_\\nu$.
\n\n
作者采用包含最新实验数据和全局拟合结果的全局分析方法，评估三种惰性中微子混合方案：3+1（三个活性+一个惰性）、1+3（一个活性+三个惰性）和2+2（两个活性+两个惰性）。他们计算了与无中微子双贝塔衰变相关的有效马约拉纳质量 $m_{\\beta\\beta}$，同时考虑活性中微子质量的正常序（NH）和倒转序（IH）。利用当前及预期的 $0\\nu\\beta\\beta$ 实验限制，推导出惰性中微子质量 $m_s$ 相对于最轻活性中微子质量 $m_{\\text{lightest}}$ 的上限，并对四代中微子总质量之和 $\\sum m_\\nu$ 进行约束。

Result: The analysis shows that the 3+1 scheme is the most viable among the three models. At the 3σ confidence level, the sterile neutrino mass is constrained to $m_s = 4.75~\\text{eV}$ for NH and $4.72~\\text{eV}$ for IH, assuming maximal sensitivity to $m_{\\text{lightest}}$. The corresponding upper bounds on the total neutrino mass sum are $\\sum m_\\nu = 4.81~\\text{eV}$ (NH) and $4.78~\\text{eV}$ (IH). The 1+3 and 2+2 schemes are less favored due to tension with existing $0\\nu\\beta\\beta$ limits and oscillation data.
\n\n
分析表明，3+1方案在三种模型中最可行。在3σ置信度下，假设对 $m_{\\text{lightest}}$ 具有最大灵敏度，惰性中微子质量被限制为 $m_s = 4.75~\\text{eV}$（NH）和 $4.72~\\text{eV}$（IH）。对应的四代中微子总质量之和上限为 $\\sum m_\\nu = 4.81~\\text{eV}$（NH）和 $4.78~\\text{eV}$（IH）。由于与现有 $0\\nu\\beta\\beta$ 限制和振荡数据存在张力，1+3和2+2方案较不被支持。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the 3+1 sterile neutrino model remains consistent with current neutrinoless double beta decay constraints and provides testable predictions for upcoming experiments. The derived mass limits on the sterile neutrino and the total neutrino mass sum offer valuable guidance for both particle physics and cosmology. Future improvements in $0\\nu\\beta\\beta$ sensitivity will further probe the eV-scale sterile neutrino hypothesis and potentially resolve the short-baseline anomaly.
\n\n
本研究得出结论：3+1惰性中微子模型仍与当前无中微子双贝塔衰变限制一致，并为未来实验提供了可检验的预言。所获得的惰性中微子质量及总中微子质量之和的限制，对粒子物理和宇宙学具有重要指导意义。未来 $0\\nu\\beta\\beta$ 实验灵敏度的提升将进一步检验eV量级惰性中微子假说，并可能解决短基线反常问题。

Abstract: In short-baseline experiments such as LSND and MiniBooNE, an excess of electron neutrinos has been observed, originating from a muon neutrino beam. To address this anomaly, in the line of many works, we investigate various neutrino mixing schemes involving eV-scale sterile neutrinos alongside three active neutrinos. Using updated experimental and global fit data, we studied neutrinoless double beta decay for three different schemes such as 3+1, 1 + 3, and 2 + 2, which involve one sterile neutrino and three active neutrinos. We have done analysis of these schemes for normal hierarchy (NH) as well as for inverted hierarchy (IH) frameworks, and constrained the sterile neutrino mass in light of current and future neutrinoless double beta decay experiments. The 3+1 scheme is found to be the most viable and at the level of $3σ$ the mass of sterile neutrino with respect to the lightest neutrino mass ($m_{\text{lightest}}$) is restricted to $4.75~eV$ for the NH and $4.72~eV$ for the IH. Additionally, the limits on the sum of four neutrino masses are determined to be $4.81~eV$ for the normal hierarchy and $4.78~eV$ for the inverted hierarchy. The updated analysis of all these schemes would help us in understanding physics governing neutrinoless double beta decay and limit on the mass of sterile neutrinos.

### [26] [Exploring $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates in a coupled-channels formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05311)
*P. G. Ortega,D. R. Entem,F. Fernandez,J. Segovia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates using a coupled-channels approach, identifying numerous resonant and virtual states between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. These states form approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry multiplets, with widths from tens to hundreds of MeV. Many couple strongly to channels with excited bottomonia, suggesting specific experimental signatures.

\n\n
我们采用耦合道方法研究 $T_{ΥΥ}$ 四夸克候选态，在 $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ 与 $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ 阈值之间识别出大量共振态和虚态。这些态近似构成重夸克自旋对称性多重态，宽度从几十到几百 MeV 不等。许多态与包含激发底偶素的末态强耦合，暗示了特定的实验信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the existence and properties of fully-heavy $bb\\bar{b}\\bar{b}$ tetraquarks, which are theoretically plausible but experimentally elusive. Understanding their spectrum tests nonperturbative QCD dynamics, heavy-quark spin symmetry (HQSS), and the role of coupled-channel effects near thresholds involving radially excited bottomonia.

\n\n
动机在于探索全重 $bb\\bar{b}\\bar{b}$ 四夸克态的存在性与性质，这类态在理论上合理但实验上难以观测。理解其谱结构可检验非微扰 QCD 动力学、重夸克自旋对称性（HQSS）以及涉及径向激发底偶素阈值附近的耦合道效应。

Method: The authors employ a coupled-channels framework where meson-meson interactions are derived from a constituent quark model via the Resonating Group Method (RGM). They consider all $L \\leq 2$ partial waves for combinations of $Υ(1S)$, $Υ(2S)$, $η_b(1S)$, and $η_b(2S)$ in quantum number sectors $J^P = 0^\\pm, 1^\\pm, 2^\\pm$. Physical states are identified as poles of the scattering matrix $S$ in the complex energy plane.

\n\n
作者采用耦合道框架，其中介子-介子相互作用通过共振群方法（Resonating Group Method, RGM）从组分夸克模型导出。他们考虑了 $Υ(1S)$、$Υ(2S)$、$η_b(1S)$ 和 $η_b(2S)$ 在量子数 $J^P = 0^\\pm, 1^\\pm, 2^\\pm$ 各个通道中所有 $L \\leq 2$ 的分波。物理态被识别为复能量平面上散射矩阵 $S$ 的极点。

Result: The analysis reveals a rich spectrum of poles—both resonant and virtual—between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. These poles organize into approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry (HQSS) multiplets. Lower-mass states are often dominated by a single channel (threshold-driven), while higher-mass states exhibit significant mixing among channels with radially excited bottomonia. Predicted widths range from tens to several hundred MeV. Branching ratios show preferential coupling to final states containing at least one excited bottomonium ($Υ(2S)$ or $η_b(2S)$), implying limited visibility in ground-state-only channels like $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$.

\n\n
分析揭示了在 $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ 与 $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ 阈值之间丰富的极点谱——包括共振态和虚态。这些极点近似构成重夸克自旋对称性（HQSS）多重态。低质量态通常由单一通道主导（阈值驱动），而高质量态则在包含径向激发底偶素的通道间表现出显著混合。预测宽度范围为几十至几百 MeV。分支比显示这些态倾向于耦合到至少包含一个激发底偶素（$Υ(2S)$ 或 $η_b(2S)$）的末态，意味着在仅含基态的通道（如 $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$）中可观测性有限。

Conclusion: This work provides a quantitative prediction for the spectrum and decay patterns of fully-bottom tetraquarks, highlighting the importance of coupled-channel dynamics and heavy-quark spin symmetry. It offers concrete guidance for experimental searches at facilities like LHCb and Belle II, emphasizing that detection strategies should prioritize channels with excited bottomonia rather than solely ground-state pairs.

\n\n
本工作对全底四夸克态的谱结构和衰变模式给出了定量预言，突显了耦合道动力学和重夸克自旋对称性的重要性。它为 LHCb 和 Belle II 等实验装置的搜寻提供了具体指导，强调探测策略应优先考虑包含激发底偶素的通道，而非仅关注基态对。

Abstract: We investigate the spectrum of $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates within a coupled-channels framework. The analysis includes all $L\leq2$ combinations of $Υ(1S)$, $Υ(2S)$, $η_b(1S)$, and $η_b(2S)$ in the $J^P = 0^\pm, 1^\pm, 2^\pm$ sectors. The meson-meson interaction is derived from an underlying constituent quark model through the resonating group method, and the properties of the states are obtained from poles of the scattering matrix. We find a rich spectrum of resonant, and virtual, states distributed between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. The pattern of poles exhibits approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry multiplets. Several states are dominated by a single channel and can be associated with threshold-driven structures, while higher-mass resonances show sizable mixing among channels involving radially excited bottomonia. The predicted widths range from tens to several hundred MeV. Branching ratios indicate that many states couple predominantly to final states with at least one excited bottomonium, whereas only a subset of the spectrum is expected to be visible in the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$, $η_b(1S)Υ(1S)$ and $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$ channels. These results provide quantitative guidance for experimental searches of fully heavy tetraquarks and offer a test of coupled-channel dynamics and heavy-quark spin symmetry in the $bb\bar b\bar b$ sector.

</details>


### [27] [Renormalization and Factorization Scale-Invariant Predictions for the Higgs Rare Decay $H\to J/ψ+γ$ via the Principle of Maximum Conformality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05329)
*Qi-Sha Ran,Xing-Gang Wu,Jiang Yan,Xu-Chang Zheng,Chang-Xin Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper computes the Higgs decay width to $J/ψ+γ$ at N$^2$LO in NRQCD using the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) to eliminate renormalization- and factorization-scale dependencies, yielding a precise and robust prediction: $Γ(H→J/ψ+γ) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) × 10^{-11}$ GeV.
\n\n
本文在非相对论性QCD（NRQCD）框架下，利用最大共形原理（Principle of Maximum Conformality, PMC）计算了Higgs玻色子稀有衰变道 $H→J/ψ+γ$ 在N$^2$LO阶的衰变宽度，消除了重整化标度与因子化标度的依赖性，得到了精确且稳健的预言：$Γ(H→J/ψ+γ) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) × 10^{-11}$ GeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The rare exclusive decay $H\to J/ψ+γ$ offers a clean channel to probe the charm-quark Yukawa coupling, which is challenging to access directly due to the small mass of the charm quark. Traditional fixed-order QCD predictions suffer from large renormalization- and factorization-scale uncertainties, limiting their reliability. The authors aim to provide a more precise and theoretically stable prediction by applying the PMC to remove these ambiguities.
\n\n
稀有独占衰变道 $H\to J/ψ+γ$ 为探测粲夸克Yukawa耦合提供了一个干净的通道，而由于粲夸克质量较小，该耦合难以直接测量。传统的固定阶QCD预言受制于显著的重整化标度和因子化标度不确定性，限制了其可靠性。作者旨在通过应用最大共形原理（PMC）消除这些不确定性，从而给出更精确、理论更稳定的预言。

Method: The calculation is performed within nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD), employing the factorization formalism where the decay amplitude separates into short-distance coefficients (computed perturbatively up to N$^2$LO) and long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs). The Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) is applied to systematically eliminate renormalization-scheme and scale ambiguities by resumming large logarithms from Yukawa coupling renormalization. The LDME $\langle J/ψ({\bm ε})|ψ^{\dagger}{\bm σ}\cdot{\bm ε}χ(μ_Λ) |0\rangle$ is extracted using the experimental leptonic decay width of $J/ψ$, and combined with the PMC-improved short-distance coefficient to yield a factorization-scale-invariant result.
\n\n
计算在非相对论性QCD（NRQCD）框架内进行，采用因子化形式，将衰变振幅分解为短程系数（微扰计算至N$^2$LO阶）和长程矩阵元（LDMEs）。应用最大共形原理（PMC）系统地消除重整化方案和标度模糊性，通过对Yukawa耦合重整化产生的大对数项进行重求和实现。利用 $J/ψ$ 的实验轻子衰变宽度提取长程矩阵元 $\langle J/ψ({\bm ε})|ψ^{\dagger}{\bm σ}\cdot{\bm ε}χ(μ_Λ) |0\rangle$，并将其与经PMC改进的短程系数结合，得到一个因子化标度不变的结果。

Result: The authors obtain a factorization- and renormalization-scale-invariant prediction for the decay width: $Γ(H\to J/ψ+γ) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}$ GeV. The uncertainty combines errors from $Δα_s(m_Z)$, $ΔΓ_{J/ψ\to e^+e^-}$, $Δ\overline{m}_c(\overline{m}_c)$, and an estimate of N$^3$LO contributions via Bayesian analysis. The perturbative series shows good convergence and no residual scale dependence, marking a significant improvement over previous literature.
\n\n
作者得到了一个对因子化标度和重整化标度均不变的衰变宽度预言：$Γ(H\to J/ψ+γ) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}$ GeV。不确定度综合了来自 $Δα_s(m_Z)$、$ΔΓ_{J/ψ\to e^+e^-}$、$Δ\overline{m}_c(\overline{m}_c)$ 的误差以及通过贝叶斯分析对N$^3$LO贡献的估计。微扰级数展现出良好的收敛性且无剩余标度依赖性，相比以往文献有显著改进。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates, for the first time, that the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) can be successfully applied to exclusive heavy-quarkonium production processes to yield fixed-order predictions that are simultaneously invariant under both renormalization and factorization scale variations. This provides a robust theoretical framework for extracting fundamental parameters like the charm Yukawa coupling from rare Higgs decays.
\n\n
本工作首次证明，最大共形原理（PMC）可成功应用于独占重夸克偶素产生过程，得到在固定阶微扰计算下同时对重整化标度和因子化标度变化保持不变的预言。这为从稀有Higgs衰变中提取基本参数（如粲夸克Yukawa耦合）提供了稳健的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the \(J/ψ\) direct production mechanism in the rare exclusive Higgs decay \(H\to J/ψ+γ\) within nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD), which provides a clean probe for extracting the charm-quark Yukawa coupling to the Higgs boson. The Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) is used to remove conventional renormalization-scheme and scale ambiguities in the next-to-next-to-leading-order (N\(^2\)LO) perturbative QCD series. Large logarithmic contributions arising from Yukawa coupling renormalization are resummed, providing a reliable foundation for subsequent analyses. Using the experimentally measured leptonic decay width of \(J/ψ\) and the N\(^2\)LO perturbative result, we extract the factorization-scale-dependent long-distance matrix element \(\langle J/ψ({\bm ε})|ψ^{\dagger}{\bm σ}\cdot{\bm ε}χ(μ_Λ) |0\rangle\). Combining this with the factorization-scale-dependent short-distance coefficient, we obtain a factorization-scale-invariant decay width for the channel. Compared with earlier predictions in the literature, our fixed-order result for \(Γ(H\to J/ψ+γ)\) is more robust and precise, with good convergence and no renormalization- or factorization-scale dependence. We find \(Γ(H\to J/ψ+γ) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}\) GeV, where the uncertainty is the quadratic sum of contributions from \(Δα_s(m_Z) = \pm 0.0009\), \(ΔΓ_{J/ψ\to e^+e^-} = \pm 0.10\ \text{GeV}\), \(Δ\overline{m}_c(\overline{m}_c) = \pm 0.0046\ \text{GeV}\), and the estimated magnitude of N\(^3\)LO contributions from Bayesian analysis. This work demonstrates for the first time how the PMC can be applied to obtain fixed-order perturbative predictions that are invariant under both renormalization and factorization scale variations.

</details>


### [28] [Evaluation of Feynman integrals via numerical integration of differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05336)
*Pau Petit Rosàs*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a new numerical integrator for Feynman integrals based on solving their differential equations, featuring an improved treatment of branch cuts. It achieves fast evaluation (milliseconds to hundreds of milliseconds) in double and quadruple precision for one- and two-loop master integrals, enabling on-the-fly computation in Monte Carlo event generators and efficient grid generation for complex topologies.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于求解微分方程的新数值积分器用于Feynman积分，其对branch cuts的处理方式有所改进。该方法在double和quadruple精度下对one-loop和two-loop的master integrals实现了快速计算（毫秒至数百毫秒量级），使得在Monte Carlo事件生成器中可实时计算，并能高效生成复杂拓扑结构的网格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing numerical methods for evaluating Feynman integrals often suffer from slow performance or difficulties in handling branch cut structures, especially at higher loop orders. This limits their use in real-time applications like Monte Carlo event generators or in generating grids for complicated integral families. The authors aim to overcome these limitations by revisiting the differential equation approach with a robust numerical treatment of analytic continuations across branch cuts.
\n\n
现有的Feynman积分数值计算方法通常存在计算速度慢或难以处理branch cut结构的问题，尤其在高圈图情形下更为严重。这限制了它们在Monte Carlo事件生成器等实时应用或复杂积分族网格生成中的使用。作者希望通过重新审视微分方程方法，并结合对跨越branch cuts的解析延拓进行稳健的数值处理，以克服这些局限。

Method: The authors numerically integrate the differential equations satisfied by a basis of master integrals. Their key innovation lies in a novel algorithmic treatment of branch cuts during the integration path deformation, ensuring correct analytic continuation without requiring manual intervention. The integrator is implemented to support both double and quadruple floating-point precision and is designed for parallel execution. It avoids symbolic preprocessing and instead relies on purely numerical evaluation along deformed contours in the complex plane.
\n\n
作者对master integrals基底所满足的微分方程进行数值积分。其关键创新在于在积分路径形变过程中对branch cuts采用了新的算法处理，确保了解析延拓的正确性而无需人工干预。该积分器支持double和quadruple浮点精度，并设计为可并行执行。该方法避免了符号预处理，而是完全依赖于在复平面上形变路径上的纯数值计算。

Result: The method successfully evaluates one-loop and two-loop integral families in double precision within milliseconds and hundreds of milliseconds, respectively. It demonstrates high numerical stability and correctness across phase-space regions involving threshold crossings. The implementation shows significant speedup compared to existing tools, making it feasible to compute high-complexity topologies on demand or generate interpolation grids more efficiently.
\n\n
该方法成功地在毫秒和数百毫秒内分别完成了one-loop和two-loop积分族在double精度下的计算。它在涉及阈值穿越的相空间区域表现出高度的数值稳定性和正确性。与现有工具相比，其实现展现出显著加速，使得按需计算高复杂度拓扑结构或更高效地生成插值网格成为可能。

Conclusion: The proposed numerical integrator based on differential equations with improved branch cut handling provides a fast, stable, and parallelizable framework for evaluating Feynman integrals. It paves the way for integrating multi-loop corrections directly into Monte Carlo simulations and reduces the computational burden of precomputing grids for complex amplitudes. Future work includes extending the method to higher loops and automating initial condition determination.
\n\n
所提出的基于微分方程并改进branch cut处理的数值积分器，为Feynman积分的计算提供了一个快速、稳定且可并行化的框架。这为将多圈修正直接整合进Monte Carlo模拟铺平了道路，并减轻了为复杂振幅预先计算网格的计算负担。未来工作包括将该方法推广至更高圈图以及实现初始条件的自动化确定。

Abstract: We revisit the idea of numerically integrating the differential form of Feynman integrals. With a novel approach for the treatment of branch cuts, we develop an integrator capable of evaluating a basis of master integrals in double and quadruple precision, with significantly smaller run times than other tools. This opens the door to evaluating higher complexity Feynman integrals on the fly in Monte Carlo generators, and enables a cheaper and easy to parallelise generation of grids for the topologies with prohibitive computational times. To show its performance, we test one- and two-loop integral families, achieving evaluation times in double precision of milliseconds and hundreds of milliseconds, respectively. We comment on the results and suggest room for improvement.

</details>


### [29] [Constraints on millicharged particles from thunderstorms on the Solar system planets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05338)
*Ekaterina Dmitrieva,Petr Satunin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the production of millicharged particles (mCPs) via the Schwinger mechanism in planetary thunderstorms, using observational data to derive stringent constraints on mCP charge and mass. The strongest limits arise from Saturn’s thunderstorms: $q > 10^{-11}$ for fermionic mCPs and $q > 10^{-24}$ for bosonic mCPs, which are claimed to be the best current bounds.
\n\n
本文研究了通过Schwinger机制在行星雷暴中产生millicharged particles (mCPs) 的过程，并利用观测数据对mCP的电荷和质量施加了严格限制。最强的限制来自土星大气中的雷暴：对于费米子mCP有 $q > 10^{-11}$，对于玻色子mCP有 $q > 10^{-24}$，据称这是目前文献中最好的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to exploit naturally occurring strong electric fields in planetary thunderstorms as laboratories for probing physics beyond the Standard Model, specifically the existence of millicharged particles. Since terrestrial experiments face limitations in field strength and volume, planetary environments—especially those with intense and large-scale discharges like Saturn—offer unique opportunities to constrain mCP properties.
\n\n
动机是利用行星雷暴中自然存在的强电场作为探测超出标准模型物理（特别是millicharged particles的存在）的天然实验室。由于地面实验在电场强度和空间尺度上存在限制，而行星环境（尤其是像土星这样具有强烈且大尺度放电现象的行星）为约束mCP性质提供了独特机会。

Method: The authors compute the production rate of both fermionic and scalar millicharged particles via the Schwinger mechanism in time-dependent electric fields characteristic of thunderstorms. For scalar mCPs, they include Bose enhancement effects. They then use empirical data on electric field strengths and spatial extents from satellite missions (e.g., Cassini for Saturn) to model realistic thunderstorm conditions and translate non-observation of anomalous energy loss or discharge anomalies into lower bounds on the particle charge $q$ as a function of mass.
\n\n
作者计算了在雷暴典型时变电场中通过Schwinger机制产生的费米子和标量millicharged particles的产率。对于标量mCP，他们计入了Bose enhancement效应。随后，他们利用卫星任务（如卡西尼号对土星的观测）获得的电场强度和空间尺度的实测数据，构建现实的雷暴条件模型，并将未观测到异常能量损失或放电异常的现象转化为对粒子电荷 $q$（作为质量函数）的下限约束。

Result: The analysis yields the strongest existing constraints on millicharged particles: for fermionic mCPs, $q > 10^{-11} e$ (assuming masses below the MeV scale), and for bosonic mCPs, $q > 10^{-24} e$, both derived from Saturn’s thunderstorm data. These bounds significantly improve upon previous laboratory and astrophysical limits, particularly for very light bosonic mCPs due to Bose enhancement amplifying the Schwinger production rate.
\n\n
分析得出了目前对millicharged particles最强的限制：对于费米子mCP，在质量低于MeV量级时有 $q > 10^{-11} e$；对于玻色子mCP，有 $q > 10^{-24} e$，两者均源自土星雷暴数据。这些限制显著优于以往的实验室和天体物理限制，特别是对于极轻的玻色子mCP，因为Bose enhancement放大了Schwinger机制的产率。

Conclusion: Planetary thunderstorms, especially on gas giants like Saturn, serve as powerful natural accelerators for constraining exotic weakly coupled particles. By combining Schwinger pair production theory with in situ atmospheric measurements, this work sets new benchmarks for millicharged particle searches, demonstrating that astrophysical environments can outperform terrestrial experiments for certain parameter regimes.
\n\n
行星雷暴（尤其是土星等气态巨行星上的雷暴）可作为约束 exotic 弱耦合粒子的强大天然加速器。通过将Schwinger对产生理论与原位大气测量相结合，本工作为millicharged particle搜寻设立了新基准，表明在某些参数区间内，天体物理环境可超越地面实验的灵敏度。

Abstract: We investigate the production of millicharged particles (mCPs) by the Schwinger mechanism in thunderstorms in the atmospheres of different planets in the Solar system. We study both fermion and scalar mCPs; for scalar mCPs, we take into account the effect of Bose enhancement. We use the observational data of planetary atmospheres obtained by satellite missions to establish constraints on the charge and mass of mCP particles. The best constraints came from the observation of thunderstorms in Saturn's atmosphere: $q > 10^{-11}$ for fermionic mCP and $q > 10^{-24}$ for bosonic mCPs. These constraints are, to the best of our knowledge, the best in the literature.
