### [30] [Lepton mixing and charged lepton flavour violation from inverse seesaw with non-degenerate heavy states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05360)
*F. P. Di Meglio,C. Hagedorn*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates an inverse seesaw model with six gauge singlets (3+3) where the flavour structure is governed by discrete flavour symmetries $\Delta(3n^2)$ or $\Delta(6n^2)$, combined with CP symmetry. The Dirac mass matrix of the sterile neutrinos encodes all non-trivial flavour information, leading to three pseudo-Dirac sterile neutrino pairs with distinct masses. The study evaluates charged lepton flavour violation (cLFV) signals and finds that current experimental bounds are not very restrictive, but future experiments like Mu3E, COMET, and Mu2e will significantly probe the model.
\n\n
本文研究了一种具有六个规范单态（3+3）的逆跷跷板模型，其中味结构由离散味对称性$\Delta(3n^2)$或$\Delta(6n^2)$与CP对称性共同决定。惰性中微子的Dirac质量矩阵承载了所有非平凡的味结构，从而形成三对具有不同质量的准Dirac惰性中微子。文章评估了带电轻子味破坏（cLFV）信号，发现当前实验限制并不十分严格，但未来实验如Mu3E、COMET和Mu2e将显著探测该模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from explaining the observed pattern of light neutrino masses and mixing via the inverse seesaw mechanism while incorporating a predictive flavour structure through discrete non-Abelian flavour symmetries $\Delta(3n^2)$ or $\Delta(6n^2)$ and CP. These symmetries constrain the form of the mass matrices, linking lepton mixing angles to symmetry-breaking patterns. Additionally, the model aims to explore testable predictions for charged lepton flavour violating processes, which are sensitive probes of new physics beyond the Standard Model.
\n\n
动机源于通过逆跷跷板机制解释观测到的轻中微子质量和混合模式，同时借助离散非阿贝尔味对称性$\Delta(3n^2)$或$\Delta(6n^2)$与CP对称性引入可预测的味结构。这些对称性约束了质量矩阵的形式，将轻子混合角与对称性破缺模式联系起来。此外，该模型旨在探索带电轻子味破坏过程的可观测预言，这些过程是对标准模型之外新物理的敏感探针。

Method: The authors construct an inverse seesaw framework with three active and three sterile neutrino gauge singlets. The flavour symmetry $\Delta(3n^2)$ or $\Delta(6n^2)$, along with CP, is imposed on the Lagrangian. Residual symmetries in the charged lepton and neutrino sectors are used to fix the structure of the mass matrices. The Dirac mass matrix of the sterile states carries the full non-trivial flavour dependence, while the other mass matrices are constrained to be proportional to the identity or have simple forms. Lepton mixing is derived from the mismatch between the diagonalization matrices of the charged lepton and neutrino mass matrices. The parameter space is scanned under the requirement that the predicted PMNS mixing angles lie within their 3$\sigma$ experimental ranges. Branching ratios for cLFV processes such as $\mu \to e\gamma$, $\mu \to 3e$, $\tau \to \ell\gamma$, $\tau \to 3\ell$, and $\mu-e$ conversion in nuclei are computed using standard loop formulas involving sterile neutrino contributions.
\n\n
作者构建了一个包含三个活性中微子和三个惰性中微子规范单态的逆跷跷板框架。在拉格朗日量中施加味对称性$\Delta(3n^2)$或$\Delta(6n^2)$以及CP对称性。利用带电轻子和中微子扇区中的剩余对称性来固定质量矩阵的结构。惰性态的Dirac质量矩阵承载全部非平凡味依赖，而其他质量矩阵被约束为正比于单位矩阵或具有简单形式。轻子混合由带电轻子和中微子质量矩阵对角化矩阵之间的不匹配导出。在要求所预测的PMNS混合角落在其实验3$\sigma$范围内的条件下，对参数空间进行扫描。使用包含惰性中微子贡献的标准圈图公式计算了$\mu \to e\gamma$、$\mu \to 3e$、$\tau \to \ell\gamma$、$\tau \to 3\ell$以及原子核中$\mu-e$转换等cLFV过程的分支比。

Result: The model successfully accommodates the observed lepton mixing angles at the 3$\sigma$ level or better. The resulting sterile neutrino spectrum consists of three pseudo-Dirac pairs with generally non-degenerate masses. Current experimental limits on cLFV processes do not strongly exclude the viable parameter space. However, projected sensitivities from upcoming experiments—Mu3E (for $\mu \to 3e$), COMET and Mu2e (for $\mu-e$ conversion)—are expected to probe significant portions of the model’s parameter space, offering strong tests of the framework.
\n\n
该模型成功地在3$\sigma$水平或更高精度下拟合了观测到的轻子混合角。所得的惰性中微子谱由三对通常非简并质量的准Dirac粒子组成。当前对cLFV过程的实验限制并未强烈排除可行的参数空间。然而，即将开展的实验——Mu3E（针对$\mu \to 3e$）、COMET和Mu2e（针对$\mu-e$转换）——的预期灵敏度将探测该模型参数空间的很大一部分，从而对该框架提供强有力的检验。

Conclusion: The inverse seesaw model based on $\Delta(3n^2)$ or $\Delta(6n^2)$ flavour symmetries provides a predictive and phenomenologically viable framework for neutrino masses and mixing. While consistent with current neutrino oscillation data and cLFV bounds, it is highly testable in near-future experiments. The interplay between residual flavour symmetries, CP, and the structure of the sterile sector leads to distinctive signatures in cLFV observables, making this class of models a compelling target for next-generation intensity-frontier experiments.
\n\n
基于$\Delta(3n^2)$或$\Delta(6n^2)$味对称性的逆跷跷板模型为中微子质量和混合提供了一个具有预言能力且现象学上可行的框架。该模型与当前中微子振荡数据和cLFV限制一致，但可在近期实验中被高度检验。剩余味对称性、CP与惰性扇区结构之间的相互作用在cLFV观测量中产生独特信号，使这类模型成为下一代强度前沿实验的有力候选目标。

Abstract: We analyse an inverse seesaw scenario with 3+3 gauge singlets. The flavour structure is determined by a flavour symmetry, Delta (3 n^2) or Delta (6 n^2), n integer, and CP and their residual groups among charged leptons and the neutral states. For the latter, the Dirac mass matrix of the gauge singlets carries all non-trivial flavour structure. Consequently, the heavy sterile states form three pseudo-Dirac pairs which have in general distinct masses. We discuss the signal strength of different charged lepton flavour violating processes. Ensuring that the lepton mixing angles can be accommodated at the 3 sigma level or better, we find that the current bounds on the branching ratios of mu -> e gamma, mu -> 3 e, tau -> l gamma and tau -> 3 l, l=e, mu, as well as the rate of mu-e conversion in nuclei do not strongly constrain the considered parameter space, while the limits expected from the upcoming experiments Mu3E, COMET and Mu2e will have a relevant impact.

</details>


### [31] [Connecting Flavor and Baryon Asymmetry via Leptogenesis in Effective Froggatt-Nielsen Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05372)
*Cheshta Batra,Rusa Mandal,Kunal Rawat,Tom Tong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Summary generation failed

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: We investigate the hierarchical flavor structure of the Standard Model in a Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) framework, where the spontaneous breaking of a $U(1)_{\rm FN}$ symmetry by a complex flavon field generates fermion masses and mixing patterns through higher-dimensional operators. Extending the setup with three right-handed neutrinos (RHNs), light neutrino masses arise via the Type-I seesaw mechanism. Allowing complex FN coefficients enables a consistent description of the CKM and PMNS matrices while inducing CP-violating signatures in meson decays. Building on our previous work, where the lightest RHN acts as a viable dark matter (DM) candidate produced through freeze-in or freeze-out mechanisms, we investigate the origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The heavier RHNs generate a lepton asymmetry through out-of-equilibrium decays, including both Standard Model channels and additional flavon-induced processes in which the flavon appears as an intermediate or final-state particle. We compute the corresponding one-loop CP asymmetries and incorporate these effects in the Boltzmann equations. We show that although freeze-in and freeze-out DM production occur in two qualitatively distinct regions of the FN symmetry-breaking scale $v_φ$, successful thermal leptogenesis can be achieved in both regimes. In the large-$v_φ$ (freeze-in-compatible) region the results approach the standard leptogenesis limit, while in the freeze-out-compatible region the lower value of $v_φ$ implies lighter RHNs, requiring resonant enhancement. This tightly constrained framework, in which $v_φ$ simultaneously controls RHN masses and the interaction strengths of the flavon and DM sectors, provides a predictive and unified description of flavor hierarchies, neutrino masses, CP violation, dark matter, and baryogenesis within a single effective theory.

### [32] [Accelerating Feynman Integral Evaluation by Avoiding Contour Deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05444)
*Stephen P. Jones,Anton Olsson,Thomas Stone*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a novel method to rewrite dimensionally regulated Feynman parameter integrals in the Minkowski regime as sums of real, positive integrands with complex prefactors, bypassing the need for contour deformation and achieving up to several orders of magnitude speedup in numerical integration compared to pySecDec. The approach is generalized to arbitrary Feynman integrals—including those with massive propagators—via an improved resolution procedure using Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition.
\n\n
本文提出了一种新方法，将Minkowski区域中维度正规化的Feynman参数积分重写为实正被积函数之和乘以复数前因子，从而避免了轮廓变形（contour deformation）的需要，在数值积分中相比pySecDec实现了高达几个数量级的加速。该方法通过使用Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition算法改进的resolution过程，推广到任意Feynman积分，包括含质量传播子的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Contour deformation is a major bottleneck in the numerical evaluation of Feynman integrals in the Minkowski regime due to its algorithmic complexity and computational cost. The authors aim to eliminate this step by reformulating the integrals into a form that retains real, positive integration domains while isolating all complex structure into analytic prefactors, thereby enabling faster and more stable numerical integration.
\n\n
在Minkowski区域中，Feynman积分的数值计算因轮廓变形（contour deformation）的算法复杂性和计算开销而成为主要瓶颈。作者旨在通过将积分重构为实正积分域的形式，并将所有复结构隔离到解析前因子中，从而消除这一步骤，实现更快、更稳定的数值积分。

Method: The method rewrites dimensionally regulated Feynman parameter integrals as a sum over sectors where each sector’s integrand is real and positive, multiplied by a complex prefactor derived from the analytic structure of the original integral. This avoids the need for contour deformation. The authors implement two explicit examples to illustrate the technique. To extend applicability to general Feynman integrals (including those with massive propagators), they enhance the resolution of singularities using the Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition (GCAD) algorithm, which systematically partitions the integration domain to isolate divergences.
\n\n
该方法将维度正规化的Feynman参数积分重写为若干sector之和，每个sector的被积函数均为实且正，乘以一个由原积分解析结构导出的复数前因子，从而避免轮廓变形。作者通过两个具体例子展示该技术。为将方法推广至一般Feynman积分（包括含质量传播子的情形），他们采用Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition（GCAD）算法改进奇点resolution过程，系统性地划分积分区域以隔离发散。

Result: The proposed method achieves performance improvements of up to several orders of magnitude compared to the contour deformation implementation in pySecDec for the tested examples. It successfully handles integrals in the Minkowski regime without requiring complex contour shifts, and the GCAD-based resolution procedure enables application to arbitrary topologies, including those with massive internal lines.
\n\n
所提出的方法在测试案例中相比pySecDec中的轮廓变形实现获得了高达几个数量级的性能提升。该方法成功处理Minkowski区域中的积分而无需复平面上的轮廓移动，且基于GCAD的resolution过程使其可应用于任意拓扑结构，包括含质量内线的情形。

Conclusion: The reformulation of Feynman integrals into real-positive integrands with complex prefactors provides a robust and efficient alternative to contour deformation for numerical evaluation in the Minkowski regime. Coupled with the Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition algorithm, the method is universally applicable to any Feynman integral, offering significant computational advantages for high-precision calculations in quantum field theory.
\n\n
将Feynman积分重构为实正被积函数与复数前因子的组合，为Minkowski区域中数值计算提供了一种稳健高效的轮廓变形替代方案。结合Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition算法，该方法可普遍适用于任意Feynman积分，为量子场论中的高精度计算带来显著的计算优势。

Abstract: We describe our method for rewriting dimensionally regulated Feynman parameter integrals in the Minkowski regime as a sum of real, positive integrands multiplied by complex prefactors. This representation eliminates the need for a contour deformation, which is one of the main computational bottlenecks in numerical integration. We demonstrate clearly how the method works on two examples, and benchmark the performance against contour deformation as implemented in pySecDec, where we observe performance gains of up to several orders of magnitude. We describe an improvement in the resolution procedure using the Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition algorithm, which generalises our method to any Feynman integral, including those with massive propagators.

### [33] [Quantum field theories with many fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04481)
*Ludo Fraser-Taliente*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This thesis explores large-$N$ melonic quantum field theories (QFTs)—including SYK-like models, tensor models, and vector models—using the large-$N$ limit to access strongly-coupled regimes. It introduces $\tilde{F}$-extremization as a method to solve such theories in the infrared (IR), where conformal field theories (CFTs) are determined by maximizing the number of degrees of freedom (measured by $\tilde{F}$) under interaction constraints. The quartic Yukawa tensor model in continuous dimension serves as a concrete example, exhibiting multiple fixed points, stability properties, and an operator spectrum consistent across large-$N$ and $\\epsilon$-expansion methods.
\n\n
本论文研究大$N$梅洛尼克量子场论（QFT）——包括SYK类模型、张量模型和矢量模型——利用大$N$极限探索强耦合区域。文中提出$\tilde{F}$-极值化方法，用于求解红外（IR）极限下的此类理论，其中共形场论（CFT）由在相互作用约束下最大化自由度数目（以$\tilde{F}$度量）唯一确定。连续维度下的四次Yukawa张量模型作为具体例子，展现出多重不动点、稳定性特性及算符谱，这些结果在大$N$展开与$\epsilon$展开之间一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand strongly-coupled quantum field theories, which are generally intractable with standard perturbative methods. The large-$N$ limit offers a solvable regime where diagrams simplify due to dominance of melonic graphs. Melonic QFTs—including Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK)-like models, tensor models, and certain vector models—exhibit emergent conformal symmetry in the IR and serve as tractable laboratories for studying non-perturbative physics, quantum chaos, and holography. The thesis aims to develop systematic tools to analyze and solve such theories, particularly in their conformal limits.
\n\n
动机在于理解强耦合量子场论，这类理论通常无法用标准微扰方法处理。大$N$极限提供了一个可解区域，其中费曼图因梅洛尼克图（melonic graphs）主导而大幅简化。梅洛尼克QFT——包括Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）类模型、张量模型和某些矢量模型——在红外区表现出涌现的共形对称性，为研究非微扰物理、量子混沌和全息对偶提供了可处理的理论平台。本文旨在发展系统性工具以分析并求解此类理论，特别是在其共形极限下。

Method: The paper employs the large-$N$ expansion, focusing on melonic dominance, and introduces $\tilde{F}$-extremization: a variational principle that determines the IR conformal fixed point by extremizing $\tilde{F}$, the universal part of the free energy on a sphere (or its analytic continuation). This method leverages the fact that in melonic theories, the IR CFT is uniquely fixed by maximizing the number of effective degrees of freedom subject to the constraint imposed by interactions. The approach is illustrated via two solvable toy models (a 0D theory and a generalized free field flow) to demonstrate large-$N$ simplifications and renormalization group (RG) techniques. The quartic Yukawa tensor model in $d = 4 - \\epsilon$ dimensions is then solved using both large-$N$ and $\\epsilon$-expansion methods, with operator spectra and fixed-point stability analyzed through consistency between these complementary approaches.
\n\n
本文采用大$N$展开，聚焦于梅洛尼克图主导机制，并引入$\tilde{F}$-极值化方法：一种变分原理，通过极值化球面上自由能的普适部分$\tilde{F}$来确定红外共形不动点。该方法基于梅洛尼克理论中一个关键事实——红外CFT由在相互作用约束下最大化有效自由度数目唯一确定。作者通过两个可解玩具模型（零维理论和广义自由场流）阐明大$N$简化机制与重整化群（RG）技术。随后，在$d = 4 - \\epsilon$维中求解四次Yukawa张量模型，结合大$N$展开与$\epsilon$展开两种方法，通过二者的一致性分析算符谱与不动点稳定性。

Result: The key results include: (1) formulation of $\tilde{F}$-extremization as a general solution method for large-$N$ melonic QFTs in the strongly-coupled IR limit; (2) demonstration that the IR CFT is completely fixed by maximizing $\tilde{F}$ under a simple interaction-induced constraint; (3) explicit solution of the quartic Yukawa tensor model in continuous dimension, revealing multiple interacting fixed points; (4) analysis of fixed-point stability and operator spectrum, showing agreement between large-$N$ and $\\epsilon$-expansion predictions; (5) confirmation that melonic CFTs exhibit universal features—existence of multiple fixed points, specific spectral structures, and stability governed by interaction topology.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 提出$\tilde{F}$-极值化作为大$N$梅洛尼克QFT在强耦合红外极限下的通用求解方法；(2) 证明红外CFT完全由在相互作用诱导的简单约束下最大化$\tilde{F}$所确定；(3) 显式求解连续维度下的四次Yukawa张量模型，揭示多个相互作用不动点；(4) 分析不动点稳定性与算符谱，显示大$N$展开与$\epsilon$展开预测的一致性；(5) 确认梅洛尼克CFT具有普适特征——存在多重不动点、特定谱结构，以及由相互作用拓扑决定的稳定性。

Conclusion: The thesis establishes $\tilde{F}$-extremization as a powerful and general framework for solving large-$N$ melonic QFTs in their conformal infrared phases. It underscores the remarkable simplicity of these strongly-coupled fixed points, which are entirely constrained by entropy-like maximization of degrees of freedom ($\tilde{F}$) and interaction structure. The success of this approach in the quartic Yukawa model suggests broad applicability across melonic theories. Future work includes extending $\tilde{F}$-extremization to fermionic or supersymmetric melonic models, exploring connections to holography, and investigating dynamical aspects beyond fixed points.
\n\n
本文确立了$\tilde{F}$-极值化作为求解大$N$梅洛尼克QFT在共形红外相中的强大通用框架。它强调了这些强耦合不动点的显著简洁性——完全由自由度（$\tilde{F}$）的类熵最大化与相互作用结构所约束。该方法在四次Yukawa模型中的成功表明其在梅洛尼克理论中具有广泛适用性。未来工作包括将$\tilde{F}$-极值化推广至费米型或超对称梅洛尼克模型、探索与全息对偶的联系，以及研究超越不动点的动力学行为。

Abstract: The large-$N$ quantum field theories provide a window into the regime of strongly-coupled physics. Our principal object of study in this thesis is the large-$N$ family of melonic QFTs, which contain the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev-like models, tensor models, and vector models. We begin with a review of this limit of a large number of degrees of freedom (large-$N$) as an approach to the solution of QFTs. Two toy models are used to clarify this approach: a zero-dimensional field theory and the flow of a generalized free field theory. Both models are solvable, and so we can explicitly demonstrate: using the former, the simplifications at large $N$; using the latter, the tools used to study scale-dependence of physics -- the renormalization group. We develop $\tilde{F}$-extremization, a simple method of solution for an arbitrary large-$N$ melonic QFT in its strongly-coupled limit. The infrared conformal field theories show remarkable simplicity, in that they are entirely solved by the requirement that they have as many degrees of freedom as possible, up to a simple constraint arising from the interaction between the fields. We measure the number of degrees of freedom of the conformal infrared theory via $\tilde{F}$, the universal part of the free energy. We then present the example of the quartic Yukawa model in continuous dimension. This model is considered as a tensor field theory, and solved for its conformal limit; we then illustrate its multiplicity of fixed points and their stability, as well as its operator spectrum, matching the data between the large-$N$ and dimensional expansions. These features reflect general characteristics of melonic conformal field theories: their existence, stability, and spectral characteristics. We conclude with future directions of exploration for the melonic theories.

</details>


### [34] [Higher-Spin and Higher-Point Constraints on Stringy Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04485)
*Ivano Basile,Grant N. Remmen,Georgina Staudt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper uses multiparticle factorization and soft kinematics to constrain possible deformations of tree-level open string and superstring amplitudes. It shows that the Regge intercept is uniquely fixed by seven-point factorization, matching bosonic string theory, and proves that certain satellite deformations of four-point superstring amplitudes are ruled out by unitarity due to the infinite higher-spin tower.
\n\n
本文利用多粒子因子化和软动学来约束树图级开弦和超弦振幅的可能形变。研究表明，通过七点因子化可唯一确定Regge截距，与玻色弦理论精确匹配，并证明由于无限高自旋塔的存在，某些四点超弦振幅的卫星形变被幺正性排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test the rigidity of string theory by exploring whether its scattering amplitudes can be consistently deformed while preserving fundamental physical principles like unitarity, locality, and analyticity. The authors aim to understand how the infinite tower of higher-spin states in string theory constrains low-energy effective descriptions and excludes alternative theories with only finite particle content.
\n\n
动机在于通过探索弦理论散射振幅是否能在保持幺正性、局域性和解析性等基本物理原理的前提下被一致地形变，从而检验弦理论的刚性。作者旨在理解弦理论中无限高自旋态塔如何约束低能有效描述，并排除仅含有限粒子内容的替代理论。

Method: The authors apply multiparticle factorization constraints on Koba-Nielsen-type amplitudes up to the second excited level, assuming minimal degeneracy among intermediate states of identical spin. They use seven-point factorization to fix the Regge intercept. For superstrings, they analyze deformations with massless external states under arbitrary spectral degeneracy using soft kinematics, and derive multipositivity bounds in the large-level limit by accounting for the full tower of higher-spin resonances. These bounds are then applied to Gross's family of satellite amplitudes.
\n\n
作者对Koba-Nielsen型振幅施加多粒子因子化约束，假设相同自旋中间态在第二激发能级内具有最小简并度，并利用七点因子化固定Regge截距。对于超弦，他们在任意谱简并条件下，利用软动学分析具有无质量外态的形变，并通过计入完整的高自旋共振塔，在大能级极限下导出多重正定性（multipositivity）界。这些界随后被应用于Gross提出的卫星振幅族。

Result: The Regge intercept is uniquely determined to match that of the bosonic string via seven-point factorization. Novel constraints on worldsheet integrand deformations are derived. In the superstring case, multipositivity bounds at leading and subleading orders in the large-level expansion rule out the simplest factorizable satellite deformation of four-point amplitudes, demonstrating that such deformations violate unitarity when the infinite higher-spin tower is included.
\n\n
通过七点因子化，Regge截距被唯一确定为与玻色弦一致。作者还导出了关于世界面积分元（worldsheet integrand）形变的新约束。在超弦情形中，大能级展开的领头阶和次领头阶多重正定性界排除了四点振幅中最简单的可因子化卫星形变，表明当包含无限高自旋塔时，此类形变违反幺正性。

Conclusion: The infinite tower of higher-spin string excitations imposes stringent consistency conditions that severely restrict possible deformations of string amplitudes. This rigidity supports the idea that string theory is essentially unique among consistent theories of quantum gravity with higher-spin states, and cannot be mimicked by effective field theories with only finitely many fields.
\n\n
无限高自旋弦激发态塔施加了严格的自洽条件，极大限制了弦振幅的可能形变。这种刚性支持了如下观点：在包含高自旋态的自洽量子引力理论中，弦理论本质上是唯一的，无法被仅含有限多场的有效场论所模拟。

Abstract: We employ multiparticle factorization to constrain deformations of tree-level open string amplitudes. Assuming minimal degeneracy among intermediate states of the same spin up through the second excited level, we find that the Regge intercept among all amplitudes of the Koba-Nielsen type can be uniquely fixed using seven-point factorization, precisely matching the bosonic string. Moreover, we produce novel constraints on deformations of the worldsheet integrand. We then turn to deformations of superstrings, with massless external states and arbitrary spectral degeneracy, using soft kinematics. Accounting for the infinite tower of higher-spin resonances, we obtain novel multipositivity bounds to leading and subleading order in the large-level limit. We apply these bounds to the simplest factorizable satellite deformation in the family of amplitudes found by Gross, showing that any deformation of four-point string amplitudes of this type is forbidden by unitarity. Our results reinforce the folklore that the higher-spin tower of string excitations is dramatically more rigid than any finite number of species.

### [35] [Nonabelian Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture and Monopole Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04494)
*Matthew Reece,Tom Rudelius*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates violations of the Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC) in heterotic string orbifold compactifications and confirms a recent hypothesis: whenever LWGC is violated, fractionally charged confined monopoles are present. It shows that superextremal particles populate the charge lattice of a quotient gauge group $G/K$, where $K$ is a discrete subgroup of the center $Z(G)$, and confined monopoles occupy the dual magnetic lattice. This implies LWGC violation is impossible for gauge groups with trivial centers and is bounded by the maximal order of the center in nonabelian theories.
\n\n
本文研究了杂化弦（heterotic string）轨道折叠紧致化（orbifold compactifications）中Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture（LWGC）的破坏情形，并验证了一个近期假说：每当LWGC被破坏时，必然存在分数电荷的禁闭磁单极子（confined monopoles）。研究表明，超极端粒子（superextremal particles）填充商群 $G/K$ 的电荷格点，其中 $K$ 是规范群中心 $Z(G)$ 的一个离散子群，而禁闭磁单极子则占据 $G/K$ 的对偶磁荷格点。这表明对于中心平凡的规范群，LWGC破坏不可能发生；更一般地，在非阿贝尔规范理论中，LWGC破坏的程度受中心最大阶数的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the existence of counterexamples to the Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC)—a refinement of the Weak Gravity Conjecture (WGC) requiring superextremal particles at every point of the electric charge lattice $Γ$. While most quantum gravity theories satisfy LWGC, known violations raise questions about their structural origin. A recent conjecture posits that such violations must involve fractionally charged confined monopoles. The authors aim to test this hypothesis in explicit string theory constructions, specifically toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string, which exhibit LWGC violation in both abelian and nonabelian sectors.
\n\n
动机源于Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture（LWGC）——即Weak Gravity Conjecture（WGC）的一个精细化版本，要求在电荷格点 $Γ$ 的每个格点上都存在超极端粒子（superextremal particles）——存在反例这一事实。尽管大多数量子引力理论满足LWGC，但已知的破坏情形引发了对其结构起源的疑问。近期一个猜想提出，此类破坏必然涉及分数电荷的禁闭磁单极子（confined monopoles）。作者旨在通过具体的弦论构造（特别是杂化弦的环面轨道折叠紧致化）来检验这一假说，这些构造在阿贝尔和非阿贝尔规范扇区中均表现出LWGC破坏。

Method: The authors analyze explicit toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string that violate the LWGC. They examine the structure of the gauge group $G$, its center $Z(G)$, and identify a discrete subgroup $K \subseteq Z(G)$. They then study the charge lattice of the quotient group $G/K$ and compare it with the spectrum of superextremal particles and confined monopoles. By mapping the locations of these states in both electric and magnetic charge lattices, they verify whether the hypothesized correlation between LWGC violation and the presence of fractionally charged confined monopoles holds.
\n\n
作者分析了明确违反LWGC的杂化弦环面轨道折叠紧致化模型。他们考察规范群 $G$ 及其中心 $Z(G)$ 的结构，并识别出一个离散子群 $K \subseteq Z(G)$。随后，他们研究商群 $G/K$ 的电荷格点结构，并与超极端粒子谱和禁闭磁单极子谱进行对比。通过将这些态在电荷与磁荷格点中的位置进行映射，验证了LWGC破坏与分数电荷禁闭磁单极子存在之间的假定关联。

Result: In all examined cases of LWGC-violating heterotic orbifolds, there exists a discrete subgroup $K \subseteq Z(G)$ such that: (1) superextremal particles exist at every site of the electric charge lattice of $G/K$, and (2) confined monopoles exist at every site of the corresponding magnetic charge lattice. This confirms the hypothesis linking LWGC violation to fractionally charged confined monopoles. Moreover, the results imply that LWGC violation cannot occur if $Z(G)$ is trivial, and in nonabelian theories, the extent of violation is constrained by the maximal order of elements in $Z(G)$.
\n\n
在所有考察的LWGC破坏型杂化轨道折叠模型中，均存在一个离散子群 $K \subseteq Z(G)$，使得：(1) 超极端粒子存在于商群 $G/K$ 电荷格点的每个格点上；(2) 禁闭磁单极子存在于对应磁荷格点的每个格点上。这证实了LWGC破坏与分数电荷禁闭磁单极子之间存在关联的假说。此外，结果表明，若 $Z(G)$ 平凡，则LWGC破坏不可能发生；在非阿贝尔理论中，破坏程度受 $Z(G)$ 中元素最大阶数的限制。

Conclusion: The study provides strong evidence that LWGC violation in consistent quantum gravity theories is not arbitrary but tightly linked to the global structure of the gauge group—specifically, its center. The presence of fractionally charged confined monopoles appears to be a necessary feature of such violations. This leads to a refined understanding of the WGC landscape: LWGC may fail only when the gauge group admits a nontrivial center, and the degree of failure is quantitatively bounded by the center’s structure. These findings support the idea that consistency conditions in quantum gravity encode deep constraints on gauge theory data.
\n\n
本研究提供了有力证据，表明在自洽的量子引力理论中，LWGC破坏并非任意，而是与规范群的整体结构（尤其是其中心）紧密关联。分数电荷禁闭磁单极子的存在似乎是此类破坏的必要特征。这深化了我们对WGC景观的理解：LWGC仅当中心非平凡时才可能失效，且失效程度由中心结构定量限制。这些发现支持如下观点：量子引力中的自洽性条件对规范理论数据施加了深刻的约束。

Abstract: Within the known landscape of quantum gravity, most theories satisfy the Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC), which requires a superextremal particle at every site in the electric charge lattice $Γ$. However, counterexamples to the LWGC exist, and it was recently hypothesized that such counterexamples necessarily feature fractionally charged confined monopoles. In this work, we verify this hypothesis in toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string, which notably feature LWGC violation in both the abelian and nonabelian gauge sectors. In all the cases we consider, there exists a discrete subgroup of the center of the gauge group $K \subseteq Z(G)$ such that superextremal particles exist at every site in the charge lattice of the quotient group $G/K$, while (confined) monopoles exist at all sites in the magnetic charge lattice of $G/K$. This suggests that LWGC violation cannot occur for gauge groups with trivial centers, and more generally the degree of LWGC violation in a nonabelian gauge theory is bounded in terms of the maximal order of the center.

</details>


### [36] [From BPS geodesics to mode-driven dynamics in the scattering of multiple BPS vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04495)
*Alberto Alonso-Izquierdo,Maximilian Bachmaier,Andrzej Wereszczynski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates how the excitation of a massive bound mode modifies geodesic motion in the 3- and 4-vortex sectors of the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling. While BPS geodesics with enhanced symmetry remain invariant, generic collisions (e.g., 1–2 or 2–2 vortex head-on) exhibit significant deviations from BPS trajectories due to mode-generated forces, leading to enhanced chaos in final-state formation.
\n\n
本文研究了在临界耦合下，Abelian-Higgs 模型中 3- 和 4-涡旋系统中，大质量束缚模的激发如何修正测地线运动。具有增强对称性的 BPS 解对应的测地线保持不变，但在一般情形下（例如轴对称的 1- 和 2-涡旋或两个 2-涡旋的对心碰撞），由于模诱导力（mode-generated force）的作用，涡旋轨迹显著偏离 BPS 测地线，从而增强了末态形成的混沌行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding the dynamics of vortices beyond the moduli space approximation in the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling, where BPS solutions exist. Specifically, the authors aim to explore how internal excitations—namely massive bound modes—affect low-energy vortex scattering, which is typically modeled by geodesic motion on the moduli space. This addresses the limitations of the naive geodesic approximation when non-BPS deformations are present.
\n\n
动机源于在临界耦合的 Abelian-Higgs 模型中，超越模空间近似（moduli space approximation）来理解涡旋动力学，其中存在 BPS 解。作者特别关注内部激发——即大质量束缚模——如何影响通常由模空间上的测地线运动描述的低能涡旋散射。这解决了当存在非 BPS 形变时，朴素测地线近似方法的局限性。

Method: The authors employ a perturbative analysis around BPS configurations, incorporating the backreaction of a massive bound mode on the vortex dynamics. They compute the mode frequency along geodesics and derive an effective force—the mode-generated force—proportional to the gradient of this frequency. This modifies the standard geodesic equation on the moduli space: $$\\frac{D^2 q^i}{dt^2} = -g^{ij} \\partial_j \\omega(q),$$ where $\\omega(q)$ is the mode frequency and $g_{ij}$ the metric on moduli space. Numerical integration of these corrected trajectories is performed for specific multi-vortex sectors (3- and 4-vortex).
\n\n
作者采用围绕 BPS 构型的微扰分析，将大质量束缚模对涡旋动力学的反作用纳入考虑。他们沿测地线计算模频率，并导出一个有效力——模诱导力——正比于该频率的梯度。这修正了模空间上的标准测地线方程：$$\\frac{D^2 q^i}{dt^2} = -g^{ij} \\partial_j \\omega(q),$$ 其中 $\\omega(q)$ 为模频率，$g_{ij}$ 为模空间度规。针对特定的多涡旋系统（3- 和 4-涡旋），对这些修正轨迹进行了数值积分。

Result: The study finds that geodesics preserving enhanced symmetry (e.g., coincident vortices with rotational symmetry) are unaffected by the massive mode, as $\\nabla \\omega = 0$ along those paths. However, in generic asymmetric collisions—such as head-on scattering between a 1-vortex and a 2-vortex or between two 2-vortices—the mode frequency varies spatially, generating a non-zero force that significantly deflects trajectories from the BPS geodesics. This deviation amplifies sensitivity to initial conditions, thereby enhancing chaotic behavior in the final configuration.
\n\n
研究发现，保持增强对称性的测地线（例如具有旋转对称性的重合涡旋）不受大质量模的影响，因为在这些路径上 $\\nabla \\omega = 0$。然而，在一般的非对称碰撞中——如 1-涡旋与 2-涡旋或两个 2-涡旋的对心散射——模频率在空间上变化，产生非零力，使轨迹显著偏离 BPS 测地线。这种偏离放大了对初值的敏感性，从而增强了末态构型中的混沌行为。

Conclusion: The inclusion of massive bound mode excitations goes beyond the standard moduli space approximation and reveals richer dynamical structure in vortex scattering. While symmetric BPS trajectories are robust, generic scattering processes are highly sensitive to internal degrees of freedom, leading to pronounced deviations and increased chaos. This underscores the necessity of incorporating mode dynamics for accurate modeling of non-BPS vortex interactions.
\n\n
引入大质量束缚模的激发超越了标准的模空间近似，揭示了涡旋散射中更丰富的动力学结构。尽管对称的 BPS 轨迹是稳健的，但一般的散射过程对内部自由度高度敏感，导致显著偏离并增强混沌。这凸显了在精确建模非 BPS 涡旋相互作用时，必须纳入模动力学。

Abstract: We analyze how the geodesic motion in the 3- and 4-vortex sectors of the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling is deformed by the excitation of a massive bound mode. We find that the geodesics corresponding to BPS solutions with enhanced symmetry remain unchanged, although the direction of the actual motion depends on the mode-generated force, i.e., a force arising from the change of the mode frequency along the geodesic. In a generic case, for example in head-on collisions between the axially symmetric 1- and 2-vortex or between two 2-vortices, the vortex trajectories can differ strongly from the BPS geodesic. This enhances the chaotic behavior in the formation of the final state.

### [37] [On curvature corrections for field theory cosmic strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05243)
*Josu C. Aurrekoetxea,Jose J. Blanco-Pillado,Alberto García Martín-Caro,J. M. Queiruga*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We derive the low-energy effective action for cosmic strings in the Abelian-Higgs model, showing that curvature corrections vanish when only translational Goldstone modes are included. Including massive soliton fluctuations, we find leading curvature effects arise via coupling to the worldsheet Ricci scalar. Lattice simulations with Adaptive Mesh Refinement confirm the effective theory’s predictions and reveal a parametric instability transferring energy from massive modes to Goldstone modes.
\n\n
我们推导了Abelian-Higgs模型中宇宙弦的低能有效作用量，表明当仅保留平移Goldstone模时，曲率修正项消失。引入孤子剖面的高能涨落后，发现主导的曲率效应通过这些重模与世界面Ricci标量的耦合产生。采用自适应网格细化（Adaptive Mesh Refinement）的格点模拟验证了有效理论的预测，并揭示了一种参数不稳定性，将能量从重模转移至Goldstone模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the low-energy dynamics of cosmic strings is crucial for modeling their role in cosmology and high-energy physics. While effective field theory (EFT) approaches often assume generic curvature corrections, a first-principles derivation from the underlying solitonic field theory—specifically the Abelian-Higgs model—is needed to determine whether such corrections actually arise. Moreover, incorporating massive excitations beyond the Goldstone modes is essential for capturing richer string dynamics, including possible instabilities and energy transfer mechanisms.
\n\n
理解宇宙弦的低能动力学对于建模其在宇宙学和高能物理中的作用至关重要。尽管有效场论（EFT）方法通常假设存在一般的曲率修正项，但仍需从底层孤子场论（特别是Abelian-Higgs模型）出发进行第一性原理推导，以确定此类修正是否真实存在。此外，纳入Goldstone模之外的重激发态对捕捉更丰富的弦动力学（包括可能的不稳定性与能量转移机制）至关重要。

Method: Starting from the Abelian-Higgs Lagrangian in flat spacetime, the authors perform a systematic expansion around the static vortex solution to derive the effective action on the string worldsheet. They separate massless translational Goldstone modes from massive profile fluctuations. Using constrained path integrals or matching techniques, they integrate out high-energy modes to obtain the low-energy EFT. The leading curvature-dependent terms are identified through couplings between massive modes and the worldsheet Ricci scalar $R^{(2)}$. Numerical validation is performed via lattice simulations of the full nonlinear field equations using Adaptive Mesh Refinement (AMR) to resolve both core and large-scale string dynamics.
\n\n
作者从平直时空中的Abelian-Higgs拉格朗日量出发，围绕静态涡旋解进行系统展开，以推导弦世界面上的有效作用量。他们将无质量的平移Goldstone模与有质量的剖面涨落分离。通过约束路径积分或匹配技术，积分掉高能模以获得低能EFT。主导的曲率依赖项通过重模与世界面Ricci标量$R^{(2)}$的耦合被识别出来。数值验证通过使用自适应网格细化（AMR）对完整非线性场方程进行格点模拟，以同时解析弦芯与大尺度弦动力学。

Result: The analysis shows that the Nambu-Goto action receives no intrinsic curvature corrections at leading order when only Goldstone modes are retained, confirming its robustness as the universal low-energy description. When massive soliton fluctuations are included, the leading correction takes the form $\\int d^2\\sigma \\sqrt{-g} \\, \\phi^2 R^{(2)}$, where $\\phi$ represents the massive mode. Lattice simulations confirm the effective equations of motion derived from this extended action and demonstrate a parametric resonance instability: energy injected into massive modes decays into Goldstone modes via curvature-mediated interactions.
\n\n
分析表明，当仅保留Goldstone模时，Nambu-Goto作用量在领头阶不存在内禀曲率修正项，证实了其作为普适低能描述的稳健性。当包含孤子重涨落后，主导修正项形式为$\\int d^2\\sigma \\sqrt{-g} \\, \\phi^2 R^{(2)}$，其中$\\phi$代表重模。格点模拟验证了由此扩展作用量导出的有效运动方程，并揭示了一种参数共振不稳定性：注入重模的能量通过曲率介导的相互作用衰变为Goldstone模。

Conclusion: The effective theory of cosmic strings derived directly from the Abelian-Higgs model validates the Nambu-Goto action as the correct leading-order description and clarifies the origin of higher-order corrections. Curvature effects enter only through interactions with massive worldsheet fields, not as intrinsic geometric terms. This framework provides a controlled EFT for cosmic strings with predictive power for nonlinear dynamics and energy cascade phenomena, confirmed by first-principles numerical simulations.
\n\n
直接从Abelian-Higgs模型导出的宇宙弦有效理论验证了Nambu-Goto作用量作为正确领头阶描述的地位，并阐明了高阶修正的起源。曲率效应仅通过与世界面上重场的相互作用引入，而非作为内禀几何项。该框架为宇宙弦提供了一个受控的有效场论（EFT），对非线性动力学和能量级联现象具有预测能力，并已通过第一性原理数值模拟得到证实。

Abstract: We present a combined analytical and numerical study of the effective action of field theory cosmic strings in the Abelian-Higgs model in flat space. Starting directly from the underlying solitonic field theory description, we provide a systematic derivation of the low energy effective action and present evidence for the absence of nontrivial curvature correction terms when only the translational Goldstone modes are retained. Using this framework, we extend the effective theory to include higher energy fluctuations of the soliton profile, which map to massive degrees of freedom propagating on the worldsheet. We show that the leading curvature contribution enters only through the coupling between these massive modes and the worldsheet Ricci scalar. We validate the resulting effective theory via lattice simulations of the full field theory equations of motion in flat space, implemented with Adaptive Mesh Refinement to capture the string dynamics across different scales. The numerical simulations confirm the dynamics obtained using the effective action in its validity range. Furthermore, they also demonstrate the existence of the predicted parametric instability of excited strings that drives the transfer of energy from massive excitations to the Goldstone sector.

### [38] [Spin Chains from large-$N$ QCD at strong coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04506)
*David Berenstein,Hiroki Kawai*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper reformulates large $N$ QCD in the strong coupling limit as constrained 1D spin chains derived from the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian, revealing integrable subsectors but non-integrability of the full model due to zigzag symmetry constraints; this framework yields a reasonable estimate of the roughening transition and extends partially to higher dimensions.
\n\n
本文将强耦合极限下的大$N$ QCD通过Kogut-Susskind哈密顿量重新表述为受约束的一维自旋链模型，揭示了存在大量可积子 sector，但完整模型因禁闭弦的zigzag对称性所引入的约束而不可积；该框架通过对可积子 sector 的一阶解析结果外推，合理估计了粗糙化相变点，并部分推广至高维情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the non-perturbative dynamics of large $N$ QCD in the strong coupling regime remains a central challenge. The authors aim to leverage the mapping of lattice gauge theory to quantum spin systems to explore integrability structures and phase transitions—particularly the roughening transition of confining strings—by exploiting the simplifications available at strong coupling and large $N$.
\n\n
理解大$N$ QCD在强耦合区域的非微扰动力学仍是核心挑战。作者旨在利用格点规范理论到量子自旋系统的映射，探索可积性结构与相变（特别是禁闭弦的粗糙化相变），借助强耦合与大$N$极限下可获得的简化。

Method: The authors start from the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian for lattice QCD in the strong coupling limit and perform a reformulation into an effective one-dimensional spin chain with local Hilbert spaces constrained by Gauss’s law. They analyze the integrability of this system using Bethe ansatz techniques, identifying subsectors where zigzag symmetry constraints are absent or inactive, which remain solvable. The roughening transition is estimated by extrapolating first-order perturbative results from these integrable subsectors.
\n\n
作者从强耦合极限下的Kogut-Susskind哈密顿量出发，将其重构为受Gauss定律约束的有效一维自旋链。他们使用Bethe ansatz方法分析该系统的可积性，识别出不含或不受zigzag对称性约束的子 sector，这些子 sector 保持可解性。通过外推这些可积子 sector 的一阶微扰结果，估计粗糙化相变点。

Result: The full spin chain derived from large $N$ QCD is shown to be non-integrable when analyzed via Bethe ansatz, due to constraints imposed by the zigzag symmetry of confining strings. However, numerous subsectors—where such constraints are relaxed—are integrable. Using these integrable sectors, the authors obtain a first-principles estimate of the roughening transition point that aligns well with known results. The approach is extended to higher spatial dimensions, where similar integrable subsectors exist.
\n\n
通过Bethe ansatz分析表明，由大$N$ QCD导出的完整自旋链因禁闭弦的zigzag对称性所施加的约束而不可积。然而，大量约束被放松的子 sector 是可积的。作者利用这些可积子 sector，基于第一性原理外推得到粗糙化相变点的估计，与已知结果吻合良好。该方法被推广至更高空间维度，其中也存在类似的可积子 sector。

Conclusion: While the complete spin chain representation of strong-coupling large $N$ QCD is not integrable, the existence of integrable subsectors provides a powerful analytical handle to study non-perturbative phenomena like the roughening transition. The breakdown of integrability is directly tied to physical constraints from string zigzag symmetry, highlighting the interplay between gauge symmetry, topology, and quantum integrability in lattice gauge theories.
\n\n
尽管强耦合大$N$ QCD的完整自旋链表示不可积，但可积子 sector 的存在为研究粗糙化相变等非微扰现象提供了有力的解析工具。可积性的破缺直接源于弦的zigzag对称性所导致的物理约束，凸显了格点规范理论中规范对称性、拓扑与量子可积性之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We study the strong coupling expansion of large $N$ QCD in various dimensions, reformulating the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian on a square lattice in terms of (constrained) one dimensional spin chain models. We study the integrability properties of the spin chain obtained this way: there is large class of integrable subsectors, but we show that the full spin chain is not integrable, at least when viewed from a description based on Bethe ansatz. We demonstrate that the spin chains no longer possess integrability due to the constraints arising from the zigzag symmetry of the confining strings. The spin chain description properly estimates the roughening transition point by extrapolating the first-order analytical results based on integrability of some subsectors. The generalization to higher dimensions are also considered, where we also find the small subsectors without the zigzag constraints to be integrable.

### [39] [Regge trajectories from the adjoint sector of Matrix Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04522)
*Igor R. Klebanov,Henry W. Lin,Pavel Meshcheriakov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the adjoint sector of SU$(N)$ symmetric quantum mechanics of a Hermitian matrix in the large $N$ limit, revealing Regge trajectories with $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$ at criticality—interpreted as short folded open strings in dual 2D string theory—and a transition to long strings away from criticality.
\n\n
本文研究了大 $N$ 极限下具有 SU$(N)$ 对称性的 Hermitian 矩阵量子力学的伴随表示（adjoint）扇区，在临界点处揭示出满足 $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$ 的 Regge 轨迹——在对偶的二维弦论中被解释为“短”折叠开弦；略微偏离临界点时，高激发态转变为延伸至 Liouville 方向的“长弦”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While the singlet sector of this matrix quantum mechanics is well understood via free fermions and its connection to 2D string theory, the adjoint sector remains less explored. The authors aim to uncover new physical phenomena in this sector, especially near the critical point where the Fermi level approaches a potential maximum, which corresponds to nontrivial string dynamics in two dimensions.
\n\n
虽然该矩阵量子力学的单态（singlet）扇区通过自由费米子方法及其与二维弦论的联系已被充分理解，但其伴随表示（adjoint）扇区仍较少被探索。作者旨在揭示该扇区中的新物理现象，特别是在费米能级接近势能极大值的临界点附近——这对应于二维弦论中的非平凡弦动力学。

Method: The authors solve the Marchesini-Onofri equation governing the adjoint sector both numerically and analytically using semiclassical approximations. They analyze the spectrum near criticality where the Fermi surface touches a local maximum of the potential, and study deviations from criticality by perturbing the system slightly away from this point.
\n\n
作者通过数值方法和半经典近似解析求解支配伴随表示扇区的 Marchesini-Onofri 方程。他们分析了费米面接触势能局部极大值时的临界谱，并通过微扰系统略微偏离该点来研究非临界行为。

Result: At criticality, the energy spectrum in the adjoint sector follows Regge trajectories with eigenvalues scaling as $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$, interpreted as oscillatory modes of a short folded open string in the dual 2D string theory. This Regge behavior is universal up to subleading corrections and independent of the specific potential used to approach criticality. Slightly away from criticality, highly excited states become long strings extending into the Liouville direction.
\n\n
在临界点处，伴随表示扇区的能量谱遵循 Regge 轨迹，其本征值满足 $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$，在对偶的二维弦论中被解释为“短”折叠开弦的振荡模式。这种 Regge 行为在次领头阶修正下具有普适性，且不依赖于趋近临界点所采用的具体势能形式。略微偏离临界点时，高激发态转变为延伸至 Liouville 方向的“长弦”。

Conclusion: The adjoint sector of large $N$ matrix quantum mechanics exhibits rich string-theoretic structure: at criticality it realizes short folded open strings with universal Regge behavior, while off-critical excitations correspond to long strings in the Liouville direction. This provides a concrete quantum mechanical realization of different string configurations in 2D string theory.
\n\n
大 $N$ 矩阵量子力学的伴随表示扇区展现出丰富的弦论结构：在临界点处实现具有普适 Regge 行为的“短”折叠开弦，而非临界激发则对应于 Liouville 方向上的“长弦”。这为二维弦论中不同弦构型提供了具体的量子力学实现。

Abstract: We reexamine the large $N$ limit of SU$(N)$ symmetric quantum mechanics of a Hermitian matrix whose singlet sector is well known to be exactly solvable via free fermions. When the Fermi level approaches a maximum of the potential, there is critical behavior corresponding to string theory in two dimensions. We uncover new phenomena in the adjoint sector by solving the Marchesini-Onofri equation both numerically and analytically using semiclassical approximations: at criticality, the spectrum is governed by Regge trajectories with energy eigenvalues growing according to $Δ^2 \sim n/ α'$. In the dual 2D string theory, we interpret these states as oscillatory excitations of a ``short'' folded open string. Up to sub-leading corrections, this Regge behavior is essentially universal and is insensitive to the particular potential we choose to approach criticality. Slightly away from criticality, the highly excited states transition into ``long strings'' that extend far into the Liouville direction.

### [40] [A smooth road to bumpy horizons: shaping black holes with non-linear sigma models, from supergravity to higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04611)
*Fabrizio Canfora,Nicolás Grandi,Carla Henríquez-Báez,Julio Oliva*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper constructs new exact solutions in General Relativity coupled to non-linear sigma models, including bumpy black holes, stars, anisotropic cosmologies, and branes in $d \geq 4$, plus time-dependent 2+1D solutions, using first-order BPS equations for coset scalars.
\n\n
本文在广义相对论与非线性sigma模型耦合的框架下构造了新的精确解，包括高维（$d \geq 4$）中具有不规则视界的中性/带电/磁化黑洞、不规则恒星、各向异性宇宙学解以及黑弦和黑$p$-膜，并利用coset标量场的一阶BPS方程给出了2+1维的时间依赖解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the known solution space of Einstein gravity minimally coupled to non-linear sigma models—particularly those with homogeneous coset target spaces—by leveraging first-order Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) relations, which simplify the second-order field equations and allow for richer horizon geometries and matter configurations beyond spherical symmetry.
\n\n
动机在于通过利用一阶Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield（BPS）关系，拓展爱因斯坦引力与具有齐次coset目标空间的非线性sigma模型最小耦合体系的已知解空间。这类BPS关系可将二阶场方程简化为一阶方程，从而允许超越球对称性的更丰富的视界几何结构和物质构型。

Method: The method employs first-order BPS equations for scalar fields taking values in a homogeneous coset manifold $G/H$, originally introduced in arXiv:2601.22914 for the $SU(2)/U(1)$ model. These BPS conditions reduce the full Einstein–sigma system to a solvable set of first-order differential equations, enabling analytic construction of static and time-dependent solutions with non-trivial spatial or temporal dependence in the metric and scalar profiles.
\n\n
方法采用取值于齐次coset流形 $G/H$ 的标量场的一阶BPS方程，该方程最初在arXiv:2601.22914中针对 $SU(2)/U(1)$ 模型提出。这些BPS条件将完整的Einstein–sigma系统约化为一组可解的一阶微分方程，从而能够解析构造度规和标量场具有非平凡空间或时间依赖性的静态及时间依赖解。

Result: The authors obtain multiple new families of exact solutions: (i) neutral, electrically charged, and magnetized black holes with “bumpy” (non-spherical) horizons; (ii) self-gravitating bumpy stars; (iii) anisotropic cosmological spacetimes; (iv) black strings and black $p$-branes in $d \geq 4$; and (v) a class of time-dependent solutions in $2+1$ dimensions. Some solutions admit embeddings into supergravity theories.
\n\n
作者获得了多类新的精确解：(i) 具有“不规则”（非球对称）视界的中性、带电及磁化黑洞；(ii) 自引力不规则恒星；(iii) 各向异性宇宙学时空；(iv) $d \geq 4$ 维中的黑弦和黑$p$-膜；以及(v) 一类2+1维的时间依赖解。其中部分解可嵌入超引力理论中。

Conclusion: The use of first-order BPS relations for coset-valued scalars provides a powerful framework for generating exact, non-spherical, and even time-dependent solutions in gravity–sigma systems, significantly broadening the landscape of known solutions and offering new arenas for studying black hole microstructure, cosmic anisotropy, and holographic duals.
\n\n
对取值于coset的标量场应用一阶BPS关系，为在引力–sigma模型中生成精确的、非球对称甚至时间依赖的解提供了一个强大框架，显著拓展了已知解的景观，并为研究黑洞微观结构、宇宙各向异性及全息对偶开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We construct new families of solutions for General Relativity coupled to a general class of non-linear sigma models, some of which can be embedded in supergravity. The solutions include neutral, charged and magnetized black holes with bumpy horizons, bumpy stars, and anisotropic cosmologies in $d\geq 4$ dimensions, as well as black strings and black $p$-branes. We also present a family of time-dependent solutions in $2+1$-dimensions. The construction relies on a set of first-order Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield relations for the coset scalars, that were recently exploited for the construction of bumpy black holes on the non-linear sigma model with homogenous target $SU(2)/U(1)$ in 2601.22914 [hep-th].

### [41] [The Chern-Simons Natural Boundary and Black Hole Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04619)
*Griffen Adams,Gerald V. Dunne*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper establishes a novel correspondence between $q$-series counting quarter-BPS black hole microstates and $\hat{Z}$ invariants of Chern-Simons theory on orientation-reversed 3-manifolds, uncovered via resurgent continuation of transseries.

本文通过transseries的resurgent延拓方法，揭示了一种新的对应关系：用于计数四分之一BPS黑洞微观态的$q$-级数与一类三维定向反转流形上Chern-Simons理论的$\hat{Z}$不变量之间的对应。

Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to understand non-perturbative structures in quantum field theory and quantum gravity by connecting enumerative invariants from supersymmetric black hole physics with topological invariants from 3-manifold Chern-Simons theory. 动机源于通过将超对称黑洞物理中的枚举不变量与三维流形Chern-Simons理论中的拓扑不变量相联系，以理解量子场论和量子引力中的非微扰结构。Resurgence理论提供了一个连接微扰与非微扰扇区的框架，暗示了潜在的对偶性。

Method: The authors employ the method of resurgent continuation applied to transseries solutions—formal series incorporating both perturbative and non-perturbative exponential corrections—to analytically continue $q$-series associated with quarter-BPS state degeneracies. 作者采用resurgent延拓方法作用于transseries解——即包含微扰项与非微扰指数修正项的形式级数——对与四分之一BPS态简并度相关的$q$-级数进行解析延拓，并将其匹配到Chern-Simons理论中针对定向反转三维流形定义的$\hat{Z}$不变量。

Result: A precise mathematical correspondence is demonstrated: the resurgent completion of the $q$-series for quarter-BPS black hole degeneracies coincides with the $\hat{Z}$ invariants of Chern-Simons theory on certain orientation-reversed 3-manifolds, revealing deep links between black hole microstate counting and 3-manifold topology.

论文展示了精确的数学对应关系：四分之一BPS黑洞简并度$q$-级数的resurgent完备化与特定定向反转三维流形上Chern-Simons理论的$\hat{Z}$不变量一致，揭示了黑洞微观态计数与三维流形拓扑之间的深刻联系。

Conclusion: This work underscores the power of resurgence and transseries in uncovering hidden dualities between seemingly disparate domains—supersymmetric black holes and topological quantum field theory—suggesting that non-perturbative completions of partition functions encode geometric and topological data of underlying manifolds.

本工作强调了resurgence与transseries在揭示看似不同领域（超对称黑洞与拓扑量子场论）之间隐藏对偶性方面的强大能力，表明配分函数的非微扰完备化编码了底层流形的几何与拓扑信息。

Abstract: The method of resurgent continuation of transseries reveals a new correspondence between the $q$-series for enumerating degeneracies of quarter-BPS states in supersymmetric black holes and $\hat{Z}$ invariants of Chern-Simons theory on a class of 3 dimensional orientation-reversed manifolds.

### [42] [Holographic QCD and quarkonium melting: Finite temperature, density, and external field effects in self-consistent dynamical models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04725)
*Bruno Toniato*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This MSc dissertation constructs dynamical holographic QCD models within the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton and Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton frameworks to study meson spectra and melting under finite temperature, density, and magnetic fields. It finds sequential quarkonia dissociation, chemical potential–enhanced melting, and a transition from inverse magnetic catalysis to magnetic catalysis due to spatial anisotropy.
\n\n
本篇硕士论文在Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton和Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton框架内构建了动力学全息QCD模型，用于研究有限温度、密度和磁场下的介子谱与熔解行为。研究发现夸克偶素依次解离、化学势增强熔解效应，并因空间各向异性导致从反磁催化向磁催化的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand non-perturbative QCD phenomena—such as confinement, chiral symmetry breaking, and quarkonium dissociation—under extreme conditions (finite temperature $T$, baryon chemical potential $\\mu_B$, and magnetic field $B$), where lattice QCD faces challenges like the sign problem. The AdS/CFT correspondence offers a tractable strong-coupling approach via gauge/gravity duality to model these regimes.
\n\n
动机源于在极端条件（有限温度 $T$、重子化学势 $\\mu_B$ 和磁场 $B$）下理解非微扰QCD现象（如禁闭、手征对称性破缺和夸克偶素解离）的需求，而格点QCD在此类条件下面临符号问题等挑战。AdS/CFT 对应对偶通过规范/引力对偶提供了一种可处理的强耦合方法来建模这些区域。

Method: The author employs a top-down inspired bottom-up holographic QCD approach. Starting from the 5D Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton action, they solve the coupled Einstein, Maxwell, and dilaton field equations self-consistently to obtain a black hole background encoding finite $T$ and $\\mu$. Meson spectra are computed via linearized fluctuations of probe fields (e.g., vector modes for quarkonia). Spectral functions are extracted from retarded Green’s functions using the AdS/CFT dictionary. A nonlinear Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton extension incorporates magnetic field effects with spatial anisotropy.
\n\n
作者采用一种受自上而下启发的自下而上全息QCD方法。从5维Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton作用量出发，自洽求解耦合的Einstein、Maxwell和dilaton场方程，获得编码有限 $T$ 和 $\\mu$ 的黑洞背景。通过探针场（如矢量模用于夸克偶素）的线性化涨落计算介子谱，并利用AdS/CFT字典从推迟Green函数中提取谱函数。通过非线性的Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton扩展引入具有空间各向异性的磁场效应。

Result: Key results include: (1) a holographic confinement-deconfinement phase transition signaled by black hole thermodynamics; (2) sequential melting of heavy quarkonia states ($J/\\psi$, $\\Upsilon$, etc.) with increasing $T$, consistent with phenomenology; (3) enhanced meson dissociation at finite $\\mu$, with smooth spectral evolution across the crossover; (4) in the presence of a magnetic field, the model exhibits a shift from inverse magnetic catalysis (at low $B$) to magnetic catalysis (at high $B$), attributed to spatial anisotropy induced by the Born-Infeld action.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 由黑洞热力学表征的全息禁闭-退禁闭相变；(2) 随温度 $T$ 升高，重夸克偶素态（如 $J/\\psi$、$\\Upsilon$ 等）依次熔解，符合唯象预期；(3) 在有限化学势 $\\mu$ 下介子解离增强，且谱函数在穿越相变线时平滑演化；(4) 在磁场存在下，模型展现出从反磁催化（低 $B$）到磁催化（高 $B$）的转变，归因于Born-Infeld作用量诱导的空间各向异性。

Conclusion: The dissertation demonstrates that self-consistent dynamical holographic models based on Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton gravity can successfully capture key non-perturbative features of QCD at finite density and temperature. The inclusion of nonlinear electrodynamics (Born-Infeld) reveals a rich interplay between magnetic fields and anisotropy, reversing the expected catalysis behavior. This underscores holography as a versatile tool for exploring QCD matter under extreme conditions beyond lattice reach.
\n\n
该论文表明，基于Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton引力的自洽动力学全息模型能够成功捕捉QCD在有限密度和温度下的关键非微扰特征。引入非线性电动力学（Born-Infeld）揭示了磁场与各向异性之间的丰富相互作用，导致催化行为发生反转。这凸显了全息对偶作为探索超出格点QCD能力范围的极端条件下QCD物质的多功能工具。

Abstract: This MSc dissertation is based on the papers arXiv:2502.12694 and arXiv:2408.14813. The AdS/CFT correspondence provides a powerful framework for modeling strongly coupled gauge theories and, as a consequence, investigating non-perturbative phenomena in QCD. In this work, following an overview of the ideas that encapsulate the AdS/CFT correspondence, we present a self-consistent dynamical holographic QCD model within the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton framework, derived from the coupled field equations, to study the mass spectra and melting behavior of heavy and exotic mesons at finite temperature and density. Finite temperature analyses reveal a confinement-deconfinement transition and sequential quarkonia melting. At finite density, an increase in chemical potential accelerates meson melting, with spectral functions evolving smoothly across the phase transition line. Finally, using a nonlinear Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton model, magnetic field effects demonstrate a shift from inverse magnetic catalysis to magnetic catalysis, highlighting the impact of spatial anisotropy on quarkonium stability.

### [43] [$N^{3/2}$ Scaling from $3d$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ Dualities: an Alternative Approach to Chiral Quivers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04849)
*Antonio Amariti,Giulia Lanzetti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper resolves a long-standing problem regarding the $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy in 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver gauge theories dual to M2-branes on toric Sasaki-Einstein$_7$ (SE$_7$) singularities. By expressing the three-sphere partition function as a hyperbolic hypergeometric integral and applying exact identities, the authors show it equals that of non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors—whose $N^{3/2}$ behavior is known—thereby establishing the scaling for chiral quivers via a generalized Giveon-Kutasov duality.
\n\n
本文解决了关于3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver规范理论（对偶于M2-brane在toric Sasaki-Einstein$_7$（SE$_7$）奇点上）自由能的$N^{3/2}$标度这一长期未决问题。作者将三球配分函数表示为hyperbolic hypergeometric积分，并利用精确积分恒等式，证明其等价于已知具有$N^{3/2}$行为的non-chiral quiver加chiral flavor的情形，从而通过广义的Giveon-Kutasov对偶性确立了chiral quiver的$N^{3/2}$标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$ correspondence, where 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs are conjectured to describe the worldvolume theory of $N$ M2-branes probing Calabi–Yau 4-fold singularities. For toric SE$_7$ geometries without internal points in their toric diagrams, the dual field theories are chiral quivers constructed via un-higgsing of non-chiral parent theories. Although their moduli spaces correctly reproduce the expected M-theory geometry, the large-$N$ behavior of the free energy—specifically the $N^{3/2}$ scaling predicted by supergravity—remained unproven for over ten years, despite recent partial progress. This work aims to close this gap rigorously.
\n\n
动机源于AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$对偶，其中3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT被猜想描述$N$个M2-brane探测Calabi–Yau 4-fold奇点的世界体理论。对于toric图中无内点的toric SE$_7$几何，其对偶场论是通过un-higgsing non-chiral母理论构造的chiral quiver。尽管其模空间正确复现了M理论预期的几何，但自由能的大$N$行为——特别是超引力预言的$N^{3/2}$标度——十多年来一直未被严格证明，尽管近期有部分进展。本文旨在严谨地填补这一空白。

Method: The authors reformulate the three-sphere ($S^3$) partition function of the chiral quiver theories using supersymmetric localization, which reduces it to a matrix integral of hyperbolic hypergeometric type. They then apply recently established exact integral identities for such hyperbolic functions, which relate the partition function of a chiral quiver to that of a non-chiral quiver with additional chiral flavor multiplets. This identity is interpreted as a generalization of Giveon-Kutasov duality—which originally relates Chern-Simons-matter theories with different ranks and levels—to chiral settings. The method leverages analytic properties of the double sine function and residue calculus to establish equivalence at finite $N$, which then implies identical large-$N$ asymptotics.
\n\n
作者利用超对称局域化将chiral quiver理论的三球（$S^3$）配分函数重新表述为hyperbolic hypergeometric类型的矩阵积分。随后应用近期建立的此类hyperbolic函数的精确积分恒等式，将chiral quiver的配分函数关联到带有额外chiral flavor多重态的non-chiral quiver的配分函数。该恒等式被解释为Giveon-Kutasov对偶性的推广——后者原本关联不同秩和Chern-Simons level的Chern-Simons-matter理论——至chiral情形。该方法利用double sine函数的解析性质与留数计算，在有限$N$下建立等价性，从而推出相同的大$N$渐近行为。

Result: The key result is the proof that the $S^3$ free energy $F = -\log |Z_{S^3}|$ of the chiral quiver theories exhibits the $N^{3/2}$ scaling at large $N$, matching the supergravity prediction for M2-branes on toric SE$_7$ cones. This is achieved by demonstrating an exact equality: $Z_{\\text{chiral}} = Z_{\\text{non-chiral + flavors}}$, where the right-hand side is a theory whose $N^{3/2}$ scaling was previously established. The result holds for all members of the family of chiral quivers corresponding to toric diagrams without internal points, thereby resolving a decade-old open problem.
\n\n
核心结果是证明了chiral quiver理论的$S^3$自由能$F = -\log |Z_{S^3}|$在大$N$极限下呈现$N^{3/2}$标度，与M2-brane在toric SE$_7$锥上的超引力预言一致。这是通过证明精确等式$Z_{\\text{chiral}} = Z_{\\text{non-chiral + flavors}}$实现的，其中右侧理论的$N^{3/2}$标度此前已被确立。该结果适用于所有对应于无内点toric图的chiral quiver族，从而解决了长达十年的开放问题。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a large-$N$ duality between chiral quiver gauge theories and non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors through an exact identity of their $S^3$ partition functions. This not only confirms the expected $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy for the chiral theories—validating their proposed holographic duality to M2-branes on toric SE$_7$—but also extends the scope of Giveon-Kutasov-like dualities to chiral settings. The work demonstrates the power of exact results in supersymmetric localization and hyperbolic special functions in resolving long-standing questions in the AdS/CFT correspondence.
\n\n
本文通过$S^3$配分函数的精确恒等式，建立了chiral quiver规范理论与带chiral flavor的non-chiral quiver之间的大$N$对偶性。这不仅确认了chiral理论自由能的预期$N^{3/2}$标度——验证了其与M2-brane在toric SE$_7$上全息对偶的猜想——还将Giveon-Kutasov类对偶性的适用范围推广至chiral情形。该工作展示了超对称局域化与hyperbolic特殊函数的精确结果在解决AdS/CFT对偶中长期问题方面的强大能力。

Abstract: We investigate families of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver gauge theories conjectured to be dual to M2-branes probing toric SE$_7$ singularities. Geometrically, these families correspond to toric diagrams without internal points. At the field theory level, the models are constructed via an un-higgsing procedure applied to non-chiral quivers. While the moduli space of these theories was shown to match M-theory expectations, determining the $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy remained an open problem for over a decade, with positive results emerging only very recently. In this work, we address this challenge by reformulating the three-sphere partition function as a hyperbolic hypergeometric integral. Using exact integral identities, we show that the free energy reduces precisely to that of non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors, for which the $N^{3/2}$ scaling is already established. Physically, this mathematical identity corresponds to the equivalence of three-sphere partition functions under a generalization of Giveon-Kutasov duality to chiral quivers. Our results thus provide a large $N$ duality between the chiral quivers and non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors, confirming the $N^{3/2}$ scaling for the chiral quivers under study.

</details>


### [44] [Parameter compression in the flux landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04941)
*Aman Chauhan,Michele Cicoli,Sven Krippendorf,Anshuman Maharana,Pellegrino Piantadosi,Andreas Schachner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper employs data-driven methods—specifically physics-informed autoencoders and topological data analysis—to explore the structure of no-scale type IIB flux vacua from a 12-dimensional flux space. It finds that the effective dimensionality is significantly reduced, with non-linear latent representations capturing key physical features like small $|W_0|$, and persistent hom日消息 revealing stable topological structures in both flux and moduli spaces.
\n\n
本文采用数据驱动方法——特别是物理信息自编码器和拓扑数据分析——探索来自12维flux空间的no-scale type IIB flux vacua的结构。研究发现有效维度显著降低，非线性潜在表示能够捕捉如小$|W_0|$等关键物理特征，而persistent homology揭示了flux空间和moduli空间中稳定的拓扑结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The vast landscape of string theory vacua, particularly in type IIB flux compactifications, poses a major challenge for systematic exploration and phenomenological selection. Traditional linear methods fail to capture complex, non-linear correlations among fluxes and moduli that govern physically relevant properties such as the magnitude of the flux superpotential $|W_0|$. The authors aim to develop advanced data-analytic tools to uncover hidden structures in this high-dimensional vacuum ensemble, paving the way for foundation models in string phenomenology.
\n\n
弦论真空景观（尤其是type IIB flux紧化）的庞大规模对系统性探索和唯象选择构成了重大挑战。传统的线性方法无法捕捉flux与moduli之间控制物理相关性质（如flux超势大小$|W_0|$）的复杂非线性关联。作者旨在开发先进的数据分析工具，以揭示这一高维真空集合中的隐藏结构，为弦论唯象学中的foundation models奠定基础。

Method: The authors combine non-linear dimensionality reduction via a physics-informed autoencoder with topological data analysis (TDA). The autoencoder is trained on the joint flux-moduli dataset to learn a low-dimensional latent representation that respects physical constraints and emphasizes features like small $|W_0|$. Simultaneously, they apply persistent homology—a TDA technique—to both flux and moduli subspaces to detect robust topological features (e.g., connected components, loops) that persist across scales, thereby characterizing the global geometry of the vacuum distribution.
\n\n
作者结合了基于物理信息自编码器的非线性降维方法与拓扑数据分析（TDA）。自编码器在flux-moduli联合数据集上训练，学习一个低维潜在表示，该表示尊重物理约束并突出如小$|W_0|$等特征。同时，他们将persistent homology（一种TDA技术）应用于flux和moduli子空间，以检测在不同尺度下持久存在的稳健拓扑特征（如连通分量、环结构），从而刻画真空分布的整体几何结构。

Result: The study reveals that the intrinsic dimensionality of the 12-dimensional flux space is much lower than naively expected. The physics-informed autoencoder successfully isolates regions of the vacuum ensemble with small $|W_0|$, exposing non-trivial correlations invisible to linear techniques like PCA. Persistent homology identifies long-lived topological features in both flux and moduli spaces, indicating non-random, structured organization of vacua. These findings demonstrate that machine learning and TDA can extract meaningful physical insights from large ensembles of string vacua.
\n\n
研究表明，12维flux空间的内在维度远低于直观预期。物理信息自编码器成功分离出具有小$|W_0|$的真空区域，揭示了主成分分析（PCA）等线性方法无法察觉的非平凡关联。Persistent homology在flux和moduli空间中均识别出长寿命的拓扑特征，表明真空具有非随机的、结构化的组织。这些结果证明，机器学习与TDA能够从大规模弦论真空集合中提取有意义的物理洞见。

Conclusion: This work establishes a novel framework for analyzing the string landscape using modern data science tools. By integrating physics-informed machine learning with topological data analysis, it uncovers hidden geometric and topological structures in flux compactifications. The results constitute a crucial step toward building foundation models in string phenomenology capable of navigating the vacuum landscape and identifying regions compatible with low-energy physics.
\n\n
本工作建立了利用现代数据科学工具分析弦论景观的新框架。通过将物理信息机器学习与拓扑数据分析相结合，揭示了flux紧化中隐藏的几何与拓扑结构。这些成果是构建弦论唯象学中foundation models的关键一步，使模型能够导航真空景观并识别与低能物理相容的区域。

Abstract: We present a data-driven investigation of the exhaustive ensemble of no-scale type IIB flux vacua constructed in \cite{Chauhan:2025rdj}. Using a combination of linear and non-linear dimensionality-reduction techniques, we analyse both flux and moduli spaces and demonstrate that the effective dimensionality of the underlying 12-dimensional flux space is substantially reduced. A central component of our study is a physics-informed autoencoder, which provides a non-linear compression of the flux and moduli data into a low-dimensional latent space. The learned latent representation organises vacua according to desired features and, in particular, isolates distinguished regions associated with small values of the flux superpotential $|W_0|$, revealing non-trivial correlations that are not captured by linear methods. In parallel, we apply tools from topological data analysis, specifically persistent homology, to probe the global structure of the vacuum distribution. This allows us to identify robust, long-lived topological features in both moduli and flux subspaces. This work is a necessary step for developing foundation models in string phenomenology.

</details>


### [45] [Gravitational instantons from closed superstring field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04953)
*Ivo Sachs,Xianghang Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the exact marginality of deformations resolving a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold in closed superstring theory by computing equations of motion up to third order in the deformation parameter, including $α'$ corrections. It shows no obstructions arise at third order and recovers the Eguchi-Hanson gravitational instanton in the field theory limit up to second order.
\n\n
本文通过在闭合超弦理论中计算至形变参数三阶的运动方程（包含 $α'$ 修正），研究了 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 轨形（orbifold）分解形变的精确边缘性（exact marginality）。结果表明三阶修正对所有形变模（moduli）均无障碍，并在场论极限下通过适当选择模空间参数，在二阶精度内重现了 Eguchi-Hanson 引力瞬子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to determine whether the deformation corresponding to the resolution of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold singularity remains exactly marginal in string theory when higher-order $α'$ corrections are included. This addresses the consistency of such resolutions as truly marginal operators in the worldsheet CFT and their embedding into full string dynamics.
\n\n
动机在于确定当包含高阶 $α'$ 修正时，对应于 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 轨形奇点分解的形变在弦论中是否保持精确边缘性。这关系到此类分解作为世界面共形场论（CFT）中真正边缘算符的一致性及其在完整弦动力学中的嵌入。

Method: The authors solve the closed superstring equations of motion perturbatively up to third order in the deformation modulus, incorporating $α'$ corrections from the string effective action. They analyze the solvability (i.e., absence of obstructions) of these equations using cohomological methods tied to the underlying SCFT. Additionally, they take the field theory limit ($α' \to 0$) with specific moduli choices to compare with known supergravity solutions.
\n\n
作者在弦有效作用量中引入 $α'$ 修正，将闭合超弦运动方程按形变模展开至三阶进行微扰求解。他们利用与底层超共形场论（SCFT）相关的上同调方法分析这些方程的可解性（即无障碍条件）。此外，他们通过选取特定模空间参数并取场论极限（$α' \to 0$），与已知的超引力解进行对比。

Result: The third-order correction to the deformation is found to be unobstructed for all values of the deformation moduli, indicating exact marginality persists beyond leading order. In the field theory limit, the solution reproduces the Eguchi-Hanson gravitational instanton up to second order in the deformation parameter.
\n\n
结果发现，对所有形变模而言，三阶修正均无障碍，表明精确边缘性在领头阶之后依然保持。在场论极限下，该解在形变参数的二阶精度内重现了 Eguchi-Hanson 引力瞬子。

Conclusion: The resolution of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold via this deformation defines an exactly marginal direction in the moduli space of closed superstring vacua, even when $α'$ corrections are included. This supports the use of such deformations in constructing smooth, non-singular string backgrounds and connects worldsheet CFT data to spacetime geometry through explicit supergravity solutions.
\n\n
通过该形变对 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 轨形的分解即使在包含 $α'$ 修正的情况下，也在闭合超弦真空模空间中定义了一个精确边缘方向。这支持了此类形变在构建光滑、无奇点弦背景中的应用，并通过显式的超引力解将世界面 CFT 数据与时空几何联系起来。

Abstract: We test exact marginality of the deformation describing the resolution of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold by analyzing the closed superstring equations of motion to third order in the size, including $α'$ corrections. We find that the third order correction is unobstructed for all deformation moduli. We are also able to reproduce the Eguchi-Hanson gravitational instanton up to the second order in the field theory limit with a suitable choice of moduli.

### [46] [Simulating Lattice Gauge Theories with Virtual Rishons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05151)
*David Rogerson,João Barata,Robert M. Konik,Raju Venugopalan,Ananda Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces a novel virtual rishon framework that enforces gauge symmetry in lattice gauge theories using a quantum-link formulation, enabling simulations in $d+1$ spacetime dimensions with both classical tensor networks and near-term quantum hardware. The method is validated in U(1) gauge theories: for $d=1$, it reproduces features of the multi-flavor Schwinger model linked to Wess-Zumino-Witten CFT; for $d=2$, it accurately computes the confining string tension.
\n\n
本文提出了一种新颖的虚拟rishon框架，通过量子链（quantum-link）形式在格点规范理论中强制实现规范对称性，使得在$d+1$维时空下可同时使用经典张量网络和近期量子硬件进行模拟。该方法在U(1)规范理论中得到验证：对于$d=1$，重现了多味Schwinger模型与Wess-Zumino-Witten共形场论相关的特征；对于$d=2$，准确计算出了禁闭弦张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Simulating real-time dynamics of lattice gauge theories remains a major challenge for both classical and quantum computational methods. Existing approaches often struggle to preserve local gauge symmetry while scaling to higher dimensions or including dynamical matter. This work aims to address these limitations by constructing a framework that intrinsically respects gauge symmetry through a quantum-link formulation with virtual rishons, making it suitable for both tensor network simulations and implementation on near-term quantum devices.
\n\n
模拟格点规范理论的实时动力学对经典和量子计算方法而言仍是一个重大挑战。现有方法在扩展到高维或包含动力学物质时，往往难以保持局域规范对称性。本工作旨在通过构建一个基于虚拟rishon的量子链表述框架，内在地保持规范对称性，从而克服这些限制，使其既适用于张量网络模拟，也适合在近期量子设备上实现。

Method: The authors introduce a quantum-link model based on a virtual rishon representation, where both gauge and matter fields are encoded as qubits. Gauge symmetry is enforced at intermediate steps of the algorithm via this representation. The framework supports arbitrary boundary conditions and topological angles, and is compatible with both classical tensor network techniques and hybrid quantum-classical algorithms. Simulations are performed for U(1) gauge theories in (1+1)D (multi-flavor Schwinger model) and (2+1)D, with observables such as conformal signatures and string tension extracted.
\n\n
作者引入了一种基于虚拟rishon表示的量子链模型，其中规范场和物质场均被编码为量子比特（qubits）。通过该表示，在算法中间步骤强制实现规范对称性。该框架支持任意边界条件和拓扑角，并兼容经典张量网络技术和混合量子-经典算法。研究对U(1)规范理论在(1+1)维（多味Schwinger模型）和(2+1)维情形进行了模拟，并提取了共形特征和弦张力等观测量。

Result: For $d = 1$, the framework successfully captures the physics of the multi-flavor Schwinger model with $1 \leq N_f \leq 3$, including its connection to the Wess-Zumino-Witten conformal field theory, under arbitrary boundary conditions and nonzero topological angle $\theta$. For $d = 2$, the confining string tension is computed and found to be in close agreement with continuum expectations. These benchmarks demonstrate the method’s accuracy and scalability across dimensions.
\n\n
对于$d = 1$，该框架成功捕捉了$1 \leq N_f \leq 3$多味Schwinger模型的物理特性，包括其与Wess-Zumino-Witten共形场论的联系，并适用于任意边界条件和非零拓扑角$\theta$。对于$d = 2$，计算出的禁闭弦张力与连续极限下的预期高度一致。这些基准测试证明了该方法在不同维度下的准确性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: The virtual rishon framework provides a unified, gauge-symmetric approach for simulating lattice gauge theories in $d+1$ dimensions using both classical tensor networks and near-term quantum hardware. Its success in reproducing known results in (1+1)D and (2+1)D U(1) theories establishes it as a robust and scalable platform for future studies of non-Abelian gauge theories and real-time dynamics.
\n\n
虚拟rishon框架为在$d+1$维中使用经典张量网络和近期量子硬件模拟格点规范理论提供了一个统一且规范对称的方法。其在(1+1)维和(2+1)维U(1)理论中成功复现已知结果，确立了其作为未来研究非阿贝尔规范理论和实时动力学的稳健且可扩展平台的地位。

Abstract: Classical tensor network and hybrid quantum-classical algorithms are promising candidates for the investigation of real-time properties of lattice gauge theories. We develop here a novel framework which enforces gauge symmetry via a quantum-link virtual rishon representation applied at intermediate steps. Crucially, the gauge and matter degrees of freedom are dynamical variables encoded in terms of qubits, enabling analysis of gauge theories in $d+1$ spacetime dimensions. We benchmark this framework in a U(1) gauge theory with and without matter fields. For $d = 1$, the multi-flavor Schwinger model with $1\leq N_f\leq3$ flavors is analyzed for arbitrary boundary conditions and nonzero topological angle, capturing signatures of the underlying Wess-Zumino-Witten conformal field theory. For $d = 2$, we extract the confining string tension in close agreement with continuum expectations. These results establish the virtual rishon framework as a scalable and robust approach for the simulation of lattice gauge theories using both classical tensor networks as well as near-term quantum hardware.
