### [47] [Introduction to holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05186)
*Nele Callebaut*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: These course notes provide a pedagogical introduction to holography, focusing on the AdS/CFT correspondence as a concrete realization of quantum gravity via a duality between a gravitational theory in Anti-de Sitter (AdS) space and a non-gravitational conformal field theory (CFT) on its boundary. The notes build from foundational symmetries (Poincaré and conformal) through AdS geometry to the full duality, including finite-temperature effects, black hole thermodynamics, and the role of entanglement in emergent gravity.
\n\n
这些课程笔记为全息原理（holography）提供了教学性介绍，重点聚焦于AdS/CFT对偶——这是一种通过反德西特（Anti-de Sitter, AdS）空间中的引力理论与其边界上无引力的共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）之间的对偶关系来实现量子引力的具体范例。笔记从基础对称性（庞加莱对称性和共形对称性）出发，逐步过渡到AdS几何，最终构建完整的对偶框架，包括有限温度效应、黑洞热力学，以及纠缠在引力涌现（“gravity emerges from entanglement”）中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to offer a structured, pedagogical pathway for Master’s students to understand holography—a key framework in modern theoretical physics for addressing quantum gravity—by emphasizing the foundational role of symmetry and the concrete AdS/CFT correspondence. The course aims to demystify how a higher-dimensional gravitational theory can be encoded in a lower-dimensional quantum field theory without gravity.
\n\n
其动机是为硕士生提供一条结构清晰、教学性强的学习路径，以理解全息原理——这是现代理论物理中处理量子引力的关键框架——通过强调对称性的基础作用以及具体的AdS/CFT对偶。课程旨在阐明高维引力理论如何被编码在一个低维且无引力的量子场论中。

Method: The method is expository and pedagogical, progressing logically through key concepts: starting with Poincaré symmetry in QFT, then conformal symmetry in CFTs, followed by the geometry and physics of Anti-de Sitter space. After establishing these building blocks, the notes formally introduce the AdS/CFT correspondence, extend it to finite temperature via black hole thermodynamics, and conclude with modern insights linking quantum entanglement to the emergence of spacetime geometry.
\n\n
该方法是阐述性与教学性的，按逻辑顺序推进关键概念：从量子场论（QFT）中的庞加莱对称性开始，继而讨论共形场论（CFT）中的共形对称性，再进入反德西特（AdS）空间的几何与物理。在建立这些基础模块后，笔记正式引入AdS/CFT对偶，并通过黑洞热力学将其推广至有限温度情形，最后以量子纠缠与时空几何涌现之间联系的现代观点作结。

Result: The result is a self-contained set of lecture notes that successfully bridges foundational quantum field theory and advanced topics in holography. Students gain a clear understanding of how AdS/CFT realizes holography, how black holes encode thermal states in the dual CFT, and how entanglement entropy in the boundary theory relates to geometric properties in the bulk—culminating in the idea that spacetime and gravity may emerge from quantum entanglement.
\n\n
其成果是一套自洽的讲义，成功衔接了基础量子场论与全息原理中的前沿课题。学生能够清晰理解AdS/CFT如何实现全息对偶、黑洞如何在对偶CFT中编码热态，以及边界理论中的纠缠熵如何与体空间（bulk）的几何性质相关联——最终导向“时空与引力可能从量子纠缠中涌现”这一核心思想。

Conclusion: The course concludes that holography, particularly through AdS/CFT, provides a powerful and concrete framework for studying quantum gravity, where symmetry principles, black hole thermodynamics, and quantum entanglement are deeply intertwined. It underscores the paradigm that gravity is not fundamental but emergent from the entanglement structure of a non-gravitational quantum system.
\n\n
课程得出结论：全息原理，特别是通过AdS/CFT对偶，为研究量子引力提供了一个强大而具体的框架，其中对称性原理、黑洞热力学与量子纠缠深度交织。它强调了一种范式转变：引力并非基本相互作用，而是从一个无引力的量子系统的纠缠结构中涌现出来的。

Abstract: These are course notes for the 'Introduction to holography' Master level course at University of Cologne. The goal of the course is to give a pedogogical introduction to holography. Holography is a popular approach to quantum gravity, in which a theory of gravity can be described by a lower-dimensional boundary theory that itself has no gravity. The most concrete known example of a holographic model is the AdS/CFT correspondence, where the gravitational theory has a negative cosmological constant (the universe is asymptotically Anti-de Sitter) and the boundary theory is a conformal field theory. Symmetry plays a very important role in this duality. We therefore start the course with a review of Poincaré symmetry in quantum field theory, before moving on in the second chapter to conformal symmetry in conformally invariant quantum field theories or CFT's. Then we move to the basics of AdS physics in chapters 3 and 4, which will already reveal hints to the existence of a duality with CFT. After gathering the basic ingredients (CFT and AdS), in the second half of the course we are ready to formulate the AdS/CFT correspondence (chapter 5), including finite temperature AdS/CFT (chapter 6), which involves black holes and their thermodynamics in the gravitational theory (chapter 7). We end the course with an introduction to entanglement in AdS/CFT and the origin of statements that 'gravity emerges from entanglement' in holography.

### [48] [Discrete \texorpdfstring{$θ$}{theta} Projection: A Gauge-Protected Solution to the Strong CP Problem Without Axions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05195)
*Sameer Ahmad Mir,Bobby Eka Gunara,Mir Faizal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes "Discrete theta Projection," an axionless solution to the strong CP problem by gauging a discrete $Z_N$ subgroup of the $\theta$-angle shift symmetry. This orbifolds the QCD path integral, restricting instanton sectors and dynamically selecting the CP-conserving vacuum with $|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$, without fine-tuning. The mechanism ensures radiative and gravitational stability via higher-form/two-group symmetries and integer-quantized couplings from anomaly inflow, predicts suppressed neutron EDM ($\propto 1/N$), no axion phenomenology, and distinctive lattice signatures.
\n\n
本文提出“离散θ投影”（Discrete theta Projection）——一种无需轴子的强CP问题解决方案，通过对θ角平移对称性的离散$Z_N$子群进行规范（gauging），对QCD路径积分进行轨形化（orbifold），限制瞬子（instanton）扇区，并在无需微调的情况下动态选择CP守恒真空，满足$|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$。该机制通过高形式/二群（higher-form/two-group）对称性和由反常流入（anomaly inflow）确定的整数量子化耦合，确保辐射和引力稳定性，预言中子电偶极矩被压低（$\propto 1/N$）、无轴子信号、无畴壁/等曲率问题，并具有独特的格点诊断特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong CP problem arises because experimental limits on the neutron electric dipole moment require the physical QCD vacuum angle $\bar{\theta}$ to be unnaturally small ($\lesssim 10^{-10}$). While Peccei-Quinn axion models offer a dynamical relaxation, they rely on a global $U(1)$ symmetry that is expected to be broken by quantum gravity effects and are tightly constrained by astrophysical and cosmological observations. This motivates the search for alternative, axionless mechanisms that are robust against quantum gravity and do not introduce new light degrees of freedom or cosmological relics.
\n\n
强CP问题源于中子电偶极矩的实验上限要求物理QCD真空角$\bar{\theta}$异常小（$\lesssim 10^{-10}$）。尽管Peccei-Quinn轴子模型提供了动力学弛豫机制，但其依赖的全局$U(1)$对称性预期会被量子引力效应破坏，且受到天体物理和宇宙学观测的严格限制。这促使人们寻找替代性的、无需轴子的机制，这些机制应对量子引力稳健，且不引入新的轻自由度或宇宙学遗迹。

Method: The authors gauge a finite cyclic subgroup $Z_N$ of the continuous $2\pi$ shift symmetry of the QCD $\theta$-angle, coupling QCD to a compact, local, gapped topological field theory (TFT). This procedure orbifolds the total path integral, identifying $\theta \sim \theta + 2\pi/N$ and restricting the allowed instanton number to integer multiples of $N$. They show that in the infinite-volume limit, the vacuum energy is given by the lower envelope of the periodic images of the original QCD vacuum energy, thereby dynamically selecting the minimum closest to $\theta = 0$. The construction is formalized using higher-form and two-group global symmetries, with integer-quantized couplings fixed by anomaly inflow from a 5D bulk, ensuring consistency with mixed gauge-gravity anomalies and forbidding continuous renormalization of $\theta$.
\n\n
作者对QCD θ角的连续$2\pi$平移对称性的有限循环子群$Z_N$进行规范，将QCD与一个紧致、局域、能隙化的拓扑场论（TFT）耦合。此过程对总路径积分进行轨形化，识别$\theta \sim \theta + 2\pi/N$，并将允许的瞬子数限制为$N$的整数倍。他们证明，在无穷体积极限下，真空能量由原始QCD真空能量周期性图像的下包络给出，从而动态选择最接近$\theta = 0$的极小值。该构造通过高形式（higher-form）和二群（two-group）全局对称性形式化，其整数量子化耦合由来自五维体（5D bulk）的反常流入（anomaly inflow）固定，确保与混合规范-引力反常的一致性，并禁止θ的连续重整化。

Result: The mechanism dynamically enforces $|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$ without any initial fine-tuning. It predicts a neutron electric dipole moment suppressed by a factor of $1/N$, the absence of an axion or other light pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone bosons, and no associated domain wall or isocurvature problems. On the lattice, the vacuum energy as a function of $\theta$ is piecewise analytic with cusps at $\theta = (2k+1)\pi/N$, and its global curvature scales as $1/N^2$. The authors provide a complete effective field theory (EFT) formulation, a nonperturbative proof of the vacuum projection mechanism, a full analysis of 't Hooft anomalies, and explicit UV completions—including discrete clockwork models—that realize large $N$ while preserving all consistency conditions.
\n\n
该机制在无需初始微调的情况下动态强制$|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$。它预言中子电偶极矩被压低因子$1/N$，不存在轴子或其他轻赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子，也无相关的畴壁或等曲率问题。在格点上，作为θ函数的真空能量是分段解析的，在$\theta = (2k+1)\pi/N$处有尖点，其整体曲率按$1/N^2$缩放。作者提供了完整的有效场论（EFT）表述、真空投影机制的非微扰证明、完整的’t Hooft反常分析，以及明确的紫外（UV）完备化方案（包括离散发条（discrete clockwork）模型），这些方案在实现大$N$的同时保持了所有一致性条件。

Conclusion: Discrete theta Projection provides a theoretically robust, axionless resolution to the strong CP problem that is stable under quantum corrections and quantum gravity, thanks to its foundation in gauged discrete symmetries and topological field theory. It evades the pitfalls of axion models while making concrete, falsifiable predictions for neutron EDM experiments and lattice QCD simulations, offering a compelling alternative paradigm for addressing naturalness in QCD.
\n\n
离散θ投影（Discrete theta Projection）提供了一种理论上稳健的、无需轴子的强CP问题解决方案，其基于规范化的离散对称性和拓扑场论，对量子修正和量子引力效应稳定。该方案规避了轴子模型的缺陷，同时对中子电偶极矩实验和格点QCD模拟做出了具体且可证伪的预言，为解决QCD中的自然性问题提供了一个引人注目的替代范式。

Abstract: We address the strong CP problem: why the physical QCD angle theta-bar must be extraordinarily small given the stringent bounds on the neutron electric dipole moment. Peccei-Quinn axion models can relax theta-bar dynamically, but rely on an approximate global symmetry expected to be violated by quantum gravity and face severe astrophysical and cosmological constraints. We propose Discrete theta Projection, an axionless, gauge-protected resolution obtained by gauging a finite cyclic subgroup $Z_N $of the $2π$ shift symmetry of theta. Coupling QCD to a compact, local and gapped topological sector orbifolds the path integral, identifying theta values that differ by $2π/N$ and admitting only instanton sectors whose topological charge lies in $Z_N$. In the large four-volume limit the vacuum energy becomes the lower envelope of the orbifold images, so the theory dynamically selects the branch closest to the CP-symmetric point, enforcing $|\barθ| \le π/N$ without assuming any prior smallness. Because the discrete shift is gauged, continuous renormalization of theta is forbidden; the construction can be formulated via higher-form/two-group structure with integer-quantized couplings fixed by anomaly inflow, ensuring radiative and gravitational stability and satisfying mixed gauge-gravity consistency conditions. The framework predicts a neutron EDM suppressed by $1/N$, no axion signatures, no domain-wall/isocurvature issues, and lattice diagnostics: piecewise-analytic theta dependence with cusps at odd fractions of the reduced period and a global curvature scaling as $1/N^2$. We provide the EFT construction, a nonperturbative proof of vacuum projection, a full anomaly analysis, and UV embeddings (including discrete clockwork chains) that generate large effective N while preserving integrality and consistency throughout.

### [49] [3d-3d correspondence and abelian flat connection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05236)
*Hee-Joong Chung*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that the homological block of a knot complement in $S^3$ for $G_{\mathbb{C}} = SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$ can be realized as the half-index of a 3d $\\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric theory by expressing the homological block as an inverted Habiro series. The authors verify this through explicit examples and argue the construction generalizes to arbitrary knots. Additionally, they recover the colored Jones polynomial by selecting specific poles in the integral representation of the half-index.
\n\n
本文通过将同调块表示为倒置的Habiro级数，证明了对于 $G_{\\mathbb{C}} = SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$，$S^3$ 中纽结补空间的同调块（homological block）可实现为一个三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 超对称理论的半指标（half-index）。作者通过若干具体例子验证了该构造，并认为其可推广至一般纽结。此外，通过在半指标的积分表达式中选取特定极点，他们复现了colored Jones多项式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the conjectural relationship between quantum invariants of 3-manifolds (such as homological blocks and colored Jones polynomials) and supersymmetric partition functions of 3d $\\mathcal{N}=2$ theories. Specifically, the authors aim to realize the $SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$ homological block—a refinement of the Witten–Reshetikhin–Turaev invariant—as a physical observable (the half-index) in a dual 3d gauge theory, thereby bridging topological quantum field theory with supersymmetric localization techniques.
\n\n
动机源于三维流形的量子不变量（如同调块和colored Jones多项式）与三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 超对称理论配分函数之间的猜想性联系。作者特别旨在将 $SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$ 同调块——Witten–Reshetikhin–Turaev 不变量的一种精细化形式——实现为对偶三维规范理论中的物理可观测量（即半指标），从而在拓扑量子场论与超对称局域化技术之间建立桥梁。

Method: The authors express the homological block as an inverted Habiro series, which is a formal power series expansion suitable for analytic continuation beyond roots of unity. They then identify this series with the half-index—a supersymmetric partition function on $D^2 \\times S^1$ with Neumann boundary conditions—of a proposed 3d $\\mathcal{N}=2$ theory associated to the knot complement. Explicit computations are carried out for specific knots (e.g., trefoil, figure-eight). Furthermore, by evaluating the contour integral representation of the half-index and selecting poles corresponding to positive integer representations, they recover the colored Jones polynomial.
\n\n
作者将同调块表示为倒置的Habiro级数——一种适用于超越单位根进行解析延拓的形式幂级数。随后，他们将该级数与所提出的、对应于纽结补空间的三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 理论的半指标（即在具有Neumann边界条件的 $D^2 \\times S^1$ 上的超对称配分函数）相识别。文中对特定纽结（如三叶结、八字结）进行了显式计算。此外，通过对半指标的围道积分表达式进行求值，并选取对应于正整数表示的极点，他们复现了colored Jones多项式。

Result: The paper successfully realizes the $SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$ homological block of knot complements as the half-index of a 3d $\\mathcal{N}=2$ theory via the inverted Habiro series formulation. This correspondence is verified in concrete examples and is expected to hold generally. Moreover, the colored Jones polynomial emerges naturally from the same half-index by a specific choice of integration contour dictated by physical boundary conditions.
\n\n
本文成功地通过倒置Habiro级数形式，将纽结补空间的 $SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$ 同调块实现为三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 理论的半指标。该对应关系在具体例子中得到验证，并预期具有一般性。此外，通过由物理边界条件决定的特定积分围道选择，colored Jones多项式自然地从同一半指标中浮现。

Conclusion: The work establishes a concrete physical realization of homological blocks in terms of 3d $\\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric indices, reinforcing the deep connection between quantum topology and supersymmetric gauge theories. It provides a unified framework where both the homological block (a non-perturbative invariant) and the colored Jones polynomial (a perturbative invariant) arise from the same underlying half-index, differing only by the choice of integration contour or boundary conditions.
\n\n
本工作建立了同调块在三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 超对称指标下的具体物理实现，强化了量子拓扑与超对称规范理论之间的深刻联系。它提供了一个统一框架：同调块（非微扰不变量）与colored Jones多项式（微扰不变量）均源自同一底层半指标，仅因积分围道或边界条件的选择不同而表现各异。

Abstract: We realize a homological block of a knot complement in $S^3$ for $G_{\mathbb{C}}=SL(2,\mathbb{C})$ as a half-index of a 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ theory via an expression of the homological block as an inverted Habiro series by working out some examples, which we expect to extend to general knots. Also, by choosing a certain set of poles in the integral expression of the half-index, we obtain the colored Jones polynomial.

</details>


### [50] [Canonical Quantisation of Bound and Unbound WQFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05237)
*Riccardo Gonzo,Gustav Mogull*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper develops a canonical quantization approach to Worldline Quantum Field Theory (WQFT) that avoids the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral, enabling unified treatment of scattering and bound states in the classical two-body problem. By quantizing Hamilton's equations for two charged particles interacting via a scalar field—both in flat space (post-Lorentzian expansion) and around a background (self-force expansion)—the authors compute gauge-invariant matrix elements of the operator $\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$ up to 3PL order in the 1SF regime. These matrix elements describe both conservative and radiative dynamics and extend naturally to gravity and electromagnetism.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于正则量子化的Worldline Quantum Field Theory (WQFT)方法，摒弃了Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分，从而统一处理经典二体问题中的散射与束缚态。作者对通过标量场相互作用的两个带电粒子的哈密顿方程进行量子化——在平直空间中采用post-Lorentzian (PL)展开，在非零背景附近采用self-force (SF)展开——并计算算符$\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$的规范不变矩阵元，直至1SF框架下的3PL阶。这些矩阵元同时描述保守与辐射动力学，并可自然推广至引力和电磁相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional WQFT formulations rely on the Schwinger-Keldysh closed-time-path formalism, which is tailored for in-in expectation values and real-time evolution but can be cumbersome for extracting gauge-invariant observables in classical binary dynamics. The authors aim to construct a more direct, operator-based framework using canonical quantisation that treats both scattering (infinite time) and bound orbits (finite time) on equal footing, while cleanly separating conservative and radiative effects through the logarithm of the time-evolution operator $\hat{U}$.
\n\n
传统的WQFT表述依赖于Schwinger-Keldysh闭合时间路径形式，该方法适用于in-in期望值和实时演化，但在提取经典双星动力学中的规范不变可观测量时较为繁琐。作者旨在构建一个更直接的、基于算符的正则量子化框架，将散射（无限时间）与束缚轨道（有限时间）置于同等地位，并通过时间演化算符$\hat{U}$的对数清晰分离保守效应与辐射效应。

Method: The authors employ canonical quantisation of Hamilton’s equations for two point particles coupled to a scalar field. They consider two perturbative regimes: (i) post-Lorentzian (PL) expansion in flat spacetime for scattering, and (ii) self-force (SF) expansion around a fixed background for bound motion. The central object is the operator $\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$, whose Magnus expansion provides a systematic way to compute classical observables. Matrix elements of $\hat{N}$ are evaluated with and without external scalar states, yielding gauge-invariant results. The formalism avoids path integrals entirely, relying instead on operator algebra and time-ordered exponentials.
\n\n
作者对耦合到标量场的两个点粒子的哈密顿方程进行正则量子化。他们考虑两种微扰机制：(i) 平直时空中的post-Lorentzian (PL)展开用于散射；(ii) 固定背景附近的self-force (SF)展开用于束缚运动。核心对象是算符$\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$，其Magnus展开为计算经典可观测量提供了系统方法。通过含或不含外标量态的$\hat{N}$矩阵元计算，得到规范不变结果。该形式完全避免路径积分，转而依赖算符代数和时间序指数。

Result: The paper computes a complete set of gauge-invariant $\hat{N}$-matrix elements describing 1SF scattering dynamics up to 3PL order, as well as corresponding matrix elements for bound orbits. These encode physical observables such as scattering angles, binding energy shifts, and radiative losses. The framework successfully unifies conservative (time-symmetric) and radiative (time-asymmetric) contributions within a single operator formalism. The method is shown to generalize straightforwardly to both electromagnetic and gravitational interactions.
\n\n
本文计算了一组完整的规范不变$\hat{N}$矩阵元，描述1SF散射动力学直至3PL阶，并给出了对应的束缚轨道矩阵元。这些矩阵元编码了散射角、结合能修正和辐射损耗等物理可观测量。该框架成功地在单一算符形式下统一了保守（时间对称）与辐射（时间不对称）贡献。该方法被证明可直接推广至电磁与引力相互作用。

Conclusion: The canonical quantisation approach to WQFT provides a powerful, unified operator-based framework for classical binary dynamics, applicable to both scattering and bound states without recourse to the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism. By focusing on $\hat{N} = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}$, the method isolates physically meaningful, gauge-invariant observables and naturally accommodates both conservative and dissipative effects. Its extension to gravity suggests broad applicability in precision modeling of binary systems in general relativity and beyond.
\n\n
基于正则量子化的WQFT方法为经典双星动力学提供了一个强大而统一的算符框架，适用于散射与束缚态，且无需依赖Schwinger-Keldysh形式。通过聚焦于$\hat{N} = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}$，该方法分离出物理上有意义的规范不变可观测量，并自然容纳保守与耗散效应。其向引力理论的推广表明该方法在广义相对论及更广泛理论中对双星系统的高精度建模具有广阔应用前景。

Abstract: Using canonical quantisation, and eschewing the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral, we derive a version of the Worldline Quantum Field Theory (WQFT) formalism suitable for both scattering and bound configurations of the classical two-body problem. Focusing on a pair of charged particles interacting via a scalar field, we quantise Hamilton's equations both in flat space and around a non-zero background, perturbing in post-Lorentzian (PL) and self-force (SF) expansions respectively. Our quantisation procedure provides access to the Magnus series, and is perfectly suited for computing matrix elements of $\hat{N}(t,t_0)=- i \hbar \log\hat{U}(t,t_0)$, both with and without external scalar states, for finite time intervals (bound orbits) and infinite time intervals (scattering). Doing so, we provide a complete set of gauge-invariant matrix elements describing the 1SF scattering dynamics up to 3PL order, and corresponding matrix elements for bound orbits. We also demonstrate how $\hat{N}$-matrix elements encode physical observables, providing a unified operator-based framework for conservative and radiative dynamics of binary systems. The new WQFT formalism generalises naturally to both gravity and electromagnetism.

</details>


### [51] [Gauge-string duality, monomial bases and graph determinants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05259)
*Garreth Kemp,Sanjaye Ramgoolam*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces degeneracy graphs to study sequences of subalgebras in finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebras $\mathcal{A}$, where each subalgebra is generated by incrementally adding one generator. These graphs encode projectors in each subalgebra as nodes, and a monomial basis for $\mathcal{A}$ is constructed using combinatorial properties of the graph. The authors prove consistency with projector counting and provide explicit constructions for 1- and 2-layer cases, supported by computational evidence for general invertibility of the change-of-basis matrix (a Vandermonde determinant in the 1-layer case). Applications include constructing matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras, relevant to AdS/CFT and quantum information theory.
\n\n
本文引入退化图（degeneracy graphs）来研究有限维交换结合半单代数 $\mathcal{A}$ 中的子代数序列，其中每个子代数通过逐次添加一个生成元构建。这些图将各子代数中的投影算子（projectors）编码为节点，并利用图的组合性质构造出 $\mathcal{A}$ 的单项式基（monomial basis）。作者证明了该构造与 $\mathcal{A}$ 中投影算子的计数一致，并对单层和双层情形给出了显式构造，同时通过计算证据支持一般情形下基变换矩阵的可逆性（单层情形下为范德蒙行列式）。该构造在非交换半单代数中矩阵单位（matrix units）的算法构造中有应用，与 AdS/CFT 对应和量子信息理论相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from questions at the interface of the AdS/CFT correspondence and quantum information theory, which require understanding the structure of projectors in nested sequences of subalgebras of a finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebra $\mathcal{A}$. Such projectors are essential for decomposing algebras into irreducible components and for constructing orthogonal bases of gauge-invariant operators, which appear in holographic duality and quantum error correction. The challenge lies in systematically generating these projectors when the algebra is built non-linearly by adjoining generators one at a time.
\n\n
动机源于 AdS/CFT 对应与量子信息理论交叉领域的问题，这些问题要求理解有限维交换结合半单代数 $\mathcal{A}$ 的嵌套子代数序列中投影算子（projectors）的结构。这类投影算子对于将代数分解为不可约分量、以及构造规范不变算子的正交基至关重要，而后者出现在全息对偶和量子纠错中。核心挑战在于：当代数通过逐次添加生成元以非线性方式构建时，如何系统地生成这些投影算子。

Method: The authors introduce degeneracy graphs—finite layered tree graphs where each node corresponds to a projector in a subalgebra obtained at a given step of generator adjunction. Nodes are labeled by formal variables representing eigenvalues of the newly added generator. Using the combinatorial structure of these graphs, they construct a linear basis of $\mathcal{A}$ consisting of monomials in the generators. They then relate this monomial basis to the natural projector basis via a change-of-basis matrix and analyze its invertibility. Explicit formulas for projectors are derived in the 1- and 2-layer cases, and extensive numerical computations support a conjectured formula for the determinant of the transformation matrix in the general case.
\n\n
作者引入退化图（degeneracy graphs）——一种有限分层树图，其中每个节点对应于在某一步添加生成元后所得子代数中的一个投影算子。节点用形式变量标记，代表新添加生成元的本征值。利用这些图的组合结构，他们构造出由生成元的单项式组成的 $\mathcal{A}$ 的线性基。随后，他们通过一个基变换矩阵将此单项式基与自然的投影算子基联系起来，并分析其可逆性。在单层和双层情形下推导出投影算子的显式公式，并通过大量数值计算支持对一般情形下变换矩阵行列式的猜想公式。

Result: The paper establishes a combinatorial framework linking degeneracy graphs to the structure of commutative semisimple algebras built incrementally. It proves that the monomial basis constructed from the graph correctly reproduces the expected number of projectors in $\mathcal{A}$. Explicit expressions for projectors are given for 1- and 2-layer graphs with arbitrary node counts. The change-of-basis matrix between monomials and projectors is shown to be invertible: its determinant is a Vandermonde determinant in the 1-layer case, and computational evidence supports a simple non-vanishing formula for the determinant in multi-layer cases. Examples include centers of symmetric group algebras and algebras generated by Jucys-Murphy elements.
\n\n
本文建立了一个组合框架，将退化图与逐步构建的交换半单代数结构联系起来。证明了从图构造的单项式基能正确复现 $\mathcal{A}$ 中预期的投影算子数量。对任意节点数的单层和双层图给出了投影算子的显式表达式。单项式基与投影算子基之间的变换矩阵被证明是可逆的：单层情形下其行列式为范德蒙行列式，多层情形下则通过计算证据支持一个简单的非零行列式公式。示例包括对称群代数的中心和由 Jucys-Murphy 元素生成的极大交换子代数。

Conclusion: The degeneracy graph approach provides a systematic and computationally tractable method to construct projector bases in incrementally generated commutative semisimple algebras. This construction not only clarifies the algebraic structure underlying such sequences but also enables practical algorithms for building matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras. These results have direct implications for constructing orthogonal bases of multi-trace gauge-invariant operators in AdS/CFT and for tasks in quantum information theory involving operator algebras and their decompositions.
\n\n
退化图方法为在逐步生成的交换半单代数中构造投影算子基提供了一种系统且计算可行的方法。该构造不仅阐明了此类代数序列背后的代数结构，还为在非交换半单代数中构建矩阵单位（matrix units）提供了实用算法。这些结果对 AdS/CFT 中多迹规范不变算子的正交基构造，以及量子信息理论中涉及算子代数及其分解的任务具有直接意义。

Abstract: Questions at the intersection of the AdS/CFT correspondence and quantum information theory motivate the study of projectors in sequences of subalgebras of finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebras $\mathcal{A}$, obtained by incrementally adjoining one generator at each step to produce a non-linear generating set for $\mathcal{A}$. We define degeneracy graphs, which are finite layered tree graphs whose nodes represent projectors in the successive subalgebras. Using combinatorial properties of the degeneracy graph, we give a simple formula for constructing a linear basis of $\mathcal{A}$ in terms of monomials in the generators.The nodes can be labelled by formal variables corresponding to the eigenvalues of the generators added at each layer. We prove that the construction is compatible with the required counting of projectors in $\mathcal{A}$, and give explicit constructions of the projectors in terms of the monomials, in the cases of one- and two-layer degeneracy graphs with arbitrary numbers of nodes. More generally, we provide extensive computational evidence for the invertibility of the matrix relating the proposed monomial basis to the projector basis, by evaluating its determinant. In the 1-layer case, this is a Vandermonde determinant. A simple formula for the non-vanishing determinant in the general layer case is conjectured and supported by the computational data. The construction is illustrated with examples including centres of symmetric group algebras and maximally commuting subalgebras generated by JucysMurphy elements. We outline applications of the monomial basis to algorithms for constructing matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras, with relevance to orthogonal bases of multi-matrix gauge-invariant operators and to quantum information theory.

</details>


### [52] [7D (non-)susy vacua & DWs from dynamical open strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05470)
*Valentina Bevilacqua,Giuseppe Dibitetto,Giuseppe Sudano*

TL;DR: The paper investigates warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity on $S^3$ with spacetime-filling O6/D6 sources, extending the 7D half-maximal gauged supergravity description by including open string degrees of freedom (scalars and fluxes). This is achieved by coupling extra vector multiplets to the gravity multiplet and modifying the embedding tensor. New AdS$_7$ vacua—both supersymmetric and non-supersymmetric—are found, along with domain wall solutions connecting them, obtained analytically and numerically.
\n\n
本文研究了带有时空填充O6/D6源的massive type IIA超引力在$S^3$上的翘曲紧化，通过引入开弦自由度（标量和通量）扩展了7维半极大规范超引力描述。该扩展通过将额外矢量多重态与引力多重态耦合并修改embedding tensor实现。理论标量势展现出新的AdS$_7$真空解（包括超对称与非超对称情形），并给出了连接不同真空的畴壁解（解析与数值解）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how open string degrees of freedom associated with spacetime-filling D-branes and orientifold planes influence lower-dimensional effective supergravity descriptions. While the closed string sector of such compactifications is captured by 7D half-maximal gauged supergravity, incorporating open string modes requires extending the field content and gauging structure. This extension is crucial for exploring new vacuum structures and interpolating solutions in AdS/CFT and string phenomenology contexts.

动机源于理解与时空填充D膜和orientifold平面相关的开弦自由度如何影响低维有效超引力描述。尽管此类紧化的闭弦部分已被7维半极大规范超引力所描述，但纳入开弦模要求扩展会场内容和规范结构。这种扩展对于探索AdS/CFT及弦唯象学中新真空结构和插值解至关重要。

Method: The authors extend the 7D half-maximal ($\mathcal{N}=2$) gauged supergravity by coupling additional vector multiplets that encode open string scalars and fluxes. They generalize the embedding tensor formalism to include new components corresponding to the couplings induced by O6/D6 sources. The scalar potential is then derived from this extended gauged supergravity framework, and its critical points are analyzed to identify AdS$_7$ vacua. Domain wall solutions are constructed by solving first-order BPS equations (for supersymmetric cases) or second-order equations of motion (for non-supersymmetric cases), yielding both analytical and numerical interpolating geometries.
\n\n
作者通过耦合额外矢量多重态（编码开弦标量和通量）来扩展7维半极大（$\mathcal{N}=2$）规范超引力。他们推广了embedding tensor形式体系，纳入由O6/D6源诱导的新耦合分量。随后从该扩展框架导出标量势，并分析其临界点以识别AdS$_7$真空。畴壁解通过求解一阶BPS方程（超对称情形）或二阶运动方程（非超对称情形）构造，得到解析与数值插值几何。

Result: The extended 7D supergravity admits novel AdS$_7$ vacuum solutions, both preserving and breaking supersymmetry. These vacua arise due to the modified scalar potential from the inclusion of open string modes via extra vector multiplets and an enriched embedding tensor. The paper also presents explicit domain wall solutions—analytical in supersymmetric cases and numerical otherwise—that interpolate between pairs of these vacua, demonstrating rich dynamical connections in the landscape of 7D supergravity.
\n\n
扩展后的7维超引力展现出新的AdS$_7$真空解，既包含保持超对称的情形，也包含破缺超对称的情形。这些真空源于通过额外矢量多重态和更丰富的embedding tensor引入开弦模后修正的标量势。论文还给出了显式的畴壁解——超对称情形下为解析解，否则为数值解——在不同真空对之间插值，展示了7维超引力景观中丰富的动力学联系。

Conclusion: Including open string degrees of freedom in warped compactifications of massive type IIA leads to a consistent extension of 7D half-maximal gauged supergravity with richer vacuum structure. The resulting theory supports new AdS$_7$ vacua and domain walls, enhancing our understanding of holographic duals and the role of localized sources in dimensional reduction. This framework provides a controlled setting to study non-supersymmetric AdS solutions and their stability within string theory.
\n\n
在massive type IIA的翘曲紧化中纳入开弦自由度，可一致地扩展7维半极大规范超引力，并带来更丰富的真空结构。所得理论支持新的AdS$_7$真空和畴壁，深化了我们对全息对偶及局域源在维度约化中作用的理解。该框架为研究弦理论中非超对称AdS解及其稳定性提供了可控环境。

Abstract: Warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity on a 3-sphere with spacetime-filling O6/D6 sources are known to admit a half-maximal gauged supergravity description in 7D. We study the effect of introducing open string degrees of freedom (scalars and fluxes) in such dimensional reductions, associated with the spacetime-filling sources. From the 7D supergravity point of view, this can be realized by coupling the gravity multiplet with extra vector multiplets and adding new components to the embedding tensor describing the gauging. The scalar potential of the underlying theory exhibits novel AdS7 vacuum solutions, with and without supersymmetry. Finally, we explore the net of domain wall solutions interpolating between the different pairs of vacua, and present analytical as well as numerical solutions.

### [53] [Scattering amplitudes in dimensionless quadratic gravity coupled to QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05476)
*I. F. Cunha,A. C. Lehum*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper computes tree-level $2\to2$ scattering amplitudes in agravity—a scale-invariant, renormalizable quadratic gravity theory—coupled to Abelian gauge fields and matter (charged fermions and scalars). It provides analytic expressions for unpolarized squared matrix elements across multiple channels, includes photon–graviton interference, confirms gauge independence, and reveals universal ultra-Planckian differential cross sections scaling as $d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$.
\n\n
本文计算了在agravity（一种尺度不变、可重整化的二次量子引力理论）与Abelian规范场及物质（带电费米子和标量）耦合下的树图阶$2\to2$散射振幅。文章给出了多个散射道的无极化平方矩阵元解析表达式，包含了光子–引力子干涉项，验证了结果对引力规范固定参数的独立性，并揭示了微分截面在超普朗克能区具有普适标度律$d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how higher-derivative quantum gravity (specifically agravity) modifies standard QED-like scattering processes at ultra-Planckian energies. Previous studies often neglected gauge boson–graviton interference or focused only on pure graviton exchange; this work aims to provide a complete amplitude-level picture including all relevant tree-level contributions and to establish universal high-energy behavior in the presence of both gauge and gravitational interactions.
\n\n
动机在于理解高阶导数量子引力（特别是agravity）如何在超普朗克能量下修正标准类QED散射过程。以往研究常忽略规范玻色子–引力子干涉或仅关注纯引力子交换；本文旨在提供一个包含所有相关树图贡献的完整振幅级图像，并确立在规范与引力相互作用共存下的普适高能行为。

Method: The authors compute tree-level $2\to2$ scattering amplitudes in a theory combining agravity (with a $1/p^4$ graviton propagator due to higher-derivative terms) and Abelian gauge theory. They consider charged fermions and scalars interacting with photons and gravitons, systematically include photon–graviton interference diagrams, and calculate unpolarized squared matrix elements for various channels. Gauge independence is explicitly verified by showing results are insensitive to the gravitational gauge-fixing parameter. The analysis leverages the dimensionless nature of agravity couplings and the structure of the higher-derivative graviton propagator.
\n\n
作者在结合agravity（因高阶导数项导致引力子传播子为$1/p^4$）与Abelian规范理论的框架下计算树图阶$2\to2$散射振幅。他们考虑带电费米子和标量与光子及引力子的相互作用，系统地包含光子–引力子干涉图，并计算多个散射道的无极化平方矩阵元。通过显式验证结果对引力规范固定参数的不敏感性来确认规范无关性。分析利用了agravity耦合的无量纲特性及高阶导数引力子传播子的结构。

Result: The key results are: (1) compact analytic formulas for unpolarized squared matrix elements across seven distinct scattering channels; (2) explicit confirmation that amplitudes are independent of the gravitational gauge-fixing parameter; (3) observation of forward/backward enhancements due to the $1/p^4$ graviton propagator; (4) universal ultra-Planckian scaling of differential cross sections as $d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$ for all channels, reflecting the dimensionless gravitational couplings in agravity.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 七个不同散射道的无极化平方矩阵元的紧凑解析公式；(2) 显式验证振幅对引力规范固定参数的独立性；(3) 由于$1/p^4$引力子传播子导致的前向/后向增强效应；(4) 所有散射道的微分截面在超普朗克能区均呈现普适标度律$d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$，反映了agravity中引力耦合的无量纲特性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that agravity induces universal high-energy behavior in matter scattering through its higher-derivative graviton, with interference between gauge and gravitational interactions playing a crucial role. The analytic amplitudes serve as foundational inputs for future investigations into infrared definitions, ultraviolet consistency, and potential phenomenological signatures of scale-invariant quantum gravity coupled to matter.
\n\n
研究表明，agravity通过其高阶导数引力子在物质散射中诱导出普适的高能行为，其中规范与引力相互作用的干涉起关键作用。所得解析振幅为未来研究红外定义、紫外一致性以及与物质耦合的尺度不变量子引力的潜在唯象信号提供了基础输入。

Abstract: We study ultra-Planckian $2\to2$ scattering in an Abelian gauge theory coupled to agravity, the scale-free and renormalizable realization of quadratic quantum gravity. Focusing on charged fermions and scalars interacting with the photon and the higher-derivative graviton, we present compact analytic expressions for the unpolarized squared matrix elements for a broad set of tree-level processes, including photon--photon, fermion--fermion, fermion--photon, scalar--fermion, scalar--photon, scalar--scalar, and annihilation channels. In contrast to purely graviton-mediated analyses, we retain systematically the photon--graviton interference contributions and verify explicitly the independence of the results on the gravitational gauge-fixing parameter. The amplitudes display characteristic forward/backward enhancements associated with small momentum transfer, amplified by the $1/p^{4}$ graviton propagator, while their high-energy scaling reflects the underlying dimensionless gravitational couplings. Moreover, for all channels analyzed the corresponding differential cross sections exhibit the universal ultra-Planckian scaling $dσ/dΩ\propto 1/s$, where $s$ is the Mandelstam invariant (the squared center-of-momentum energy). Our results furnish a unified amplitude-level description of how higher-derivative gravity reshapes familiar QED scattering at ultra-Planckian energies and provide analytic building blocks for further studies of IR definitions and UV consistency in agravity with matter.

</details>
