### [54] [Reheating after Starobinsky Inflation in the Jordan Frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04497)
*Gláuber C. Dorsch,Luiz Carlos Miranda,Nelson Yokomizo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies gravitational reheating in the Jordan-frame Starobinsky $R^2$ inflation model, where no inflaton field exists and reheating occurs solely via gravitational particle production from Ricci scalar oscillations. The authors find that the background behaves like pressureless matter during reheating, include backreaction to show exponential damping of oscillations, compute a reheating temperature $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV, and highlight frame-dependent differences between Jordan and Einstein descriptions when quantum effects are considered.
\n\n
本文研究了Jordan框架下Starobinsky $R^2$暴胀模型中的引力再加热过程，该模型不含显式的inflaton场，再加热完全由Ricci标量振荡引发的引力粒子产生机制驱动。作者发现背景在再加热阶段表现为无压物质，计入反作用后Ricci标量振荡呈指数衰减，从而自然终止粒子产生，并计算出再加热温度 $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV。文章最后指出，尽管Jordan框架与Einstein框架在经典层面等价，但在考虑量子效应时可能导致不同的微观物理解释和定量预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the fact that in the Jordan frame formulation of the Starobinsky model—where inflation arises from an $R^2$ correction to the Einstein–Hilbert action without introducing a fundamental scalar inflaton—the mechanism of reheating must be purely gravitational. Understanding how particle production occurs in this setting, how the background evolves post-inflation, and whether quantum effects introduce frame dependence are crucial for a complete picture of early-universe cosmology in modified gravity theories.
\n\n
动机源于Starobinsky模型在Jordan框架下的表述：暴胀由Einstein–Hilbert作用量的$R^2$修正项驱动，无需引入基本标量inflaton场，因此再加热机制必须完全是引力性的。理解在此设定下粒子如何产生、暴胀后背景如何演化，以及量子效应是否引入框架依赖性，对于构建修改引力理论中早期宇宙演化的完整图像至关重要。

Method: The authors work directly in the Jordan frame of $f(R) = R + R^2/(6M^2)$ gravity. They first solve the modified Friedmann equations to obtain the post-inflationary background dynamics, identifying an effective fluid with equation of state $w \approx 0$. They then compute gravitational particle production using the time-varying Ricci scalar $R(t)$ as the source, treating it as a classical background. Crucially, they incorporate the backreaction of produced particles via Boltzmann equations coupled to the background evolution, leading to a damped oscillatory solution for $R(t)$. Finally, they compare results with the Einstein-frame formulation, emphasizing the role of quantum corrections in breaking classical equivalence.
\n\n
作者直接在$f(R) = R + R^2/(6M^2)$引力的Jordan框架中工作。首先求解修改后的Friedmann方程以获得暴胀后的背景动力学，识别出一个状态方程参数$w \approx 0$的有效流体。随后，利用随时间变化的Ricci标量$R(t)$作为源项计算引力粒子产生，将其视为经典背景。关键步骤是通过Boltzmann方程将产生粒子的反作用耦合到背景演化中，从而得到$R(t)$的阻尼振荡解。最后，他们将结果与Einstein框架表述进行比较，强调量子修正会破坏经典等价性。

Result: The post-inflationary phase in the Jordan frame is dominated by an effective pressureless fluid arising from the $R^2$ dynamics. Gravitational particle production from coherent $R(t)$ oscillations yields a reheating temperature $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}~\mathrm{GeV}$. Backreaction induces exponential damping of the Ricci scalar oscillations, naturally ending reheating. The analysis reveals that while the Jordan and Einstein frames are classically equivalent, quantum effects (e.g., non-minimal couplings, vacuum definitions) can lead to different physical predictions for reheating observables.
\n\n
Jordan框架中暴胀后的相由$R^2$动力学导出的有效无压流体主导。Ricci标量$R(t)$的相干振荡通过引力机制产生粒子，给出再加热温度$T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}~\mathrm{GeV}$。反作用导致Ricci标量振荡呈指数衰减，自然终结再加热过程。分析表明，尽管Jordan框架与Einstein框架在经典层面等价，但量子效应（如非最小耦合、真空定义）可能导致对再加热可观测量的不同物理预言。

Conclusion: Gravitational reheating in the Jordan-frame Starobinsky model is viable and yields a well-defined reheating temperature. The effective matter-like behavior during reheating and the self-consistent inclusion of backreaction provide a robust description of the transition to radiation domination. Importantly, the study cautions against assuming full physical equivalence between Jordan and Einstein frames beyond the classical level, as quantum effects can introduce observable differences in reheating dynamics.
\n\n
Jordan框架下Starobinsky模型的引力再加热机制是可行的，并能给出明确的再加热温度。再加热期间表现出的有效物质行为以及自洽地包含反作用，为向辐射主导时期的过渡提供了稳健描述。重要的是，本研究提醒人们不应假设Jordan框架与Einstein框架在超出经典层面后仍完全物理等价，因为量子效应可能在再加热动力学中引入可观测的差异。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational reheating in the Starobinsky model in the Jordan frame, where inflation is driven by an $R^2$ modification of gravity with no explicit inflaton field. In this description, reheating proceeds exclusively through gravitational particle production triggered by the oscillations of the Ricci scalar after the end of inflation. We analyze the post-inflationary background evolution and show that an effective fluid emerging from the modified gravitational dynamics behaves as pressureless matter during the oscillatory phase. Including the backreaction of the produced particles, we demonstrate that the Ricci scalar oscillations acquire an exponential damping, consistently terminating particle production. Solving the coupled background and Boltzmann equations, we obtain a reheating temperature $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV. We finally compare the Jordan and Einstein frame descriptions and argue that, although classically equivalent, they can lead to distinct microphysical interpretations and quantitative predictions for reheating once quantum effects are taken into account.

</details>


### [55] [Nonlinear Dynamics in General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04501)
*Vitor Cardoso,Jaime Redondo-Yuste,Ulrich Sperhake,Furkan Tuncer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reveals new nonlinear phenomena in gravity—specifically higher harmonic generation, spectral broadening, and focusing—in the Einstein–Klein–Gordon system. It shows that at quadratic order in perturbation theory, monochromatic gravitational waves in vacuum exhibit weak frequency dependence at long wavelengths, which may account for the smoothness of merger waveforms while warning against overly simplistic waveform modeling.
\n\n
本文揭示了引力中的新非线性现象——特别是在 Einstein–Klein–Gordon 系统中的高次谐波生成、谱展宽和聚焦效应。文章表明，在微扰理论的二次阶下，真空中的单色引力波在长波长极限下对频率仅有微弱依赖性，这可能解释了并合波形的平滑性，同时也警示我们避免对波形进行过于简化的建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While black holes and gravitational waves are well-known nonlinear outcomes of General Relativity, the authors seek to uncover additional, less-explored nonlinear features of the Einstein equations. They aim to understand how these subtle effects—such as higher harmonic generation and spectral broadening—manifest in fundamental field-gravity couplings like the Einstein–Klein–Gordon system, and how they influence the interpretation of observed gravitational waveforms from compact binary mergers.
\n\n
尽管黑洞和引力波是广义相对论中广为人知的非线性结果，作者试图揭示爱因斯坦方程中其他较少被探索的非线性特征。他们旨在理解这些微妙效应（如高次谐波生成和谱展宽）如何在 Einstein–Klein–Gordon 等基本场-引力耦合系统中体现，并影响对致密双星并合所产生引力波形的解释。

Method: The authors employ perturbative analysis of the Einstein–Klein–Gordon system, expanding the metric and scalar field around flat spacetime. They compute scattering amplitudes at quadratic order in the perturbation, focusing on the interaction of monochromatic gravitational waves. Using techniques from nonlinear wave theory and effective field theory, they analyze frequency dependence, harmonic content, and spatial focusing properties of the scattered waves in the long-wavelength (infrared) regime.
\n\n
作者采用对 Einstein–Klein–Gordon 系统的微扰分析，将度规和标量场在平直时空背景下展开。他们在微扰的二次阶计算散射振幅，聚焦于单色引力波的相互作用。利用非线性波理论和有效场论（EFT）方法，分析了在长波长（红外）极限下散射波的频率依赖性、谐波成分和空间聚焦特性。

Result: The study demonstrates that the Einstein–Klein–Gordon system exhibits higher harmonic generation and spectral broadening due to nonlinear interactions. In vacuum, quadratic-order scattering of monochromatic gravitational waves shows only weak sensitivity to frequency at large wavelengths ($\lambda \gg r_s$). This weak dispersion helps explain the empirically observed smoothness of merger waveforms, but also implies that waveform models ignoring such nonlinearities may be misleading.
\n\n
研究表明，Einstein–Klein–Gordon 系统因非线性相互作用而表现出高次谐波生成和谱展宽。在真空中，单色引力波在二次阶散射下于长波长（$\lambda \gg r_s$）极限中仅对频率有微弱依赖性。这种弱色散性有助于解释观测到的并合波形的平滑性，但也意味着忽略此类非线性的波形模型可能是误导性的。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that beyond black hole formation and gravitational wave emission, General Relativity harbors richer nonlinear dynamics—such as harmonic generation and spectral broadening—even in weak-field regimes. These effects, though subtle, have tangible implications for gravitational waveform interpretation and underscore the need for more sophisticated theoretical models that incorporate higher-order nonlinearities in the Einstein equations.
\n\n
本文指出，除了黑洞形成和引力波辐射之外，广义相对论即使在弱场区域也蕴含更丰富的非线性动力学——如谐波生成和谱展宽。这些效应虽微弱，却对引力波形的解释具有实际影响，强调了发展更精细理论模型的必要性，以纳入爱因斯坦方程中的高阶非线性项。

Abstract: Black holes and gravitational waves are consequences of the nonlinear character of the Einstein equations. Yet, the remarkable properties of General Relativity point to the existence of other effects. Here we uncover new nonlinear facets of gravity. We establish higher harmonic generation, spectral broadening and focusing in the Einstein Klein-Gordon system. In vacuum, we show that scattering of monochromatic waves at quadratic order is weakly sensitive to frequency, at large wavelengths. These aspects can both explain the seemingly smooth behavior of mergers, but also caution us against too simplistic an interpretation of waveforms.

</details>


### [56] [Aspects of Relativity in Flat Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04574)
*C. J. Papachristou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This monograph provides a rigorous mathematical treatment of Special Relativity, emphasizing the structure and representations of the Lorentz group and their applications in relativistic mechanics and electrodynamics. An appendix has been added to the original published book manuscript.
\n\n
本专著对狭义相对论进行了严格的数学处理，重点强调Lorentz群的结构与表示及其在相对论力学和电动力学中的应用。原已出版的书稿新增了一个附录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to present a mathematically precise foundation for Special Relativity by analyzing the Lorentz group—the symmetry group of Minkowski spacetime—and to clarify how its representation theory underpins physical laws in relativistic mechanics and classical electrodynamics.
\n\n
其动机在于通过分析Lorentz群（即Minkowski时空的对称群）来为狭义相对论提供一个数学上精确的基础，并阐明其表示理论如何支撑相对论力学和经典电动力学中的物理定律。

Method: The paper employs group-theoretic methods, focusing on the Lie algebra and representation theory of the Lorentz group $SO(1,3)$, to derive transformation properties of physical quantities such as four-vectors, tensors, and spinors. It systematically applies these mathematical tools to problems in relativistic dynamics and Maxwell’s equations.
\n\n
本文采用群论方法，聚焦于Lorentz群 $SO(1,3)$ 的李代数与表示理论，推导四维矢量、张量和旋量等物理量的变换性质，并系统地将这些数学工具应用于相对论动力学和Maxwell方程的问题中。

Result: The monograph establishes a clear correspondence between the irreducible representations of the Lorentz group and fundamental physical fields, demonstrating how covariance under Lorentz transformations constrains the form of mechanical and electromagnetic laws. The added appendix likely extends or clarifies technical aspects of the core exposition.
\n\n
该专著建立了Lorentz群不可约表示与基本物理场之间的明确对应关系，展示了Lorentz变换下的协变性如何约束力学和电磁学定律的形式。新增的附录可能对核心论述中的技术细节进行了扩展或澄清。

Conclusion: The work underscores the centrality of the Lorentz group in the mathematical formulation of Special Relativity and provides a foundational reference for understanding relativistic physics through the lens of group representation theory.
\n\n
本工作强调了Lorentz群在狭义相对论数学表述中的核心地位，并通过群表示理论的视角，为理解相对论物理提供了基础性参考。

Abstract: A monograph on the mathematical aspects of Special Relativity, focusing on the Lorentz group and the properties of relativistic transformations in mechanics and electrodynamics. Manuscript of published book, with an added appendix.

</details>


### [57] [Cosmological black holes in the inflationary epoch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04590)
*Ertola Urtubey Milos,Daniela Pérez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies primordial black holes (PBHs) during inflation using a generalized McVittie metric where black hole mass scales with the cosmic scale factor. Within Starobinsky's $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model, it combines cosmological coupling, Hawking evaporation, and radiation accretion across all cosmic eras. Imposing physical constraints—such as the black hole horizon being smaller than the particle horizon, avoidance of runaway accretion, and survival through evaporation—leads to a narrow viable initial mass window. Surviving PBHs today have a maximum mass of $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$.
\n\n
本文在Starobinsky $\mathcal{R}^2$ 暴胀模型框架下，利用广义McVittie度规研究暴胀时期原初黑洞（PBH）的演化，其中黑洞质量随宇宙标度因子缩放。综合考虑宇宙学耦合、Hawking蒸发和辐射吸积在暴胀、辐射、物质及暗能量时期的共同作用，并施加物理约束（如黑洞视界始终小于粒子视界、避免吸积失控、确保蒸发后仍能存活），得出仅存在一个狭窄的初始质量窗口允许黑洞存续至今，其当前最大质量为 $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand whether primordial black holes formed during inflation can survive to the present day under realistic physical processes, including their dynamical coupling to the expanding universe, quantum evaporation via Hawking radiation, and classical accretion of ambient radiation. Previous treatments often neglect the interplay of these effects across all cosmic epochs or assume static black hole masses, which may not hold in an evolving spacetime like that of inflation.
\n\n
动机在于探究在暴胀时期形成的原初黑洞是否能在包含宇宙学耦合、Hawking量子蒸发和环境辐射经典吸积等真实物理过程的综合作用下存续至今。以往研究常忽略这些效应在所有宇宙时期中的相互作用，或假设黑洞质量恒定，而这在暴胀等动态时空背景下可能不成立。

Method: The authors employ a generalized McVittie geometry to model black holes whose gravitational mass $M(t)$ scales with the cosmic scale factor $a(t)$, i.e., $M(t) \propto a(t)$. They adopt Starobinsky’s $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model to specify the background expansion history. The evolution of black hole mass is governed by a differential equation incorporating three contributions: (1) cosmological coupling ($\\dot{M}_{\\text{cos}} = HM$), (2) Hawking evaporation ($\\dot{M}_{\\text{evap}} \\propto -1/M^2$), and (3) radiation accretion during the radiation-dominated era ($\\dot{M}_{\\text{acc}} \\propto \\rho_{\\text{rad}} M^2$). Constraints are imposed: (i) $r_s(t) < d_p(t)$ (Schwarzschild radius smaller than particle horizon), (ii) no runaway accretion ($\\dot{M}_{\\text{acc}}$ bounded), and (iii) $M(t_{\\text{end}}) > 0$ after inflation to avoid complete evaporation.
\n\n
作者采用广义McVittie几何来描述引力质量 $M(t)$ 随宇宙标度因子 $a(t)$ 缩放（即 $M(t) \\propto a(t)$）的黑洞。背景宇宙演化由Starobinsky $\mathcal{R}^2$ 暴胀模型确定。黑洞质量演化由包含三项贡献的微分方程控制：(1) 宇宙学耦合（$\\dot{M}_{\\text{cos}} = HM$），(2) Hawking蒸发（$\\dot{M}_{\\text{evap}} \\propto -1/M^2$），(3) 辐射主导时期的辐射吸积（$\\dot{M}_{\\text{acc}} \\propto \\rho_{\\text{rad}} M^2$）。施加三项约束：(i) $r_s(t) < d_p(t)$（Schwarzschild半径小于粒子视界），(ii) 无失控吸积（$\\dot{M}_{\\text{acc}}$ 有界），(iii) 暴胀结束后 $M(t_{\\text{end}}) > 0$ 以避免完全蒸发。

Result: The analysis yields a narrow allowed range for the initial black hole mass at formation during inflation. The upper bound arises from requiring the black hole event horizon to remain within the particle horizon throughout cosmic history, while the lower bound comes from ensuring the black hole does not completely evaporate before the end of inflation. Radiation accretion during the radiation era further restricts the parameter space by preventing excessive growth. The surviving population today has a maximum mass of $M(t_0) \\simeq 1.043\\times10^{-3} M_\\odot$, implying such PBHs cannot account for dark matter or observed astrophysical black holes.
\n\n
分析得出暴胀时期形成时黑洞初始质量的狭窄允许范围：上限源于要求黑洞事件视界在宇宙历史中始终小于粒子视界，下限则确保黑洞在暴胀结束前不被完全蒸发。辐射时期吸积进一步限制参数空间以防止过度增长。存续至今的黑洞最大质量为 $M(t_0) \\simeq 1.043\\times10^{-3} M_\\odot$，表明此类原初黑洞无法解释暗物质或已观测到的天体物理黑洞。

Conclusion: Primordial black holes formed during inflation with masses dynamically coupled to the scale factor can only survive to the present if their initial mass lies within a very narrow window. The combined effects of cosmological coupling, Hawking evaporation, and radiation accretion—when consistently applied across all cosmic eras—severely limit their viability as significant cosmological components. This result underscores the importance of self-consistent modeling of black hole dynamics in time-dependent backgrounds.
\n\n
在暴胀时期形成且质量与标度因子动态耦合的原初黑洞，只有在其初始质量处于极窄窗口内时才能存续至今。当宇宙学耦合、Hawking蒸发和辐射吸积在所有宇宙时期中被一致地纳入考虑时，它们作为重要宇宙学组分的可能性被严重限制。该结果强调了在含时背景中对黑洞动力学进行自洽建模的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate the evolution of black holes present during the inflationary epoch, assuming they are dynamically coupled to the cosmological background through a generalized McVittie geometry, such that their gravitational mass scales with the cosmic scale factor. Adopting Starobinsky's $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model, we analyse the combined effects of cosmological coupling, Hawking evaporation and radiation accretion during the subsequent cosmic eras: inflation, radiation, matter, and dark energy. Requiring the black hole event horizon to remain smaller than the particle horizon at all times yields an upper bound on the mass parameter. Radiation accretion during the radiation era further constrains the parameter space to prevent runaway growth. Hawking evaporation sets a lower bound on the initial mass to ensure survival through inflation. We find that only black holes formed within a narrow initial mass range during inflation can persist to the present day, reaching a maximum mass of $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$.

</details>


### [58] [Junction Conditions for General Gravitational Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04645)
*José M. M. Senovilla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper derives junction conditions for general gravitational theories with Lagrangians depending on arbitrary functions of curvature scalar invariants (including differential invariants) using distributional methods. It provides a general expression for thin-shell energy-momentum and generalized Israel conditions, identifying precise continuity requirements on Riemann tensor derivatives for proper matching or shell formation.
\n\n
本文利用分布形式推导了拉格朗日量依赖于曲率标量不变量（包括微分不变量）的任意函数的广义引力理论的连接条件。文中给出了薄壳能量-动量的一般表达式和广义Israel条件，并明确了Riemann张量导数在匹配超曲面上的连续性要求，以区分无壳匹配与壳层形成的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to systematically understand how spacetime matching works in generalized gravity theories beyond General Relativity—particularly those involving higher-order curvature invariants or non-linear functions of curvature scalars—by rigorously applying distributional calculus to derive junction conditions and characterize possible thin-shell or double-layer sources at hypersurfaces.
\n\n
动机在于系统理解广义相对论之外的广义引力理论（尤其是涉及高阶曲率不变量或曲率标量非线性函数的理论）中时空匹配的机制，通过严格应用分布形式推导连接条件，并刻画超曲面上可能出现的薄壳或双层引力源。

Method: The authors employ the distributional formalism to handle discontinuities across a timelike or null hypersurface in spacetimes governed by gravitational actions that are arbitrary functions of curvature scalar invariants (e.g., $R$, $R_{\\mu\\nu}R^{\\mu\\nu}$, $R_{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}R^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}$, and their covariant derivatives up to order $m$). They compute the field equations in the sense of distributions, isolate singular contributions supported on the hypersurface, and identify the shell energy-momentum tensor. The generalized Israel conditions are derived by matching the jump in geometric quantities to this surface source.
\n\n
作者采用分布形式处理由曲率标量不变量（例如 $R$、$R_{\\mu\\nu}R^{\\mu\\nu}$、$R_{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}R^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}$ 及其直至 $m$ 阶协变导数）的任意函数所支配的引力作用量下，类时或类光超曲面上的不连续性。他们在分布意义下计算场方程，分离出支撑在超曲面上的奇异贡献，并识别出壳层能量-动量张量。通过将几何量的跃变与该表面源相匹配，推导出广义Israel条件。

Result: Key results include: (i) Thin shells arise if the $m$th covariant derivative of the Riemann tensor is continuous across the matching hypersurface, where $m$ is the highest derivative order in the Lagrangian; (ii) Proper matching without shells requires continuity of the $(m+1)$th derivative; (iii) Theories with $m=0$ but quadratic in curvature invariants permit discontinuities in the Riemann tensor itself, leading to both thin shells and gravitational double layers; (iv) General Relativity and $F(R)$ theories are exceptional in allowing shells of curvature (impulsive gravitational waves) because they do not require continuity of the second fundamental form, unlike other higher-derivative theories.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(i) 若拉格朗日量中最高导数阶数为 $m$，当Riemann张量的 $m$ 阶协变导数在匹配超曲面上连续时，会出现薄壳；(ii) 无壳的适当匹配还需 $(m+1)$ 阶导数连续；(iii) 对于 $m=0$ 但拉格朗日量为曲率不变量二次型的理论，允许Riemann张量本身不连续，从而产生薄壳和引力双层；(iv) 广义相对论和 $F(R)$ 理论是特殊的，因为它们允许曲率壳（即脉冲引力波），而其他高阶导数理论则要求第二基本形式无跃变。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a comprehensive framework for junction conditions in general metric theories of gravity with arbitrary curvature-dependent Lagrangians. It reveals that the presence or absence of thin shells and double layers is dictated by the differentiability order of the action and the specific structure of curvature couplings, highlighting the unique status of General Relativity and $F(R)$ gravity in permitting curvature shells without requiring continuity of extrinsic geometry.
\n\n
本文为任意曲率依赖拉格朗日量的广义度规引力理论建立了完整的连接条件框架。研究表明，薄壳与双层的存在与否由作用量的可微阶数及曲率耦合的具体结构决定，凸显了广义相对论和 $F(R)$ 引力在无需外禀几何连续性条件下仍允许曲率壳的独特地位。

Abstract: The junction conditions for general theories of gravity based on actions that depend on arbitrary functions of the curvature scalar invariants (including differential invariants) are obtained using the distributional formalism. In case of the existence of thin shells, a general expression for the shell energy-momentum is presented. The generalized Israel conditions are also obtained. The conditions for a proper matching, without shells, are also derived. The main results are: (i) shells arise if the $m$th-covariant derivative of the Riemann tensor is continuous at the matching hypersurface, where $m$ is the maximum order appearing in the Lagrangian density; (ii) a proper junction without thin shells requires further that the $(m+1)$-th derivative be also continuous, (iii) theories with $m=0$ that are quadratic in the scalar curvature invariants are special and unique for they allow for discontinuities of the Riemann tensor resulting in the existence of {\em thin shells and gravitational double layers} and (iv) General Relativity and $F(R)$ theories are extraordinary theories that admit shells of curvature (i.e. impulsive gravitational waves) because other theories require the absence of jumps of the second fundamental form across the matching hypersurface. All results are derived for a minimal coupling with the matter, but the strategy would be analogous for more general couplings.

</details>


### [59] [Going into a tailspin near the abyss: analytic solutions for spinning particles on near equatorial, plunging orbits in Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04682)
*Gabriel Andres Piovano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper provides the first analytic solutions for nearly equatorial, plunging trajectories of a spinning test-particle in Kerr spacetime at linear order in the particle's spin. It includes spin-induced orbital plane precession, gives a closed-form correction to the innermost bound circular orbit (IBCO) radius, and proposes a Keplerian-like parametrization for generic plunging orbits.
\n\n
本文首次提供了Kerr时空中近赤道、径向坠入（plunging）的自旋测试粒子轨迹的解析解，结果在粒子自旋的一阶微扰下成立。解中包含了由粒子自旋进动引起的轨道平面微小进动，给出了最内束缚圆轨道（IBCO）半径的闭式修正，并提出了一种适用于一般径向坠入轨道的类开普勒参数化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Modeling extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) and their transition to the plunging phase requires accurate analytic descriptions of spinning test-particle motion in strong-field Kerr geometry. Existing treatments often neglect spin-induced orbital plane precession or are restricted to circular or equatorial orbits. This work aims to fill this gap by solving the Mathisson–Papapetrou–Dixon (MPD) equations for generic plunging orbits with $E < 1$ at first order in the small-body spin.
\n\n
对极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）及其向径向坠入阶段过渡的建模，需要在强场Kerr几何中对自旋测试粒子运动进行精确的解析描述。现有处理通常忽略自旋引起的轨道平面进动，或仅限于圆轨道或赤道轨道。本文旨在通过在小质量体自旋的一阶微扰下求解Mathisson–Papapetrou–Dixon（MPD）方程，针对能量 $E < 1$ 的一般径向坠入轨道填补这一空白。

Method: The authors solve the MPD equations in the pole-dipole approximation using a perturbative expansion in the dimensionless spin parameter $S \ll 1$. They adopt a tetrad formalism adapted to the background geodesic motion and integrate the equations of motion for nearly equatorial plunging orbits. The spin-induced precession of the orbital plane is incorporated via a small inclination angle that evolves adiabatically. A novel parametrization inspired by Keplerian orbital elements is introduced to describe the radial and angular motion during the plunge.
\n\n
作者在极-偶极近似下，使用对无量纲自旋参数 $S \ll 1$ 的微扰展开来求解MPD方程。他们采用与背景测地线运动相适应的标架（tetrad）形式，并对近赤道径向坠入轨道积分运动方程。通过一个绝热演化的微小倾角，将自旋引起的轨道平面进动纳入考虑。文中引入了一种受开普勒轨道根数启发的新参数化方法，用于描述径向坠入过程中的径向和角向运动。

Result: The paper derives explicit analytic expressions for the radial and angular coordinates as functions of proper time, including first-order spin corrections. It computes the shift in the innermost bound circular orbit (IBCO) radius due to spin, yielding a closed-form result: $\delta r_{\\text{IBCO}} \\propto S$. Furthermore, it constructs a Keplerian-like parametrization using a pseudo-eccentric anomaly to uniformly describe plunging orbits from the IBCO to the horizon.
\n\n
本文推导了径向和角向坐标关于固有时的显式解析表达式，包含一阶自旋修正。计算了自旋导致的最内束缚圆轨道（IBCO）半径偏移，得到了闭式结果：$\delta r_{\\text{IBCO}} \\propto S$。此外，通过引入伪偏心近点角（pseudo-eccentric anomaly），构建了一种类开普勒参数化方法，可统一描述从IBCO到视界之间的径向坠入轨道。

Conclusion: These analytic solutions enhance the theoretical toolkit for modeling the late inspiral and plunge phases of EMRIs with spinning secondaries. The inclusion of spin-induced orbital precession and the new parametrization facilitate more accurate waveform generation within self-force and black hole perturbation theory frameworks, particularly for data analysis with future space-based gravitational-wave detectors like LISA.
\n\n
这些解析解增强了对携带自旋次级天体的EMRI系统在旋进末期和径向坠入阶段建模的理论工具箱。自旋诱导轨道进动的纳入以及新参数化方法有助于在自力（self-force）和黑洞微扰理论框架下生成更精确的波形，尤其有利于未来空间引力波探测器（如LISA）的数据分析。

Abstract: This work presents, the first time, analytic solutions for the nearly equatorial, plunging motion of a spinning test-particle in Kerr spacetime. The equations of motion are solved at first-order in the small-body spin for all classes of plunging orbits with energy $E < 1$. The solutions incorporate the small precession of the orbital plane caused by the precession of the particle's spin. Additionally, we present the correction to the radius of the innermost bound circular orbit in closed form, and introduce a novel, Keplerian-like parametrization for generic plunging orbits. Our solutions will be useful in the modelling of inspiral-merger-ringdown waveforms with self-force methods and black hole perturbation theory.

</details>


### [60] [Inflation in fractional Newtonian cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04712)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores early universe cosmology using fractional Newtonian gravity, showing that a non-singular pre-inflationary phase naturally transitions into inflation, which acts as a stable attractor. The model links the fractional parameter $α$ to the number of $e$-folds, resolves the horizon problem, and provides a graceful exit to a standard radiation-dominated era.
\n\n
本文在分数阶牛顿宇宙学框架下研究早期宇宙演化，表明非奇异的暴胀前阶段可自然过渡到暴胀阶段（后者为稳定吸引子）。该模型将分数阶参数 $α$ 与 $e$ 折叠数关联起来，解决了视界问题，并实现了向标准辐射主导时期的优雅退出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard inflationary cosmology typically assumes an initial singularity or requires fine-tuned initial conditions. The authors aim to address these issues by employing fractional Newtonian cosmology—a framework incorporating non-local temporal dynamics via fractional derivatives—to construct a non-singular pre-inflationary phase that naturally leads into inflation without ad hoc assumptions.
\n\n
标准暴胀宇宙学通常假设初始奇点或需要精细调节的初值条件。作者旨在通过采用分数阶牛顿宇宙学（一种通过分数阶导数引入非局域时间动力学的框架）来解决这些问题，构建一个无需人为假设、自然导向暴胀的非奇异暴胀前阶段。

Method: The authors construct a fractional gravitational potential within fractional Newtonian cosmology, leading to modified Friedmann-like equations. They analyze the dynamical system near the transition between the pre-inflationary and inflationary regimes by examining the balance and sign change of the effective fractional force. Stability is assessed via attractor behavior, and the relation between the zero of the fractional force and the end of inflation is computed perturbatively to connect $α$ with observable quantities like the number of $e$-folds $N_e$.
\n\n
作者在分数阶牛顿宇宙学中构建了一个分数阶引力势，导出了修正的类Friedmann方程。他们通过分析有效分数阶力的平衡与符号变化，研究暴胀前与暴胀阶段之间过渡点附近的动力学系统。通过吸引子行为评估稳定性，并微扰计算分数阶力零点与暴胀终点之间的微小间距，从而将 $α$ 与可观测量（如 $e$ 折叠数 $N_e$）联系起来。

Result: The model exhibits a stable inflationary attractor emerging from a non-singular pre-inflationary phase. The fractional force vanishes just after inflation ends, with the separation between this zero point and the end of inflation yielding a precise relation: $N_e \approx \\frac{1}{1 - α}$ (for $α \\lesssim 1$). This ensures sufficient inflation to solve the horizon problem while predicting a graceful exit into an exact radiation-dominated solution with standard $a(t) \\propto t^{1/2}$ scaling but $α$-dependent amplitude.
\n\n
该模型展现出一个从非奇异暴胀前阶段出现的稳定暴胀吸引子。分数阶力在暴胀结束后立即消失，其零点与暴胀终点之间的间距给出了精确关系：$N_e \\approx \\frac{1}{1 - α}$（当 $α \\lesssim 1$ 时）。这保证了足以解决视界问题的暴胀量，同时预言了向精确辐射主导解的优雅退出，具有标准的 $a(t) \\propto t^{1/2}$ 标度律，但振幅依赖于 $α$。

Conclusion: Fractional Newtonian cosmology provides a self-consistent, non-singular origin for inflation without fine-tuning, naturally incorporates a graceful exit, and links the fractional order $α$ to observable cosmological parameters. This suggests that non-local temporal modifications at early times can replace ad hoc inflaton potentials while preserving standard late-time cosmology.
\n\n
分数阶牛顿宇宙学在无需精细调节的情况下提供了自洽且非奇异的暴胀起源，自然包含优雅退出机制，并将分数阶参数 $α$ 与可观测宇宙学参数联系起来。这表明早期时间的非局域时间修正可以替代人为的暴胀子势，同时保持晚期宇宙学的标准行为。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the evolution of the early universe within the framework of fractional Newtonian cosmology. By constructing a suitable fractional potential, we show that the cosmological evolution can naturally originate from a non-singular pre-inflationary regime. We find a natural transition time, separating the pre-inflationary and inflationary regimes, characterized by the balance of the corresponding forces. By analyzing the dynamics near the transition time, we show that the inflationary phase emerges as a stable dynamical attractor. We show that the fractional force vanishes and undergoes a sign change at a point very close to the end of inflation. We then determine the small separation between the force zero point and the end of inflation, and show that it leads to a meaningful relation between the number of $e$-folds and the fractional parameter $α$, ensuring consistency with observations and resolving the horizon problem. Moreover, our results demonstrate the existence of a graceful exit from inflation, followed by an exact radiation-dominated solution with the standard time dependence and an $α$-dependent normalization.

</details>


### [61] [Search for continuous gravitational waves from neutron stars in five globular clusters in the first part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04792)
*Damon H. T. Cheung,Keith Riles,Rafel Amengual,Preet Baxi,Alicia Calafat,Anamaria Effler,Tabata Aira Ferreira,Evan Goetz,Tom Kimpson,David Keitel,Alan M. Knee,Joan-Rene Merou,Quynh Lan Nguyen,Joseph O'Leary,Ornella J. Piccinni,Alicia M. Sintes,Karl Wette*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reports on the most sensitive directed searches to date for continuous gravitational waves from unknown neutron stars in five Milky Way globular clusters using LIGO data from the first eight months of the O4 observing run. No detection was made in the 20–475 Hz band for sources older than 300 years, with the strongest upper limit reaching $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for NGC 6397.
\n\n
本文报告了利用LIGO在第四次观测运行（O4）前八个月的数据，对银河系五个球状星团中未知中子星的连续引力波进行的迄今最灵敏的定向搜寻。在20–475 Hz频段内、假设源年龄大于300年的情况下未发现引力波信号，其中对NGC 6397在282 Hz附近获得的最强95%置信度上限约为$\\sim 4.2 \\times 10^{-26}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to detect or constrain continuous gravitational wave emission from rapidly spinning, non-axisymmetric neutron stars in dense stellar environments like globular clusters, which are promising sites for such sources due to frequent dynamical interactions that may produce isolated or binary neutron stars with high spin frequencies.
\n\n
动机在于探测或限制来自球状星团等致密恒星环境中快速旋转且非轴对称中子星的连续引力波辐射。这类环境因频繁的动力学相互作用可能产生孤立或双星中子星，具有较高的自转频率，是连续引力波源的理想候选区域。

Method: The authors employ the WEAVE semi-coherent search pipeline on LIGO data from the first eight months of the O4 run. This method coherently computes matched-filter detection statistics over short time segments and then incoherently sums them across the full observation period to enhance sensitivity to long-duration continuous wave signals while managing computational cost.
\n\n
作者在LIGO第四次观测运行（O4）前八个月的数据上应用WEAVE半相干搜寻流程。该方法在短时间段内相干地计算匹配滤波检测统计量，然后在整个观测期内非相干地叠加这些统计量，在控制计算成本的同时提升对长持续时间连续波信号的灵敏度。

Result: No statistically significant gravitational wave signal was detected in the 20–475 Hz frequency band under the assumption of source ages exceeding 300 years. Simulated signal injections demonstrate that the search achieves the most stringent upper limits to date over much of the parameter space, with a median 95% confidence upper limit as low as $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for the cluster NGC 6397.
\n\n
在假设源年龄超过300年的前提下，20–475 Hz频段内未探测到具有统计显著性的引力波信号。通过注入模拟信号验证，该搜寻在大部分参数空间中获得了迄今为止最严格的上限，其中对星团NGC 6397在282 Hz附近达到的中位95%置信度上限低至$\\sim 4.2 \\times 10^{-26}$。

Conclusion: The non-detection sets new observational constraints on the ellipticity and spin-down properties of potential neutron stars in globular clusters. The results represent a significant improvement in sensitivity compared to previous searches and demonstrate the effectiveness of the WEAVE semi-coherent method for future continuous gravitational wave analyses.
\n\n
未探测到信号为球状星团中潜在中子星的椭率（ellipticity）和自转减慢（spin-down）特性设定了新的观测限制。与以往搜寻相比，本结果在灵敏度上取得显著提升，并验证了WEAVE半相干方法在未来连续引力波分析中的有效性。

Abstract: We present the results of directed searches for continuous gravitational waves from unknown neutron stars in five Milky Way globular clusters. We carry out the searches in the LIGO data from the first eight months of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run using the WEAVE semi-coherent program, which sums matched-filter detection-statistic values over many time segments spanning the observation period. No gravitational wave signal is detected in the search band of 20-475 Hz for assumed source ages greater than 300 years. Injections of simulated continuous wave signals in the data indicate that we achieve the most sensitive results to date across most of the explored parameter space volume, obtaining median 95% confidence level upper limits as low as $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for NGC 6397.

</details>


### [62] [Dyonic hairy black holes in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor theories: Cubic and quartic interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04884)
*Masaki Kitagawa,Naoki Tsukamoto,Ryotaro Kase*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper constructs and classifies static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat hairy black holes in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories with both electric and magnetic charges. It extends beyond quadratic interactions to include cubic and quartic terms, derives a consistency condition to maintain second-order field equations, and identifies magnetic-charge-induced solution branches that vanish when $P \to 0$. Scalar hair is categorized as primary or secondary based on symmetry, and distinct asymptotic behaviors are found for different couplings.
\n\n
本文构建并分类了具有电荷和磁荷的 $U(1)$ 规范不变标量-矢量-张量（SVT）理论中静态、球对称、渐近平坦的带毛黑洞解。研究超越了二次相互作用，系统纳入了立方和四次项，推导出保持场方程为二阶的一致性条件，并识别出在磁单极极限 $P \to 0$ 下消失的、由磁荷诱导的解分支。标量毛发根据对称性分为 primary 和 secondary 两类，并发现不同耦合下其渐近衰减速率存在差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous studies of hairy black holes in scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories focused primarily on the quadratic sector and purely electric configurations, leaving open the role of higher-order interactions and magnetic charges. The motivation is to explore how magnetic monopoles activate new interaction channels (e.g., the cubic coupling $\tilde{f}_3$), whether consistent second-order theories can be built with such terms, and how scalar hair depends on the presence of magnetic charge—potentially leading to new observational signatures.
\n\n
先前对标量-矢量-张量（SVT）理论中带毛黑洞的研究主要集中于二次项和纯电荷构型，尚未充分探讨高阶相互作用和磁荷的作用。本文旨在探究磁单极如何激活新的相互作用通道（如立方耦合 $\tilde{f}_3$），能否在包含这些项的情况下构建自洽的二阶理论，以及标量毛发如何依赖于磁荷的存在——这可能带来新的观测特征。

Method: The authors extend $U(1)$ gauge-invariant SVT theories to include cubic and quartic derivative interactions in the presence of a magnetic charge $P$. They impose staticity, spherical symmetry, and asymptotic flatness, and analyze the resulting field equations. A key step is deriving a consistency condition for the quartic coupling to cancel dangerous higher-derivative terms induced by $P$, preserving second-order dynamics. Solutions are classified by symmetry: shift-symmetric couplings yield secondary hair via Noether current conservation, while explicit $φ$-dependence leads to primary hair. Analytic near-horizon and asymptotic expansions are matched with numerical integration to verify global regularity.
\n\n
作者将 $U(1)$ 规范不变的 SVT 理论扩展至包含磁荷 $P$ 下的立方和四次导数相互作用。他们施加静态性、球对称性和渐近平坦性，并分析所得场方程。关键步骤是为四次耦合推导一致性条件，以抵消由 $P$ 引入的危险高阶导数项，从而保持动力学为二阶。解根据对称性分类：平移对称耦合通过 Noether current 守恒产生 secondary 毛发，而显式的 $φ$ 依赖则导致 primary 毛发。通过匹配视界附近和渐近区域的解析展开与数值积分，验证了解的整体正则性。

Result: The analysis yields new families of hairy black hole solutions that exist only when magnetic charge $P \neq 0$, including branches where the cubic coupling $\tilde{f}_3$ becomes active—a term absent in purely electric cases. The scalar hair is shown to decay asymptotically at rates dependent on the interaction type (e.g., faster or slower than $1/r$). The consistency condition for the quartic sector successfully removes Ostrogradsky instabilities. All constructed solutions are globally regular, confirmed by matching analytic and numerical results.
\n\n
分析得到了仅在磁荷 $P \neq 0$ 时存在的新一族带毛黑洞解，包括立方耦合 $\tilde{f}_3$ 被激活的分支——该耦合在纯电构型中不出现。标量毛发的渐近衰减速率依赖于相互作用类型（例如快于或慢于 $1/r$）。四次项的一致性条件成功消除了 Ostrogradsky 不稳定性。所有构造的解均被证实是整体正则的，这通过解析与数值结果的匹配得以确认。

Conclusion: Magnetic charge fundamentally enriches the structure of hairy black holes in SVT theories by enabling otherwise inert interaction terms and generating novel solution branches that vanish in the $P \to 0$ limit. The distinction between primary and secondary hair persists in the presence of magnetic fields, and the asymptotic behavior of the scalar field offers potential observational discriminants. The work establishes a consistent framework for higher-order $U(1)$-invariant SVT theories with dyonic black holes.
\n\n
磁荷从根本上丰富了 SVT 理论中带毛黑洞的结构，通过激活原本惰性的相互作用项并生成在 $P \to 0$ 极限下消失的新解分支。即使在存在磁场的情况下，primary 与 secondary 毛发的区分依然成立，且标量场的渐近行为提供了潜在的观测判据。本工作为包含双荷黑洞的高阶 $U(1)$ 不变 SVT 理论建立了自洽框架。

Abstract: We construct and classify asymptotically flat, static, spherically symmetric hairy black hole solutions in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories carrying both electric and magnetic charges. Extending previous studies beyond the quadratic sector, we systematically incorporate cubic and quartic interaction terms in the presence of the magnetic charge. We derive a consistency condition for the quartic interaction that eliminates higher-order derivative terms induced by the magnetic charge, ensuring the theory remains second-order. We classify the obtained solutions based on their symmetry properties: shift-symmetric couplings yield secondary hair governed by the Noether current, whereas $φ$-dependent interactions generate primary hair. Crucially, our analysis reveals that the magnetic charge plays a key role in activating specific interaction sectors such as the cubic coupling $\tilde{f}_3$, which does not appear in the field equations in purely electric configurations. We identify solution branches that are intrinsic to the magnetic charge, as they cease to exist in the vanishing monopole limit ($P\to 0$). Furthermore, we demonstrate that the scalar hair exhibits distinct asymptotic decay rates depending on the interaction type, suggesting possible variations in observational signatures. Finally, we verify the global regularity of these solutions by connecting analytic expansions with numerical integration.

</details>


### [63] [A loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi dust model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04995)
*Luca Cafaro,Farshid Soltani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi (LTB) model for spherically symmetric gravitational collapse of pressureless dust. By modeling the system as non-interacting shells, each governed by single-shell loop quantum dynamics, the authors demonstrate that quantum evolution is non-singular: collapsing wave packets bounce at Planckian densities and transition to expansion, thereby resolving the classical central singularity. The study also compares loop quantum gravity (LQG) with Wheeler-DeWitt quantization and finds that interference effects near the bounce reduce the accuracy of the LQG effective theory in the central region.
\n\n
本文提出了一种对边际束缚的Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi（LTB）模型的圈量子化，该模型描述了无压尘埃在球对称下的引力坍缩。通过将系统建模为非相互作用的壳层，每个壳层由单独的单壳层圈量子动力学支配，作者证明了量子演化是非奇异的：坍缩的波包在Planckian能量密度处发生反弹，并随后过渡到膨胀的经典轨迹，从而解决了经典中心曲率奇点。研究还比较了圈量子引力（LQG）与Wheeler-DeWitt量子化方法，并发现反弹附近的干涉效应降低了LQG有效理论在尘埃云中心区域的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classical LTB model predicts a curvature singularity at the center during gravitational collapse of pressureless dust, signaling a breakdown of general relativity. Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG) offers a framework to resolve such singularities via quantum geometry effects. The motivation is to construct a full quantum description of the LTB collapse using LQG techniques, investigate whether the singularity is resolved, and assess the reliability of the commonly used effective dynamics in capturing the full quantum behavior—particularly in inhomogeneous settings where quantum interference may play a crucial role.
\n\n
经典的LTB模型在无压尘埃引力坍缩过程中预言了中心曲率奇点，表明广义相对论在此失效。圈量子引力（LQG）通过量子几何效应提供了一种解决此类奇点的框架。本文的动机是利用LQG技术构建LTB坍缩的完整量子描述，探究奇点是否被消除，并评估常用的有效动力学在捕捉完整量子行为方面的可靠性——尤其是在非均匀背景下，量子干涉可能起关键作用。

Method: The authors decompose the marginally bound LTB spacetime into a continuum of non-interacting spherical shells, each treated as an independent minisuperspace system. They apply loop quantization to each shell using holonomy corrections derived from LQG, leading to a quantum difference equation for the wave function of each shell. The full quantum state is a product of individual shell wave functions. Numerical simulations of single-shell dynamics are performed to track the evolution of Gaussian wave packets through collapse and bounce. The results are compared with both classical trajectories and the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization, and deviations from the loop quantum effective dynamics are analyzed, particularly focusing on interference patterns emerging near the bounce.
\n\n
作者将边际束缚的LTB时空分解为连续的非相互作用球壳，每个壳层被视为独立的minisuperspace系统。他们对每个壳层应用圈量子化，使用来自LQG的holonomy修正，导出每个壳层波函数的量子差分方程。完整的量子态是各壳层波函数的乘积。通过数值模拟单壳层动力学，追踪高斯波包在坍缩与反弹过程中的演化。结果与经典轨迹及Wheeler-DeWitt量子化进行比较，并分析与圈量子有效动力学的偏差，特别关注反弹附近出现的干涉图样。

Result: The single-shell loop quantum dynamics is non-singular: wave packets initially collapsing toward high density undergo a quantum bounce at energy densities near the Planck scale ($\\rho \\sim \\rho_{\\text{Pl}}$) and then evolve along an expanding classical trajectory. This resolves the classical central singularity of the LTB model. However, during the bounce, generic wave packets develop quantum interference patterns due to the discrete nature of the quantum geometry. These interference effects are not captured by the loop quantum effective theory, which assumes a smooth semiclassical trajectory, leading to significant deviations between the effective dynamics and the full quantum evolution near the center of the dust cloud.
\n\n
单壳层圈量子动力学是非奇异的：初始坍缩的波包在接近Planck尺度的能量密度（$\\rho \\sim \\rho_{\\text{Pl}}$）处发生量子反弹，随后沿膨胀的经典轨迹演化，从而解决了LTB模型的经典中心奇点。然而，在反弹过程中，由于量子几何的离散性，典型的波包会产生量子干涉图样。这些干涉效应无法被圈量子有效理论所捕捉——该理论假设平滑的半经典轨迹——导致在尘埃云中心附近，有效动力学与完整量子演化之间出现显著偏差。

Conclusion: Loop quantum gravity successfully resolves the central singularity in the LTB collapse model through a quantum bounce driven by discrete quantum geometry. However, the standard loop quantum effective dynamics fails to accurately describe the full quantum evolution in regions where strong interference occurs, particularly near the symmetry center. This highlights the limitations of effective descriptions in inhomogeneous quantum gravity scenarios and underscores the necessity of full quantum treatments when quantum coherence effects are significant.
\n\n
圈量子引力通过由离散量子几何驱动的量子反弹，成功解决了LTB坍缩模型中的中心奇点。然而，标准的圈量子有效动力学在强干涉发生的区域（特别是在对称中心附近）无法准确描述完整的量子演化。这揭示了在非均匀量子引力场景中有效描述的局限性，并强调了当量子相干效应显著时，必须采用完整的量子处理方法。

Abstract: We present a loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi (LTB) model, describing the gravitational collapse of pressureless dust in spherical symmetry. The full quantum LTB model is constructed as a collection of non-interacting shells, each governed by an individual single-shell loop quantum dynamics. We show that the single-shell evolution is non-singular and that wave packets initially peaked on a collapsing trajectory undergo a bounce at Planckian energy densities and subsequently follow an expanding classical trajectory, resolving the classical central curvature singularity. We also compare the loop quantum theory with the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization of the same model and assess the accuracy of the loop quantum gravity effective theory in reproducing the full quantum dynamics. Specifically, we find that initially collapsing wave packets generically develop an interference pattern at the bounce, which suppresses the accuracy of the effective theory near the center of the dust cloud.

</details>


### [64] [Observational and Thermodynamic aspects of one-dimensional Dark Energy EoS parametrization models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05009)
*Anirban Chatterjee,Yungui Gong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the Gong-Zhang (GZ) dark energy equation-of-state parametrizations—GZ-Type I and GZ-Type II—using only late-time cosmological data (SNe Ia, BAO, and $H(z)$). It finds that both models are viable alternatives to $\\Lambda$CDM, with GZ-Type II preferred due to lower parameter degeneracy and stronger Bayesian evidence. Additionally, configuration entropy is introduced as a thermodynamic probe of structure formation, showing sensitivity to dynamical dark energy effects on late-time clustering while preserving standard early-universe behavior.
\n\n
本文研究了Gong-Zhang（GZ）暗能量状态方程参数化模型——GZ-Type I 和 GZ-Type II，仅使用晚期宇宙学数据（Ia型超新星、BAO和$H(z)$）。结果表明，两种模型均为$\\Lambda$CDM的可行替代方案，其中GZ-Type II因更低的参数简并性和更强的贝叶斯证据而被优先支持。此外，引入构型熵（configuration entropy）作为结构形成的热力学探针，其对动力学暗能量在晚期成团效应具有敏感性，同时保持标准早期宇宙行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to test physically motivated, yet observationally flexible, alternatives to the standard $\\Lambda$CDM model, especially in light of persistent tensions (e.g., $H_0$) and the theoretical fine-tuning problems of a cosmological constant. The Gong-Zhang parametrizations offer a theoretically grounded framework for dynamical dark energy, and the authors aim to assess their viability using only late-time probes to avoid assumptions about early-universe physics. Furthermore, they seek to extend the analysis beyond background expansion by introducing a thermodynamically inspired diagnostic—configuration entropy—to probe structure formation.
\n\n
动机源于对标准$\\Lambda$CDM模型之外既具物理动机又具观测灵活性的替代理论的需求，尤其是在$H_0$等张力持续存在以及宇宙学常数面临理论微调问题的背景下。Gong-Zhang参数化为动力学暗能量提供了一个理论基础扎实的框架，作者旨在仅使用晚期宇宙学探针评估其可行性，以避免对早期宇宙物理的假设。此外，他们希望超越背景膨胀分析，引入一个热力学启发的诊断工具——构型熵（configuration entropy）——来探测结构形成。

Method: The authors constrain the GZ-Type I and GZ-Type II dark energy models using a suite of late-time cosmological observations: Type Ia supernovae datasets (Union3, Pantheon+SH0ES, DES-SN5YR), DESI baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) measurements, and cosmic chronometer $H(z)$ data. They perform Bayesian inference to obtain posterior distributions and apply information criteria (e.g., Jeffreys scale) to compare model performance against $\\Lambda$CDM. To go beyond background cosmology, they compute the configuration entropy—a measure derived from the phase-space distribution of matter—and analyze its production rate as a function of redshift to assess the impact of dynamical dark energy on gravitational clustering.
\n\n
作者利用一系列晚期宇宙学观测数据约束GZ-Type I和GZ-Type II暗能量模型：Ia型超新星数据集（Union3、Pantheon+SH0ES、DES-SN5YR）、DESI重子声学振荡（BAO）测量以及宇宙计时器$H(z)$数据。他们采用贝叶斯推断获得后验分布，并应用信息准则（如Jeffreys尺度）将模型与$\\Lambda$CDM进行比较。为超越背景宇宙学，他们计算构型熵（由物质相空间分布导出的量），并分析其产生率随红移的变化，以评估动力学暗能量对引力成团的影响。

Result: Both GZ parametrizations are statistically competitive with $\\Lambda$CDM across all datasets, but GZ-Type II consistently shows stronger Bayesian evidence (per Jeffreys scale) and reduced parameter degeneracies. The configuration entropy analysis reveals that its production rate is sensitive to the dynamics of dark energy at late times: deviations from $\\Lambda$CDM alter the entropy evolution, thereby affecting structure formation, while early-time behavior remains consistent with standard cosmology. This demonstrates that configuration entropy serves as a complementary probe of late-time cosmic acceleration.
\n\n
两种GZ参数化模型在所有数据集中均与$\\Lambda$CDM具有统计竞争力，但GZ-Type II始终表现出更强的贝叶斯证据（依据Jeffreys尺度）和更低的参数简并性。构型熵分析表明，其产生率对晚期暗能量动力学敏感：偏离$\\Lambda$CDM会改变熵的演化，从而影响结构形成，而早期行为仍与标准宇宙学一致。这证明构型熵可作为晚期宇宙加速的互补探针。

Conclusion: The Gong-Zhang dark energy framework—particularly GZ-Type II—is a physically transparent and observationally viable extension of $\\Lambda$CDM when tested solely with late-time data. The use of configuration entropy provides a novel, thermodynamically grounded method to probe how dynamical dark energy influences late-time structure formation without altering early-universe predictions. This dual approach (background + entropy diagnostics) strengthens the case for GZ-type models as compelling alternatives to a cosmological constant.
\n\n
Gong-Zhang暗能量框架（尤其是GZ-Type II）在仅使用晚期数据检验时，是$\\Lambda$CDM的一个物理透明且观测可行的扩展。构型熵的使用提供了一种新颖且基于热力学的方法，用于探测动力学暗能量如何影响晚期结构形成，同时不改变早期宇宙预言。这种“背景+熵诊断”的双重方法强化了GZ类模型作为宇宙学常数替代理论的说服力。

Abstract: We examine the observational viability and physical implications of the Gong-Zhang (GZ) dark--energy equation-of-state parametrizations using exclusively late-time cosmological probes. Two one-dimensional parametrization models, GZ-Type~I and GZ-Type~II, are constrained with Type~Ia supernovae (Union3, Pantheon+SH0ES, and DES-SN5YR), DESI baryon acoustic oscillations, and cosmic chronometer measurements of $H(z)$. Bayesian inference combined with information-criteria diagnostics shows that both parametrizations provide competitive alternatives to $Λ$CDM, while the GZ-Type~II model is consistently favored, exhibiting reduced parameter degeneracy and stronger Jeffreys-scale support. Beyond background expansion tests, we employ configuration entropy as a thermodynamically motivated probe of structure formation. We demonstrate that the entropy-production rate sensitively traces the impact of dynamical dark energy on late-time gravitational clustering while preserving standard early-time behavior. Our results establish the Gong-Zhang framework as a physically transparent and observationally consistent extension of $Λ$CDM, with configuration entropy providing a complementary diagnostic of late-time cosmic acceleration.

</details>


### [65] [Strong breaking of black-hole uniqueness from coexisting scalarization mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05064)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Pedro G. S. Fernandes,Lidia Marino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates a strong violation of black-hole uniqueness in a scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity theory, where multiple distinct black-hole branches coexist due to competing scalarization mechanisms—curvature-induced and spin-induced—at large spins, leading to a complex phase diagram with both continuous and discontinuous transitions.
\n\n
本文展示了在标量-高斯-博内引力理论中黑洞唯一性的强烈破缺：在大自旋下，曲率诱导和自旋诱导的标量化机制相互竞争，导致多个不同的黑洞分支共存，并形成包含连续与不连续相变的复杂相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Black-hole uniqueness theorems in General Relativity assert that stationary vacuum black holes are uniquely described by the Kerr metric. However, in modified gravity theories, this uniqueness may fail. The authors aim to identify a concrete theory where this breaking is not merely perturbative but leads to multiple coexisting non-Kerr black-hole solutions, thereby exhibiting a "strong" violation of uniqueness.
\n\n
广义相对论中的黑洞唯一性定理断言，稳态真空黑洞由Kerr度规唯一描述。然而，在修改引力理论中，这种唯一性可能失效。作者旨在寻找一个具体理论，其中这种破缺不仅是微扰性的，还会导致多个非Kerr黑洞解共存，从而表现出“强”唯一性破缺。

Method: The authors consider a scalar-tensor theory with a cubic coupling between a scalar field $\\phi$ and the Gauss-Bonnet invariant $\\mathcal{G}$, i.e., an interaction term $\\sim \\phi^3 \\mathcal{G}$. They analyze the non-linear instability of the Kerr solution under this coupling, which triggers spontaneous scalarization. By solving the full non-linear field equations at high spin, they map out the phase structure of black-hole solutions, identifying regions where curvature-induced and spin-induced scalarization mechanisms dominate or compete.
\n\n
作者考虑一个标量-张量理论，其中标量场 $\\phi$ 与高斯-博内不变量 $\\mathcal{G}$ 之间存在立方耦合，即相互作用项 $\\sim \\phi^3 \\mathcal{G}$。他们分析了在此耦合下Kerr解的非线性不稳定性，该不稳定性触发自发标量化。通过在高自旋下求解完整的非线性场方程，他们绘制出黑洞解的相结构，识别出曲率诱导与自旋诱导标量化机制主导或竞争的区域。

Result: The study reveals a rich phase diagram of black-hole solutions in the scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory with cubic coupling. At large dimensionless spin $a/M$, two distinct scalarization mechanisms—curvature-induced (favored at high curvature) and spin-induced (favored at high rotation)—compete when the coupling constant has a fixed sign. This competition yields multiple coexisting branches of black-hole solutions, connected via both continuous (second-order) and discontinuous (first-order) phase transitions.
\n\n
研究表明，在具有立方耦合的标量-高斯-博内理论中，黑洞解呈现出丰富的相图。在大无量纲自旋 $a/M$ 下，当耦合常数符号固定时，两种不同的标量化机制——曲率诱导（高曲率有利）和自旋诱导（高旋转有利）——相互竞争。这种竞争导致多个黑洞解分支共存，并通过连续（二级）和不连续（一级）相变相互连接。

Conclusion: The paper provides a concrete example of strong black-hole uniqueness violation in a well-motivated extension of General Relativity. The coexistence of multiple black-hole branches due to competing scalarization channels implies that observational signatures (e.g., in gravitational waves) could be highly non-unique, challenging the standard Kerr paradigm and offering new phenomenological avenues for testing gravity.
\n\n
本文为广义相对论的一个有动机的扩展中黑洞唯一性的强烈破缺提供了具体范例。由于竞争性标量化通道导致多个黑洞分支共存，这意味着观测信号（如引力波）可能高度非唯一，从而挑战标准的Kerr范式，并为检验引力理论提供新的现象学途径。

Abstract: Black-hole uniqueness, i.e., the statement that all stationary vacuum black holes in the universe are described by the Kerr solution, is expected to break in theories beyond General Relativity. This breaking can take a particularly strong form, if several branches of black-hole solutions beyond the Kerr solution coexist. We find an example of a theory that exhibits such strong breaking. In this theory, a cubic coupling of a scalar field to the Gauss-Bonnet invariant triggers black-hole scalarization through a non-linear instability of the Kerr solution. At large spin, curvature-induced and spin-induced scalarization mechanisms compete at fixed sign of the coupling. This results in a rich phase structure of black-hole solutions and continuous as well as discontinuous transitions between the different branches of black holes.

### [66] [External magnetic field influence on massive binary black hole inspiral gravitational waves and its similarity with environmental effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05084)
*Xulong Yuan,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper computes the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) corrections to gravitational waveforms from extreme mass-ratio inspirals into magnetized black holes (Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson and Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin), showing that magnetic fields induce leading-order corrections at $-2$ PN (KBR) and $-3$ PN (KBM), which are distinguishable from modified gravity but degenerate with certain matter distributions.
\n\n
本文计算了极端质量比旋进（EMRI）进入磁化黑洞（Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson 和 Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin）时引力波形的参数化后爱因斯坦（ppE）修正，表明磁场在 $-2$ PN（KBR）和 $-3$ PN（KBM）阶引入主导修正，这些修正可与修改引力理论区分，但与特定物质分布存在简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to isolate and characterize the imprints of external magnetic fields on gravitational wave (GW) signals from inspiraling compact objects around massive black holes, particularly to differentiate magnetic effects from other environmental or modified-gravity contributions in future GW observations.
\n\n
动机在于分离并刻画外部磁场对围绕大质量黑洞旋进的致密天体所发出引力波（GW）信号的印记，特别是在未来的引力波观测中区分磁场效应与其他环境因素或修改引力理论的贡献。

Method: The authors compute the frequency-domain ppE waveform for a small black hole inspiraling into two types of magnetized massive black holes: Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) and Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin (KBM). They perform a post-Newtonian (PN) expansion of the orbital dynamics under the influence of the external magnetic field and extract the leading and next-to-leading order phase corrections in the GW phasing formalism. Degeneracies with matter environments and modified gravity are assessed by comparing PN orders and functional forms.
\n\n
作者计算了一个小黑洞旋进两类磁化大质量黑洞——Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson（KBR）和Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin（KBM）——时的频域ppE波形。他们对受外部磁场影响的轨道动力学进行后牛顿（PN）展开，并在引力波相位形式中提取主导阶和次主导阶的相位修正。通过比较PN阶数和函数形式，评估其与物质环境及修改引力理论的简并性。

Result: For KBR black holes, the magnetic field induces a leading-order ppE correction at $-2$ PN, while spin contributes at $-1.5$ PN. For KBM black holes, the magnetic correction appears at $-3$ PN, with spin again at $-1.5$ PN. These magnetic corrections are not degenerate with known modified gravity effects but mimic the gravitational influence of surrounding matter with power-law density profiles: $γ=1$ for KBR and $γ=0$ for KBM.
\n\n
对于KBR黑洞，磁场在 $-2$ PN 阶引入主导ppE修正，而自旋贡献出现在 $-1.5$ PN 阶；对于KBM黑洞，磁场修正出现在 $-3$ PN 阶，自旋同样在 $-1.5$ PN 阶。这些磁场修正与已知的修改引力效应不简并，但会模拟周围物质的引力影响，其幂律密度分布指数分别为：KBR对应 $γ=1$，KBM对应 $γ=0$。

Conclusion: Future gravitational wave detectors may detect $-3$ or $-2$ PN order corrections in extreme mass-ratio inspiral signals, but without additional information, such signals cannot uniquely determine whether the origin is an external magnetic field or a specific matter environment; however, they can be distinguished from modifications to general relativity.
\n\n
未来的引力波探测器可能在极端质量比旋进信号中探测到 $-3$ 或 $-2$ PN 阶修正，但在缺乏额外信息的情况下，无法唯一确定其来源是外部磁场还是特定物质环境；然而，这些信号可与广义相对论的修改明确区分。

Abstract: Magnetic fields represent a critical component of astrophysical research, laying the foundation for interpreting high-energy astrophysical activity across galactic scales. In this work, we investigate the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) waveform imprints induced by the external magnetic fields of Bertotti-Robinson and Bonnor-Melvin black holes, with the aim of distinguishing such magnetic effects from environmental influences--particularly for massive black holes posited to reside at galactic centers. We first compute the ppE frequency-domain waveform for a small black hole inspiraling into a massive Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) black hole, which corresponds to a Kerr black hole embedded in an external magnetic field. We find that the leading-order correction arising from the magnetic field is at the $-2$ post-Newtonian (PN) order relative to the quadrupole term, while the next-leading-order correction is at $-1.5$ PN, originating from the spin of the black hole. We further examine the effects of a spinning Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin (KBM) black hole, whose leading-order magnetic correction is at $-3$ PN (consistent with the preceding result), whereas its spin-induced correction is also at $-1.5$ PN. The leading-order ppE corrections for both KBR and KBM black holes do not appear degenerate with any modified theory of gravity effects; nonetheless, we demonstrate that they resemble the gravitational pull contributions from additional matter with power-law distributions of index $γ=1$ and $γ=0$, respectively. As a result, future gravitational wave (GW) observations detecting $-3$ or $-2$ PN order corrections will infer their origin as either magnetic field effects or matter environmental influences.

</details>


### [67] [Double-sphere enhanced optomechanical spectroscopy constrains symmetron dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05090)
*Jiawei Li,Ka-Di Zhu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper proposes an optomechanical experimental setup using two optically levitated nanospheres in a cavity to detect symmetron-mediated fifth forces. The induced effective coupling shifts the resonance spectrum, enabling constraints on symmetron parameters in the $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV range, improving current laboratory bounds by several orders of magnitude.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于腔内两个光学悬浮纳米球的光机实验方案，用于探测对称子（symmetron）介导的第五力。该对称子诱导的有效耦合会导致光机共振谱的可测分裂，从而在 $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV 参数区间内对对称子模型施加约束，比现有实验室限制提高数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Screened scalar field models like the symmetron offer theoretically consistent alternatives to explain dark energy while evading stringent solar system and laboratory tests via screening mechanisms. However, direct laboratory detection remains difficult due to the weakness and short-range nature of the resulting fifth forces. There is a need for high-precision, table-top experiments capable of probing these screened interactions in unexplored parameter regimes.
\n\n
对称子等屏蔽标量场模型通过屏蔽机制（screening mechanisms）在理论上自洽地解释暗能量，同时规避太阳系和实验室中的严格检验。然而，由于由此产生的第五力极其微弱且作用距离短，其直接实验室探测仍极具挑战。因此，亟需高精度的桌面实验来探测这些屏蔽相互作用在尚未探索的参数区域中的效应。

Method: The authors propose a cavity-based optomechanical setup with two optically levitated nanospheres. The symmetron field mediates a Yukawa-like interaction between the spheres, generating an effective position-dependent coupling. This coupling modifies the normal modes of the mechanical oscillators, leading to a resolvable splitting in the optomechanical resonance spectrum. By modeling this spectral shift and incorporating realistic experimental noise, they forecast sensitivity to symmetron parameters, particularly the mass scale $μ$.
\n\n
作者提出一种基于腔的光机系统，其中包含两个光学悬浮的纳米球。对称子场在两球之间介导类 Yukawa 相互作用，产生一个依赖于位置的有效耦合。该耦合会改变机械振子的正则模，导致光机共振谱中出现可分辨的分裂。通过建模该谱移并结合实际实验噪声，他们预测了对对称子参数（特别是质量尺度 $μ$）的灵敏度。

Result: The proposed scheme can probe symmetron couplings in the mass range $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV, surpassing current laboratory constraints by up to several orders of magnitude. The measurable resonance splitting provides a clear signature of the symmetron-mediated fifth force, demonstrating that optomechanical spectroscopy is a powerful tool for testing screened scalar fields.
\n\n
所提出的方案可在 $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV 质量范围内探测对称子耦合，比当前实验室限制提高多达数个数量级。可测量的共振分裂为对称子介导的第五力提供了清晰信号，表明光机光谱学是检验屏蔽标量场的有力工具。

Conclusion: Optomechanical systems with levitated nanoparticles offer a promising avenue for probing screened scalar fields such as the symmetron. The predicted sensitivity improvements highlight the potential of quantum-enhanced table-top experiments to explore fundamental physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly in the domain of dark energy and modified gravity.
\n\n
基于悬浮纳米粒子的光机系统为探测对称子等屏蔽标量场提供了一条有前景的路径。所预测的灵敏度提升凸显了量子增强型桌面实验在探索超越标准模型的基本物理（尤其是暗能量与修改引力领域）方面的潜力。

Abstract: Screened scalar fields such as the symmetron provide a viable description of dark energy yet their laboratory detection remains challenging. The symmetron-mediated interaction induces an effective coupling which leads to a measurable splitting in the optomechanical resonance spectrum. We forecast constraints in the regime $μ\sim 10^{-2}$eV-$10^{-4}$ eV, which shows that this approach can improve existing laboratory bounds by up to several orders of magnitude, demonstrating the sensitivity of optomechanical spectroscopy to screened fifth forces.

### [68] [New Improved Schwarzschild Black Hole and Its Thermodynamics and Topological Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05130)
*G. Alencar,T. M. Crispim,C. R. Muniz,M. Nilton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We construct a renormalization-group (RG) improved Schwarzschild black hole using the exact running of Newton's coupling, yielding a regular de Sitter core at short distances and recovering classical Schwarzschild at large distances. Quantum corrections induce a remnant and nontrivial thermodynamic phase structure, while topological classification shows preserved global topology with shifted critical points.
\n\n
我们利用牛顿耦合的精确跑动构建了一个重整化群（RG）改进的史瓦西黑洞，该解在短距离处呈现规则的类德西特核心，在长距离处恢复经典史瓦西解。量子修正导致残余态和非平凡的热力学相结构，而拓扑分类表明全局拓扑不变，但临界点发生偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classical Schwarzschild black hole contains a curvature singularity at its center, signaling a breakdown of general relativity. Asymptotic Safety in quantum gravity suggests that gravitational couplings run with energy scale, potentially resolving such singularities. This work aims to explore whether implementing the exact RG running of Newton's constant $G(k)$ via a proper-distance-based scale identification can yield a nonsingular black hole geometry consistent with both UV completeness and IR recovery of classical GR.
\n\n
经典史瓦西黑洞在其中心存在曲率奇点，表明广义相对论失效。量子引力中的渐近安全（Asymptotic Safety）假说指出引力耦合随能标跑动，可能消除此类奇点。本文旨在探究：通过基于固有距离的尺度识别方案实现牛顿常数 $G(k)$ 的精确重整化群跑动，是否能构造出一个无奇点的黑洞几何，同时满足紫外完备性并在红外恢复经典广义相对论。

Method: The authors employ the functional renormalization group (FRG) framework within the Asymptotic Safety scenario. They use the exact beta function for Newton's coupling $G(k)$ and implement a scale identification $k = k(r)$ via an interpolating proper-distance function $d(r)$, defined as $k(r) = \\xi / d(r)$ with $\\xi$ a dimensionless parameter. This yields a coordinate-dependent effective Newton constant $G(r) = G(k(r))$. The improved Schwarzschild metric takes the form $ds^2 = -f(r)dt^2 + f(r)^{-1}dr^2 + r^2 d\\Omega^2$, where $f(r) = 1 - 2G(r)M/r$. Thermodynamic quantities (temperature, entropy, heat capacity) are derived from this metric, and the phase space is analyzed using topological methods based on the Euler characteristic.
\n\n
作者采用渐近安全框架下的泛函重整化群（FRG）方法。他们使用牛顿耦合 $G(k)$ 的精确β函数，并通过一个插值型固有距离函数 $d(r)$ 实现尺度识别 $k = k(r)$，即 $k(r) = \\xi / d(r)$（其中 $\\xi$ 为无量纲参数）。由此得到坐标依赖的有效牛顿常数 $G(r) = G(k(r))$。改进的史瓦西度规形式为 $ds^2 = -f(r)dt^2 + f(r)^{-1}dr^2 + r^2 d\\Omega^2$，其中 $f(r) = 1 - 2G(r)M/r$。热力学量（温度、熵、热容）由此度规导出，并基于欧拉示性数对相空间进行拓扑分析。

Result: The RG-improved metric exhibits a regular de Sitter core as $r \\to 0$, with $f(r) \\approx 1 - (\\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}/3) r^2$, avoiding the central singularity. At large $r$, $f(r) \\to 1 - 2GM/r$, recovering classical Schwarzschild. Thermodynamically, the Hawking temperature vanishes at a finite radius $r_0 > 0$, indicating a stable remnant. The heat capacity changes sign, revealing a phase transition. Topological analysis of the thermodynamic curvature shows that while the critical point shifts due to asymptotically safe effects, the global topological charge (Euler number) remains identical to that of the classical Schwarzschild black hole.
\n\n
RG改进的度规在 $r \\to 0$ 时呈现规则的类德西特核心，$f(r) \\approx 1 - (\\Lambda_{\\text{UV}}/3) r^2$，避免了中心奇点；在大 $r$ 极限下，$f(r) \\to 1 - 2GM/r$，恢复经典史瓦西解。热力学上，霍金温度在有限半径 $r_0 > 0$ 处趋于零，表明存在稳定残余态；热容变号，揭示相变。热力学曲率的拓扑分析表明，尽管渐近安全效应使临界点偏移，但全局拓扑荷（欧拉数）与经典史瓦西黑洞相同。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that incorporating the exact RG running of Newton's coupling within a proper-distance scale setting yields a nonsingular black hole solution that smoothly interpolates between UV de Sitter and IR Schwarzschild regimes. The resulting geometry resolves the central singularity while preserving key classical features at large scales. Moreover, quantum gravitational effects introduce novel thermodynamic behavior—including remnants and phase transitions—without altering the global topological structure of the black hole phase space, supporting the consistency of Asymptotic Safety as a UV completion of gravity.
\n\n
本工作表明，在基于固有距离的尺度设定下引入牛顿耦合的精确重整化群跑动，可得到一个无奇点黑洞解，该解在紫外区为类德西特、红外区为史瓦西，平滑过渡。所得几何消除了中心奇点，同时在大尺度保留关键经典特征。此外，量子引力效应引入了新奇的热力学行为（包括残余态和相变），却不改变黑洞相空间的全局拓扑结构，支持渐近安全作为引力紫外完备方案的一致性。

Abstract: We construct a renormalization-group improved Schwarzschild-like black hole geometry using the exact new scheme running for the Newton coupling. The scale identification is implemented via a standard interpolating proper-distance function that smoothly connects the ultraviolet and infrared regimes. We present the resulting coordinate-dependent coupling and the improved metric function, analyzing its asymptotic expansions. The large-distance limit is shown to recover the classical Schwarzschild solution, while the short-distance behavior exhibits a regular de Sitter-like core, demonstrating the regularization of the central singularity. We also analyze the thermodynamic properties of the solution, showing that quantum corrections significantly modify the small-radius behavior, leading to a remnant configuration and a nontrivial phase structure. Finally, we perform a topological classification of the thermodynamic phase space and demonstrate that asymptotically safe effects shift the critical point while preserving the global topological number of the Schwarzschild solution.

### [69] [Accretion Disk Perturbations and Their Effects on Kerr Black Hole Superradiance and Gravitational Atom Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05182)
*Ruiheng Li,Zhong-hao Luo,Zehong Wang,Fa Peng Huang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Kerr black hole superradiance can be significantly altered by accretion disk gravity, which acts as a weak external perturbation inducing energy shifts and state mixing in the $n=2$ bosonic cloud. Using a multipole expansion, the authors derive an effective three-level Hamiltonian for the $\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$ subspace. Disk-induced quadrupolar tidal fields produce distinct selection rules based on symmetry: axisymmetry causes only diagonal energy shifts; equatorial nonaxisymmetry enables $Δm = \pm2$ transitions; breaking equatorial reflection symmetry allows $Δm = \pm1$ couplings. Transient spiral waves can quench superradiance by exciting decaying modes, while static warps induce narrow "growth gaps" or enhancements near degeneracies. This shows that realistic disk environments critically affect boson cloud evolution and ultralight boson detectability.
\n\n
Kerr黑洞的超辐射可因吸积盘引力而显著改变，该引力作为微扰引起$n=2$玻色子云的能级移动和态混合。作者通过多极展开推导出$\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$子空间的有效三能级哈密顿量。吸积盘诱导的四极（$\ell_d=2$）潮汐场根据对称性产生特定选择定则：轴对称性仅导致对角能量移动；赤道面非轴对称性激活$Δm = \pm2$跃迁；破坏赤道反射对称性则允许$Δm = \pm1$耦合。瞬态$m=2$螺旋波可通过激发衰减模式抑制或熄灭超辐射，而准静态翘曲在近简并点附近产生窄“增长间隙”或增强效应。这表明真实吸积盘环境对玻色子云演化及ultralight boson的可探测性具有决定性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard treatment of BH superradiance assumes an isolated Kerr BH, but real astrophysical BHs are often surrounded by accretion disks whose gravitational field can perturb the boson cloud. Ignoring this environmental effect may lead to inaccurate predictions for superradiant growth rates and gravitational-wave signatures. The paper aims to systematically incorporate disk gravity as a weak external potential to understand how it modifies level structure, mode coupling, and ultimately the dynamics of boson cloud evolution.
\n\n
标准黑洞超辐射理论通常假设孤立的Kerr黑洞，但真实天体物理黑洞常被吸积盘包围，其引力场会扰动玻色子云。忽略这一环境效应可能导致对超辐射增长率和引力波信号的预测不准确。本文旨在将吸积盘引力系统地纳入为弱外势，以理解其如何改变能级结构、模式耦合，并最终影响玻色子云的动力学演化。

Method: The authors model the accretion disk’s gravitational potential as a weak external perturbation expanded in spherical harmonics (multipole expansion). They focus on the $n=2$ hydrogen-like bound states of the massive boson field around a Kerr BH, specifically the degenerate subspace $\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$. Using time-independent perturbation theory in the weak-coupling regime, they construct an effective 3×3 Hamiltonian. Symmetry considerations—axisymmetry, equatorial reflection symmetry, and their breaking—dictate the allowed matrix elements via selection rules ($Δm = 0, \pm1, \pm2$). Two illustrative disk models are analyzed: (i) a transient equatorial $m=2$ spiral density wave, treated as a time-dependent perturbation driving a two-level subsystem; and (ii) a quasi-static warp (breaking equatorial symmetry), leading to full three-level mixing and avoided crossings near degeneracies.
\n\n
作者将吸积盘引力势建模为弱外扰动，并用球谐函数展开（多极展开）。他们聚焦于Kerr黑洞周围大质量玻色子场的类氢束缚态中$n=2$能级，特别是简并子空间$\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$。在弱耦合极限下，利用定态微扰理论构建了一个有效的3×3哈密顿量。对称性考量——轴对称性、赤道反射对称性及其破缺——通过选择定则（$Δm = 0, \pm1, \pm2$）决定了允许的矩阵元。文中分析了两种典型吸积盘模型：(i) 瞬态赤道面$m=2$螺旋密度波，作为含时微扰驱动一个二能级子系统；(ii) 准静态翘曲（破坏赤道对称性），导致完整的三能级混合，并在近简并点附近产生避免交叉。

Result: The leading-order disk perturbation is quadrupolar ($\ell_d=2$). Under axisymmetry, it induces only diagonal energy shifts proportional to $m^2$, preserving mode decoupling. When equatorial nonaxisymmetry is present (e.g., $m_d = \pm2$ component), it couples $\ket{211}$ and $\ket{21-1}$ via $Δm = \pm2$, forming a driven two-level system that can suppress superradiance if the decaying mode is populated. Breaking equatorial reflection symmetry introduces off-diagonal couplings to $\ket{210}$ through $Δm = \pm1$, resulting in full three-level mixing. In the quasi-static limit, this produces narrow “growth gaps” in the superradiant instability band near accidental near-degeneracies, where destructive interference cancels growth; conversely, constructive reshuffling can enhance growth when spectral weight shifts toward the unstable mode. These effects demonstrate that disk geometry and time dependence critically modulate superradiant dynamics.
\n\n
主导阶吸积盘微扰为四极项（$\ell_d=2$）。在轴对称条件下，它仅引起与$m^2$成正比的对角能量移动，保持模式解耦。当存在赤道面非轴对称性（如$m_d = \pm2$分量）时，通过$Δm = \pm2$耦合$\ket{211}$与$\ket{21-1}$，形成受驱二能级系统，若衰减模式被占据，则可抑制超辐射。破坏赤道反射对称性则通过$Δm = \pm1$引入与$\ket{210}$的非对角耦合，导致完整的三能级混合。在准静态极限下，这会在超辐射不稳定带内近简并点附近产生窄“增长间隙”，其中相消干涉抵消增长；反之，当谱权重向不稳定模式偏移时，相长重排可增强增长。这些结果表明，吸积盘几何结构和时间依赖性对超辐射动力学具有关键调制作用。

Conclusion: Accretion disk gravity is not a negligible perturbation but a decisive environmental factor that reshapes the energy landscape and coupling structure of boson clouds around spinning BHs. Depending on the disk’s symmetry properties and time evolution, it can suppress, quench, or even enhance superradiant instabilities. Consequently, accurate predictions for gravitational-wave signals from boson clouds—and thus constraints on ultralight boson masses—must account for realistic disk environments. This work provides a foundational framework for incorporating such astrophysical complexity into future superradiance studies and observational strategies.
\n\n
吸积盘引力并非可忽略的微扰，而是重塑旋转黑洞周围玻色子云能级结构和耦合关系的关键环境因素。根据吸积盘的对称性和时间演化特性，它可抑制、熄灭甚至增强超辐射不稳定性。因此，对玻色子云引力波信号的精确预测（以及由此对ultralight boson质量的限制）必须考虑真实吸积盘环境。本工作为将此类天体物理复杂性纳入未来超辐射研究和观测策略提供了理论基础框架。

Abstract: Kerr black hole (BH) superradiance can form gravitational atoms and produce characteristic gravitational-wave signals, providing a probe of ultralight bosons and dark matter. In realistic systems, accretion-disk gravity can shift energy levels and mix states, modifying the effective superradiant growth. We model the disk as a weak external perturbation via a multipole expansion and derive an effective three-level Hamiltonian for the $n=2$ subspace $\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$ in the weak-coupling regime. The leading disk effect is the quadrupolar ($\ell_d=2$) tidal field, whose symmetries fix the selection rules: axisymmetry gives only diagonal shifts, equatorial nonaxisymmetry activates $Δm=\pm2$ mixing ($\ket{211}\leftrightarrow\ket{21-1}$), and breaking equatorial reflection opens $Δm=\pm1$ couplings involving $\ket{210}$. As illustrations, a transient equatorial $m=2$ spiral wave drives the resulting two-level system and can suppress or quench superradiance by populating a decaying mode, while a quasi-static warp produces full three-level mixing and can generate narrow ``growth gaps'' near accidental near-degeneracies, with the same static reshuffling also allowing enhancement when weight shifts toward the growing mode. These findings demonstrate that accretion disk perturbations are a crucial environmental factor in determining the dynamics of BH superradiance and the evolution of boson clouds, thereby providing a more reliable theoretical basis for assessing the detectability of ultralight bosons in realistic astrophysical settings.

### [70] [Can Light Cross a Singularity? Exact Solutions from Analogue Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05285)
*Juan Manuel Paez,Franco Fiorini,Santiago M. Hernández*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates electromagnetic fields in a spacetime with a strong curvature naked singularity using an analogue gravity model, finding exact regular solutions to Maxwell's equations and demonstrating that electromagnetic energy can carry a bounded power flux through the singularity.
\n\n
该论文利用类比引力模型研究了具有强曲率裸奇点的时空中的电磁场，找到了麦克斯韦方程组的精确正则解，并证明电磁能量可通过该奇点传递有限的功率流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the unresolved physical behavior of classical fields near naked singularities—spacetime regions where curvature diverges but are not hidden behind event horizons. Understanding whether field propagation remains well-defined or carries energy across such singularities tests the limits of general relativity and potential extensions via analogue models.
\n\n
动机源于对裸奇点附近经典场物理行为尚未解决的问题——裸奇点是曲率发散但未被事件视界遮蔽的时空区域。理解场传播在这些奇点附近是否仍良好定义、或能否携带能量穿越奇点，是对广义相对论及其通过类比模型可能扩展的极限检验。

Method: The authors construct an analogue gravity setup mimicking a spacetime with a strong curvature naked singularity. Within this framework, they solve the full set of Maxwell’s equations (both electrostatic and electrodynamic regimes) analytically, imposing regularity conditions at the singularity to identify physically admissible solutions.
\n\n
作者构建了一个类比引力模型，模拟具有强曲率裸奇点的时空。在此框架内，他们解析求解完整的麦克斯韦方程组（包括静电和电动力学情形），并在奇点处施加正则性条件以筛选出物理上可接受的解。

Result: Exact, regular solutions to Maxwell’s equations are obtained that remain finite at the naked singularity. Notably, some of these solutions exhibit a finite and bounded electromagnetic power flux across the singularity, implying that information or energy may traverse it without divergence.
\n\n
获得了在裸奇点处保持有限的麦克斯韦方程组的精确正则解。值得注意的是，其中某些解在穿越奇点时表现出有限且有界的电磁功率流，表明信息或能量可在无发散的情况下穿越该奇点。

Conclusion: The results challenge the conventional view that naked singularities necessarily disrupt physical field evolution, suggesting instead that under appropriate boundary conditions, classical electromagnetic fields can propagate through them coherently. This supports the utility of analogue gravity models in probing strong-gravity phenomena beyond standard black hole paradigms.
\n\n
结果挑战了“裸奇点必然破坏物理场演化”的传统观点，表明在适当的边界条件下，经典电磁场可相干地穿越裸奇点。这支持了类比引力模型在探索超越标准黑洞范式的强引力现象中的有效性。

Abstract: Using a simple spacetime hosting a strong curvature naked singularity, we employ an analogue gravity model to study electromagnetic fields in this background. We find exact solutions to the full set of electrostatic and electrodynamic equations that remain regular even in the presence of the singularity. Moreover, certain solutions sustain a regular and bounded power flux across the singularity, suggesting that electromagnetic energy may be transmitted through it.

</details>
